Ka jingieit ka dei ka shap jong U Blei ba ka dei hi ka hukum jong U Blei bad ka dei hi ka jinglong jong U Blei. Ka long ka jingiaroh kaba halor tam ban iakren bad ban leh ia ka. Hynrei haduh katno ngin lah shisha ban im bad ban leh ia ka, lym da U Blei hi da lade u jied da ka bor jong u ban ai ka jinglah ha ngi iwei pa iwei. Ka long kaba jem ban ieit bad isynei ia kiwei kumba ju leh da ki sengbhalang, ki politishan bad kiwei pat ki kynhun ne riew shimet kiba ju leh ieit bad leh isynei sha ki riew rangli da ki bam ki dihj, ki jain ki nep kiba ki la ioh pdiang na kiwei pat ki riew heh spah ne ki company bapher bapher kiba kyshan ia ki. Hynrei kam long kaba suk ban knia shisha da lade ban leh bha ia kiwei na kaei kaba dei ka jong ngi hi. Katei ka mat jong ka jingieit ri bad ka jingieit rangli ka mih halor ka jingkylli jong uwei u rangbah kumne kine ki nongdie madan ki la ioh biang ban buhai basa harud surok haduh ba la pynsatah hi khait. Kawei ka jingkynthoh kaba khlain bha ba u la ai ka long  hato kine ki khar kiw khar kaw kiba tuid na ki heh paid ka ri India ruh ki dei ki rangli u Hynniewtrep seh mo? Ka long kaba sngewtynnad ban don ia ki sengbhalang, ki seng niam ne ki riew shimet kiba trei na ka bynta ban peit ia ka bha ka miat jong ki duk ki rangbali ban kyntiew ia ka bha ka miat jong ki. Hynrei ka long ruh kaba donkam pat ban peit ha baroh arliang jong ka tyngka pliah kata ia ka dor jong ka bad ka dur jong ka. Lada kum ki sengbhalang ki ieng ban kyrshan ia ki nongdie madan ka long ruh kaba donkam ban iatreilang bad ki ban pynsngewthuh sha ki ba kato ka rukom trei ne ka bynta jong ka jingim kam dei kaba kut, hynrei haba la biang ka sngi ka por ki la dei ban thaw noh da kiwei pat kilad ki lynti khnang ba ym tang ki briew kiba bha ban miat hynrei ka shnong ka thaw ruh kan long kumta lang. Kum ki sengbhalang donkam ruh ban don ia ka mynsiem ba ieng ia da ia ka mariang ban pynneh pynsah ia ki jingiatynnad bad jingdonburom jong ka. Haba ïakren bad Nongai khubor lyngba ka phone, kane ka Samla ba wat hashuwa ban leit mudui sha u Myntri, kala dep ruh ban mudui ïa ka sha ki Heh Ophisar jong ka kynthup u Under Secretary hynrei ym shym la don ba sangap satia. Khlem kano kano ka daw, u Director u la phah pynsangeh ïa ka tulop jong nga mynta la hynriew bnai bad mynta u la pynkyn riah ïa nga sha kawei pat ka District. Nga la leit sha Byrnihat bad buh ïa ka shithi sdang treikam (Joining Letter) jong nga ong kane ka samla. Haba kylli, kane ka samla kala ïathuh ba hadien ka jingkyntait ïa ka hukum u Director( Ban sahmiet bad u), u la khang shisyndon ïa ka ban rung ha ka Ïingsah jong u bad la shu pynïeng ïa ka shabar Ïing naduh ka por ba ka wan mynstep haduh ka por ba wai trei. U (Director) ong ïa nga ba nga hap ban sah bad u naba ka dei ka kamram jong ka kat kum ka Rule. Nga la pyrshang ban wad ïa ka jingshisha la ka long don shisha ne em kata ka Rule hapoh Secretariat hynrei ngam shym la lap satia kala ong. Kat kum ka jingong jong ka, ha ka khyllipmat ba ka rungkam, la ïalam beit beit ïa ka sha ka Ïingsah u Director bad la phah sait ïa ki tiar ki tar bad phah nïad istiri ïa ki jaiñ ki nep jong u nalor ba ym shym la buh ruh ïa ka por trei ne por leit ïing. Ka ong ba ym ju don shuti ruh lait noh tang ka Sngi U Blei. Na ka liang u Nongthoh khubor u la pyrshang ruh ban ioh iakren ia u Director Bah D Langstieh hynrei ym shym la ioh satia. Ha kaba mynnyngkong U Blei u la thaw ia ka bneng bad ia ka khyndew. Bad ka pyrthei ka la long bakhlem dur bad kaba suda, bad ka jingdum ka la long halor ka khmat ka jingjylliew, bad U Mynsiem U Blei u da khih halor ki um. Bad U Blei u la ong, To long ka jingshai, bad ka jingshai ka la long. Bad U Blei u la iohi ia kata ka jingshai, ba ka la long kaba bha; bad U Blei u la pyniakhlad ia kata ka jingshai na kata ka jingdum. Te U Blei u la khot Ka Sngi ia kata ka jingshai, bad ia kata ka jingdum u la khot Ka Miet. Bad kaba lajan miet ka la long bad ka step ruh ka la long, kawei ka sngi. Te U Blei u la ong. To long ka suiñ bneng hapdeng kita ki um, bad to ai ba kan pynkhlad ia ki um na ki um. Bad U Blei u la pynlong ia ka suiñ bneng, bad u la pynkhlad ia kita ki um kiba hapoh kata ka suin bneng na kita ki um kiba halor kata ka suiñ bneng; te ka long kumta keiñ. Bad ia kata ka suiñ bneng, U Blei u la khot Ka Bneng. Bad kaba lajan miet ka la long, bad ka step ka la long, ka sngi kaba ar. U Blei u la ong ruh, To long ba 
kin ia lang sha kawei ka jaka kita ki um kiba hapoh ka bneng, bad to ai kan paw ka ryngkew: te ka la long kumta keifi. Te ia kata ka ryngkew, U Blei u la khot Ka Khyndew, bad ia kata ka jingialang ki um u la khot Ki Duriaw; bad U Blei u la iohi ba ka la long kaba bha. ''U Blei u la ong ruh, To long ba ka khyndew kan pynmih speh, ba ki jhur kin pynsei symbai, bad ba ki diengsch kin seisoh ha la ka jaid ka jaid, kiba don la u symbai hapoh jong ki, halor ka khyndew. Te ka la long kumta keiñ. Kumta te ka khyndew ka la pynmih speh, bad ki jhur ruh ki la pynmih symbai ha la ka jaid ka jaid, bad ki dieng soh kiba pynseisoh ha la ka jaid ka jaid, kiba don la u symbai hapoh jong ki; te U Blei u la iohi ba ka la long kaba bha. Te kaba lajan miet ka la long, bad ka tep ka la long, kaba lai ka sngi. U Blei u la ong ruh. To long ki jingshai ha ka sahit bneng ban pyniakhlad hapdeng ka sngi bad ka miet; bad to ai ba kin long ia ki dak, bad ia ki aiom, bad ia ki sngi, bad ia ki snem de: bad to ai ba kin long ki jingshai ha kata ka sahit ki bneng ia kaban pynshai ha ka pyrthei: te ka la long kumta ruh. Bad U Blei u la pynlong ia ki artylli ki jingshai kiba khraw; ia kata kaba kham khraw ia kaban synshar ia kaba mynsngi, bad ia kata kaba kham rit ia kaban iynshar ia kaba mynmiet: bad u la thaw ia ki khlur ruh. Bad U Blei u la buh ia ki ha kata ka sahit bneng ia kaban pynshai ha ka pyrthei, bad ia kaban synshar ia kaba mynsngi bad ia kaba mynmiet, bad ia kaban pynkhlad ia ka jingshai na ka jingdum: te U Blei u la iohi ba ka long kaba bha. Bad kaba la janmiet ka la long, bad ka step ruh ka la long, ha ka sngi kaba saw. Bad U Blei u la ong ruh, To ai ba ki um kin ia boi da kiei kiei ki kynja baim bapar, bad to ai ba kiei kiei ki kynja baher kin iaher ha khmat ka sahit bneng. Te U Blei u la thaw ia kita ki dohkha khraw kiba heh, bad ia ki kynja baim bapar baroh, da kiba kita ki um ki la iaboi, ha la ka jaid ka jaid, bad ia kiei kiei ki kynja baher ruh de ha la ka jaid ka jaid: te U Blei u la iohi ba ka la long kaba bha. Bad U Blei u la kyrkhu ia ki, u da ong, To da nangkha, bad to da nangroi, bad to da pyndap ruh ia 
kita ki um ha ki duriaw, bad to ai ba kiei kiei ruh ki kynja baher kin ianangroi ha ka khyndew. Te kaba lajan miet ka la long, bad ka step ruh ka la long, ha ka sngi kaba san. U Blei u la ong ruh. To ai ba ka khyndew kan pynmih noh ia kiei kiei ruh ki kynja bairn baroh ha la ka jaid ka jaid, ia ki jingri, bad ia kiei kiei ruh ki kynja bapar, bad ia u mrad khlaw jong ka ryngkew ha la ka jaid ka jaid: te ka la long kumta kein. Kumta U Blei u la thaw ia u mrad ka ryngkew ha la ka jaid ka jaid, bad ia ki jingri ha la ka jaid ka jaid, bad ia kiei kiei ruh ki kynja bapar baroh ha ka khyndew ha la ka jaid ka jaid: te U Blei u la iohi ba ka la long kaba bha. U Blei u la ong ruh. To pgin iathaw ia u briew ha ka dur jong ngi, katba kum ka jingsyriem jong ngi hi ; bad kin synshar halor ki dohkha ka duriaw, bad halor ki sim bneng, bad halor ki kynja mrad, bad halor ka pyrthei baroh, bad halor 
kiei kiei ki kynja bapar baroh kiba par halor ka khyndew. Kumta U Blei u la thaw ia u briew ha ka dur jong u hi, ha ka dur U Blei kein u la thaw ia u; shynrang bad kynthei u la thaw ia ki. U Blei u la kyrkhu ruh ia ki, bad U Blei u la ong ha ki. To da nangkha, bad to da nangroi, bad to da pyndap ia ka khyndew, bad to da pyndem ngon ia ka: bad to synshar halor ki dohkha ka duriaw, bad halor ki sim bneng, bad halor kiei kiei ki kynja baim baroh ba par halor ka khyndew. U Blei u la ong ruh. Ha khmih, nga la ai ha phi, ban long ka jingbam, ia u jhur baroh uba pynmih symbai, uba don halor ka khmat ka khyndew baroh, bad ia u dieng baroh, uba don ha lade u soh jong u dieng uba pynmih symbai. Bad ha u kynja mrad baroh jong ka khyndew, bad ha ki kynja baher baroh jong ka suin bneng, bad ha ki kynja bapar baroh halor ka khyndew, ba don ka jingim ha ki, nga la ai ia u jhur bajyrngam baroh ban long jingbam: bad ka la long kumta ruh. Hadien kata U lei u la iohi ia kiei kiei baroh ba u la lah thaw, ha khmih ruh, ka la bha eh. Te kaba lajan miet ka la 
long, bad kaba mynstep ruh ka la long, ha ka sngi kaba hynriew. Kumta la pyndep noh ia ki bneng bad ia ka pyrthei, bad ia ki kynhun bah baroh jong ki. Te ha kaba hynriiew ka sngi, U Blei la pyndep noh ia la ka kam ia kaba u la lah pynlong; bad ha kaba hynniew ka sngi u la shong sngi na ka kam jong u baroh ia kaba u la lah pynlong. Bad U Blei u la kyrkhu ia kata kaba hynniew ka sngi, bad u la kyntang khuid ia ka: naba ha kane ka sngi u la shong sngi na ka kam jong u baroh ia kaba U Blei u la lah pynlong bad thaw. Kane ka long ka jingiathuhkhana shaphang ki bneng bad ka pyrthei, mynba la pynlong ia ki ha kata ka sngi ba U Trai uba U Blei u la thaw ia ka pyrthei bad ia ki bneng, bad ia ki jingthung baroh jong ka lyngkha mynba kim pat 
la long ha ka khyndew, bad ia u jhur baroh jong ka lyngkha mynba um pat la mih speh: naba U Trai uba U Blei um pat shym la pynhiar ia u slap halor ka khyndew, bad haba u briew ruh um pat la don ia kaban rep ia ka khyndew. Te u lyoh u la mih na ka khyndew, bad u la ai um halor ka khmat ka khyndew baroh. Bad U Trai uba U Blei u la thaw ia u briew na ka dewmet ka khyndew, bad u la pyrsad ha ki thliew khmut jong u ia ka jingpyrsad ka jingim; bad uta u briew u la long ka mynsiem bairn. Ka kper Eden U Trai uba U Blei ruh u la thung ia ka kper ha Ka Eden shaphang mihngi; bad u la buh hangta ia uta u briew ia uba u la lah thaw. Bad U Trai uba U Blei u la pynlong ba kin mih na kata ka khyndew ki dieng baroh kiba itynnad ban khmih, bad kiba bit eh ia kaban bam; bad hapdeng kata ka kper ia u dieng ka jingim, bad ia u dieng ka jingtip ia kaba 
bha bad ia kaba sniew. Ka wah ruh ka la mih noh na Eden ia kaban ai um ia kata ka kper; bad nangta ka la khlad, bad ka la long saw tnat. Ka kyrteng jong kaba nyng- kong ka long Ka Pison: kata kaba tuid sawdong ia ka ri Habilah baroh kawei, ha kaba don ka ksiar; bad ka ksiar jong kata ka ri ka long kaba bha: hangta ruh don u bdellium bad u mawlynnai onyks.  Bad ka kyrteng ka wah kaba ar ka long Ka Gihon: kata kaba tuid sawdong ia ka ri Kush baroh kawei. Bad ka kyrteng ka wah kaba lai ka long Ka Hidekel: kata kaba tuid shaphang mihngi ia ka ri Assyria. Bad ka wah kaba saw ka long Ka luphratis. Bad U Trai uba U Blei u la shim ia uta u briew, bad u la buh ia u ha ka kper Eden ia kaban trei bad ban sumar ia ka. Bad U Trai uba U Blei u la hukum ia uta u briew, u da ong, Na u dieng baroh ha ka kper, da kaba bam me iah ban bam ei: 'hynrei na u dieng ka jingtip ia kaba bha bad ia kaba sniew men ym ioh bam na u: naba ha kata ka sngi ba men bam na u, da kaba iap men iap shisha. Bad U Trai uba U Blei u la ong ruh, Ym bit ba uta u briew un sah marwei ; ngan thaw ia u ka nongsumar lem kaba biang. Bad U Trai uba U Blei u la pynlong na ka khyndew ia ki mrad ka ryngkew baroh, bad ia ki sim bneng baroh; bad u la wallam ia ki ha U Adam ban khmih kumno un buh kyrteng ia ki : bad kat kumba uta u briew u la buh kyrteng ia kita ki kynja baim baroh, kumta hi ka la long ka kyrteng jong ki. 20Bad U Adam u la buh kyrteng ha ki kynja jingri baroh, bad ha ki sim bneng, bad ha ki mrad baroh jong ka khyndew; hynrei ia U Adam ym pat shym la shem ia ka nongsumar lem. Te U Trai uba U Blei u la pynngat ha U Adam da ka jingsamthiah kaba jur, u ruh u la iohthiah : bad u la shim ia kawei na ki shyiengkrung jong u, bad u la set pat da ka doh ha ka jaka jong ka; He U Trai uba U Blei u la pynlong ka briew, na kata ka shyieng krung ia kaba u la lah shim na uta u briew, bad u la wallam ia ka ha uta u briew. Bad U Adam u la ong, Kane mynta shisha ka 
long ka shyieng na ki shyieng jong nga, bad ka doh na ka doh jong nga: ia kane kein yn khot Ka Briew, namarba la shim ia ka na U Briew. Namarkata keñ u briew un iehnoh ia la u kjm bad ia la ka kmie, bad un iaineh bad la ka tnga: bad kin ialong ruh kawei ka doh. Te ki la long kiba lyngkhuid baroh arngut, uta u briew bad ka tnga jong u, bad kim shym la sngewlehrain. Ka jinghap jong u briew Te uta u bsein u la long uba kham sian ia ki mrad baroh ka ryngkew ia kiba U Trai uba U Blei u la lah thaw. Bad u la ong ha kata ka briew, Shisha, ka long kumta, ba U Blei u la ong, Phin ym ioh bam na u dieng baroh ha ka kper? Bad kata ka briew ka la ong ha uta u bsein, Na u soh ki dieng ha ka kper ngi ioh ban bam: hynrei na u soh jong uta u dieng uba hapdeng ka kper, U Blei u la ong, Phin ym ioh bam na u, lymne ktah ia u, ba ioh phin iap noh. Te uta u bseñ u la ong ha kata ka briew, Phin ym iap noh shisha: Namar U Blei u tip ba, ha kata ka sngi ba phin bam na u, un sa pynpeit ia ki khmat jong phi, bad ba phin long kum ki blei, kiba tip ia kaba bha bad ia kaba sniew. Te haba kata ka briew ka la iohi ba uta u dieng u la long uba bha ban bam, bad uba itynnad ia ki khmat, bad u dieng uba bit ia kaban pynstad, ka la shim na u soh jong u, bad ka la bam ruh, bad ka la ai lem ruh de ha la u tnga; u ruh u la bam. Hadien kata la pynpeit ia ki khmat jong ki baroh arngut, bad ki la tip ba ki la long kiba lyngkhuid; bad ki la iasuh lang ia ki sla u dieng dumbur, bad ki la iathaw ia lade ia ki jingpanpoh. Te ki la iohsngew ia ka jingsawa U Trai uba U Blei ba u da wan iaid ha ka kper ha ka jingpyngngad ka sngi: te U Adam bad ka tnga jong u ki la iabuhrieh ia lade na khmat U Trai uba U Blei hapdeng ki dieng jong kata ka kper. Te U Trai uba U Blei u la khot ia U Adam, bad u da ong ha u, Me don shaei? U te u la ong, Nga la iohsngew ia ka jingsawa jong me ha ka kper, nga te nga la sheptieng, naba nga la lyngkhuid; bad nga la buhrieh ia lade. Bad U Blei u la ong, Uei ba la iathuh ha me ba me la 
lyngkhuid? Shisha me la bam na uta u dieng ia uba nga la adong ia me ban ym bam na u? Te U Adam u la iathuh, Kata ka briew ia kaba me la buh lok bad nga, ka long ma ka keñ kaba la ai 
ha nga na uta u dieng, bad nga la kum bam. Te U Trai uba U Blei u la ong ha kata ka briew, Kaei kane ia kaba pha la leh? Te kata ka briew ka la iathuh, Uta u bseñ u la shukor ia nga, nga ruh nga la kum bam. Hadien kata U Trai U Blei u la ong ha uta u bsein, Namarba me la leh ia kane, la tim ia me nalor ki kynja jingri baroh, bad nalor ki kynja mrad ka ryngkew baroh; da ka kpoh jong me men par, bad ia ka dewmet men bam baroh ki sngi ka rta jong me. Bad ia ka ingshun ruh ngan buh hapdeng jong me bad kata ka briew, bad hapdeng u symbai jong me bad u symbai jong ka; u symbai jong ka un pynlwet ia ka khlieh jong me bad me men pynlwet ia ka khongdongjat jong u. Bad ha kata ka briew u la ong. Da kaba pynroi ngan pynroi ia ki jingpang jong pha, bad ia ka jingseng khun jong pha; ha ka jingshitom phan kha ki khun; bad ka jingkwah jong pha kan long sha u tnga jong pha, bad u un synshar halor jong pha. Bad ha U Adam u la ong, Namarba me la shahshkor ia ka ktien ka tnga jong me, bad ba me la bam na uta u dieng, ia uba nga la adong ia me, da kaba ong, Men ym bam na u : ia ka khyndew la tim na ka bynta jong me; da ka jingshitom men bam na ka baroh ki sngi ka rta jong me; kan pynmih shylluit ruh ia ki shiah bad ia ki shiah keng ia me; bad men bam ia u jhur ka lyngkha. Da ka jingsyep ka khmat jong me men bam ia la u kpu, haduh ban da men phaidien pat sha ka khyndew ; namar na' ka la shim ia me: naba ka dewmet me long, bad sha ka dewmet men leit phai pat. Te U Adam u la khot kyrteng ia la ka tnga, Ka Im; naba la long ma ka ka kmie jong kiba im baroh. Ua U Adam ruh bad ia ka tnga jong u U Trai uba U Blei u la thaw ia ki jingkup snieh, bad u la pynkup ruh ia ki. U Trai uba U Blei u la ong ruh. Ha khmih, uta u briew u la wan long kum uwei na ngi hi, kat ban tip ia kaba bha bad ia kaba sniew: te mynta, ba ioh un kner ia la ka kti, bad shim ruh na u dieng ka jingim, bad bam, bad im junom ruh de: namarkata U Trai uba U Blei u la beh noh ia u na ka kper Eden, ia kaban rep ia ka khyndew na kaba la shim ia u. Kumta keñ u la beh noh ia uta u briew; bad u la buh ia ki kherub shaphang mihngi ka kper Eden, bad ia kaba kum ka waitlam baphyrnai, kaba da khih talañ baroh sawdong, ia kaban sumar ia ka lynti sha uta u dieng ka jingim. Shillong, Ïaiong 12 : Ka Central Puja Committee, ka Hynñiewtrep Youth Council bad ruh ka Hill State People’s Democratic Party (HSPDP) ki la pynpaw ïa ka jingbym sngewïahap halor ka jing-pynbna jong ka sorkar pdeng ban pynlong ïa ka jingrakhe Digital India Day ha ka 14tarik, kaba dei ka Good Friday ne ka sngi ba ki Khristan ki rakhe kyrpang da kaba dawa ba ka sorkar India kadei ban weng noh mardor ïa ka jingrakhe ba ki buh ha katei ka sngi khuid.

    Na ka liang ka CPC ha ka jingïalang ba kyrkieh hynne ka sngi ha Keating Road hapoh ka jingïalam jong u president, Naba Bhatta-charjee ka la shim ïa ka rai ban kyrpad ïa ka sorkar India ban weng noh ïa katei ka sngi Digital India Day ba ki buh ha ka sngi Good Friday kum ka dak ka jingburom ïa ki Khristan.

    Ka kyrwoh na u president, ka ong ruh ba ka phah ka kyrwoh sha baroh ki paid khristan ha ka jingrakhe ïa ka sngi Thohdieng Bakhuid kaba dei ka sngi shahïap jong u Jisu Krist halor ka Diengphna ban pyllait im ïa u bynriew na ka pop.

    Na ka liang ka Hynñiewtrep Youth Council (HYC) ka la ong, “Ka rai jong ka Sorkar NDA hapoh ka jingïalam jong ka BJP ban pynlong ïa ka sngi 14tarik mynta u bnai kaba dei ka sngi Sngi Thohdieng Bakhuid (Good Friday) kum ka sngi ban rakhe ïa ka Digital India Day ka long kaei kaei kaba pynsngewsih ïa ki paidbah Kristan hapoh ka Bri U Hynniewtrep. Kane kadei ka kam ban beiñ ne lehbeiñ ïa ki Khristan bad ka kam kaba pynkheiñ noh ïa ka jingïoh mane laitluid (Secular) jong ka Ri India. ,” ong ka kyrwoh.

    Ka Seng lyngba u General Secretary, Bah Robertjune Kharjahrin ka la pynpaw ruh ïa ka jingbym sngewïahap ïa ka jingthmu jong ka sorkar pdeng ban pynlong ïa ka Good Governance Day ha ka Kristmas, lada ka don ka jingburom lang ïa baroh ki jait niam.

    Ka HYC ka kyrpad ïa baroh ki sengsaiñ pyrthei kiba don jingïadei kaba jan bad ka BJP ba ki dei ban buh kyndon kaba khlaiñ ba ka BJP kam dei satia ban thombor ne peit beiñ ïa ki niam bapher bapher lym kumta kan bha ba kin jngai lailum laiwah na ka jingïadei bad jan bad katei ka party.

    Ha kajuh ka por ka HYC ka kyntu ïa baroh ki dkhot jong ka BJP Meghalaya kiba dang burom ïa baroh ki niam ha ka jylla, ba kin ïa kren ïa ki nongïalam jong ki bad ba lada kim lah ban leh kumta, kan bha ba kin weng noh ïalade na katei ka party.

    Na ka liang ka HSPDP pat, ha u kyrwoh ba la phah da u Chairman, Media Cell ka party, Bah Londoner Sohtun u la pynpaw ba ka party ka pyrshah jur halor katei ka rai ba la shim da ka sorkar kmie ka bym burom shuh ïa ka sngi ba kyrpang jong ki paid khristan. U la ong ruh ba kane ka dei ka jingiuhroit ïa ka jinglong laitluid jong ka jingngeit niam ha ka ri baroh kawei bad ïa kane ka jingleh dei ban pynrem da baroh.

    Na ka liang u Bah RL Tariang, MLA barim bad dkhot ka BJP u la ong ba katei ka jingthmu kan ktah jur ïa ka jingsngew jong ki paidbah ha kane ka ri ba lah ban mane blei laitluid. U la kyntu jur ruh ïa u Myntri Rangbah ba u dei ban weng ne pynduh noh mardor ïa katei ka rai ban buh ïa ka Digital India ha ka Good Friday, hapoh ki 24 kynta.
Pynher shithi ka BJP sha u Modi ban pynkynriah jingrakhe ‘Digital India Day’
Pharia u Mukul Sangma da ka jingsngewniam: BJYM
13 April, 2017
Shillong, ïaiong, 12: Ka Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) 17- North Shillong Mandal Committee mynta ka sngi balang ka la pynher da ka shithi sha u Narendra Modi, Myntri Rangbahduh ka ri da kaba kyrpad ïa u ban pynkynriah noh ïa ka jingrakhe ïa ka ‘Digital India Day’ ha ka 14 tarik mynta u bnai namar ka jingïatakhuh bad ka jinglehniam ‘Sngi Thohdieng Bakhuid’ ki Khristan ha ka Jylla bad ka pyrthei baroh kawei.

    Haba pdiang sngewbha ïa ka jingpynbna u Narendra Modi ban rakhe ïa ka Digital India Day ha ka ri baroh kawei, hynrei ka BJP 17- North Shillong Mandal Committee ka la pynpaw pat ïa ka jingsngew kyndit ba ka Sorkar NDA kan jied ïa ka sngi ‘Good Friday.’

    “Ngi kwah ban pyntip sha phi ba ka 14 tarik, Ïaiong, 2017 ka dei ka sngi bakhraw jong ki Khristan ha satlak ka pyrthei kiba niew ïa kane ka sngi kum ka Sngi Thohdieng Bakhuid, kaba dei ruh ka sngi ïap jong u Trai Jisu Khrist,”ong u Bah W.O Thangkhiew ha ka dorkhas sha u Narendra Modi.

    “Ngi da thrang ban ïashim bynta lang ha ka jingrakhe ïa ka Digital India Day, hynrei ka jingjied ban rakhe ïa kane ka sngi ha ka Sngi Thohdieng Bakhuid ka long pynban kum ka jingkyntait ïa ki Khristan ban ïadon bynta lang ha ka jingrakhe. Na ka bynta ka jingmyntoi lang baroh, ngi kyrpad ïa phi ban kynriah noh ïa kane ka jingrakhe hadien ka 16 tarik mynta u bnai (sngi u Blei) kaba ki Khristan ki rakhe ïa ka sngi Mihpat jong u Trai Jisu Khrist na ka jingïap,” la ong une u nongïalam ka Party.

    Ha kajuh ka por u Bah JA Lyngdoh, uba long u Executive Member ka BJP Meghalaya Unit, bad u President ka Catholic Association Shillong Archdiocese, u la phah ïa ka jingkyrpad sha u Narendra Modi, Myntri Rangbahduh ka ri, ban pynkynriah noh ïa ka jingrakhe ïa ka Digital India Day na ka sngi thohdieng mynta ka taiew sha kawei pat ka sngi, khnang ba kan ym ktah ïa ka jingsngew jong ki riewngeit Khristan ha ka Jylla bad ka ri baroh kawei.

    U Bah Egenstar Kurkalang, President ka Bharatiya Janata Yuva Morcha (BJYM), Meghalaya Unit u la kynnoh ba u Mukul Sangma, Myntri Rangbah ka Jylla u la pharia ïa ka imlang ka sahlang da ka jingsngewniam halor ka jingkynnoh jong u ba ka Sorkar NDA ka rakhe ïa ka Digtal India ha ka sngi 'Good Friday'.

    “Ka dei tang ka jingleh politik jong u (Mukul Sangma),” ong une u Nongïalam ka BJYM.

    “Hato u Mukul um tip bad um burom ïa u Dr. B.R. Ambedkar, u Kpa bad u u nongsaiñdur ïa ka riti Synshar ka ri India ha kaba ki jaidbynriew bapher bapher bad ki jaitniam bapher bapher naduh ki ritpaid haduh ki heh paid ki ïoh ban tyngkai bad bud laitluid ïa ki riti ki dustur jong ngi da ka jingsaiñdur jong une u riewkhraw bad ïa ka Sixth Scheduled ruh la pynwandur da ka jingïalam bastad jong une u riewkhraw kaba long kawei ka jingïada kyrpang ïa ngi ki riewlum,”ong u Bah Egenstar.

    “Kumta ïa ka 14 tarik,Ïaiong la juh rakhe manla u snem ha baroh kawei ka ri India wat ha kiwei ruh ki ri. Kumta mynta ka kynti ruh ka Sorkar India ka burom ïa une u riewkhraw,”la bynrap u Bah Egenstar.

    U ong ba ka jingkynnoh jong u Mukul Sangma, ka dei ka buit ïalam bakla ïa ki paidbah bad ka jingpynkylla politk jong u bad kyntu ïa ki paidbah ba kim dei ban sngewthuh bakla ne ngop ha kum kine ki nongïalam shimkabu, hynrei ki dei ban da pynshong nongrim.     “Ka dei ka jinglehraiñ ïa u Mukul Sangma kat u Myntri Rangbah ka Jylla um sngewthuh ïa kane,” la kynthoh u Bah Egenstar.
Hukum ka High Court ban pynlong ïa ka Municipal Election ha Meghalaya
13 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaïong 12: Ka Ïingkashari Meghalaya High Court haba pynwai noh ïa ka Public Interest Litigation (PIL) , kala sngewdei ba donkam ban thaw ïa ki lad ki lynti ha ka ban lah pyndep kham kloi ïa baroh ki jingdonkam na ka bynta ban lah pynlong noh ïa ka elekshon Municipal ha ka Jylla.

    Kane ka Public Interest Litigation (PIL) ka dei kaba la mudui da u Pawan Sharma uba la mudui sha Ïingkashari halor ka jing bym lah jong ka Sorkar Jylla ban pynlong ïa ka elekshon Municipal wat hapdeng ka hukum jong ka Ïingkashari Supreme Court jong u snem 1999 ba bthah ba hap ban pynlong ïa kane ka elekshon hapoh ka hynriew bnai.

    “Ngim lap daw shuh ha kaban pynbteng ïa ka PIL bad namar kata ngin hap ban pynwai noh ryngkat ki jingsngew dei ba don kam ban thaw ïa ki lad ki lynti ban pyndep ïa baroh ki jingdonkam da ka jingshimkhia bad buh hakhmat eh ïa ka kam” ong u Chief Justice Dinesh Maheshwari bad Justice Ved Prakash ha ka hukum ba mih hynnin ka sngi.

    “Ngi la sngew hun ba ka Sorkar Jylla kala leh ïa la ka jongka kamram haba ïadei bad ka jingpynlong ïa ka elekshon Municipal hynrei ïa kane ym shym la lah ban pynlong kat kum ka jingpruid dak jong ka Riti Synshar ka Ri bad namar kata, ym lah ban ïaid lait ïa ka jingdonkam ban pynkylla thymmai ïa ki kyndon jong ka Act u snem 1973” ong ka Division Benech haba bishar ïa ka PIL.

    U Advocate General ka Jylla u BP Todi ula pynpaw ba ka Sorkar Jylla kala pyrshang ban pynlong ïa ka elekshon bad ka jing shisha hi ka long ba ka Sorkar kala dep buh ruh ïa ka tarik ban ïathep vote kata ha ka 25 tarik Naiwieng 2000 hynrei tang uwei u kyrtong ula wan thep kyrteng uba la kynran dien noh hadien bad dei namar kata ka khlem lah shuh ban pynlong ïa ka elekshon.

    Ka Ïingkashari ka shem ruh ba ka jingduna ki nongïashimbynta ka dei ruh namar ka jingpyrshah jong ki Dorbar Shnong bad ki Sengbhalang bad khnang ban lah wanrah ïa ka jingïasngewthuh jingmut, la thaw ruh ïa artylli ki Working Group Committee ha u snem 2006 bad 2008.

    Ka Sorkar Jylla kala pynpaw ruh ba ka Article 243-ZC jong ka Riti Synshar ka Ri kala khang ban pynlong ïa ki elekshon Municipal ha ki jaka ba hap hapoh ka Sicth schedule. Kala kular ruh ba ka Tnad Urban Affairs ka Jylla kan sa shim ïa ki sienjam ban pynkylla thymmai ïa ka Act 1973 bad ban pynbna noh ïa ki jaka ba hap hapoh ka Municipal khnang ban lah ha kaban pynlong noh ïa ka elekshon Municipal kat kum ka Aiñ.
Naduh 18 tarik rai ka MSSASA ban sangeh treikam khlem pud sngi
13 April, 2017
Shillong, ïaiong, 12: Ki nonghikai SSA bad 4th Teachers ka Jylla kiba don hapoh ka shatri jong ka Meghalaya SSA School Association (MSSASA) mynta ka sngi balang ki la pynbna ba kin pynlong da ka jingsangeh treikam kaba khlempud sngi ne Indefinite Strike ka ban sdang naduh 18 tarik mynta u bnai lada ka Sorkar MUA-II ka dang ïai kuman ïa ka jingdawa ban pynkiew tulop shi spah na ka shispah.

    Kane ka jingïakhih ki nonghikai SSA bad 4th Teachers ka jylla ka long ban pynbor ïa ka Sorkar MUA-II ba kan pyllait noh mardor ïa ka siew tulop bathymmai ïa ki 12481 hajar ngut ki nonghikai SSA, bad ka Arrear ka ban treikam naduh u bnai Ïaiong, 2016.

    Ka MSSASA ka la dawa ruh ïa ka Sorkar MUA-II ba kan mynjur noh ïa ka jingpynkiew tulop jong ki 1521 ngut ki nonghikai 4th Teachers kaba la sahteng naduh u snem 2013 tad haduh kine ki sngi. Nalorkata, ka MSSASA ka la dawa ruh ba ka Sorkar kan pynbeit noh mardor ïa ka kynrum kynram ha kaba ïadei bad ka result jong ki nonghikai ba ïakhun ïa ka eksamin D.El.Ed jong ka Batch 2013-2014.

    Shwa ban pynbna ïa kane ka jingïakhih, da ki hajar ngut ki nonghikai ha ryngkat bad katto katne ki khun ki kti jong ki, ki la pynlong ka jingïaid proseshon naduh madan jingkieng Nongthymmai bad pynkut ha Parking Lot, Addl. Secretariat, Shillong ha ryngkat ka rah ïa ki jingthoh bad ki jingpyrta ba pynrem ïa ka Sorkar MUA-II bad ïa u Mukul Sangma, Myntri Rangbah ka Jylla, kynthup ruh ka jingdawa hiar shuki ïa ka Deborah C. Marak, Myntri ka tnat School Education and Literacy ka Sorkar Jylla.

    U Bah Aristotle Rymbai, President ka MSSASA haba kren ha kane ka sngi, u la ong, “ngi la ïaishah baroh shikatta, da ka jingkhmihlynti ba ka Sorkar MUA - II kan shimkhia ïa ki jingeh ki nonghikai SSA bad 4th Teachers ba ki la pynsngew na ka por sha ka por khamtam ha kaba ïadei bad tulop thymmai bad Arrears jong ki 12481 hajar ngut ki nonghikai SSA kaba ki dei ban ïoh naduh u Ïaiong, 2016 katkum ka jingpynmih hukum da u Commissioner bad Secretary ka tnat pule puthi ka jylla uba long ruh u State Mission Director ka SEMAM ha ka 31 tarik Risaw, 2016 kaba haduh mynta ka Sorkar Jylla kam pat pyllait satia, ban pynkiew tulop ïa ki 4th teachers kiba don 1521 ngut hapoh ka jylla kaba la shu sah teng naduh u snem 2013, pynban ka Sorkar ka la ïai sngap mynthi bad ïai leh kyllut.”

    Haba kynthoh ïa ka jingleh kuman ka Sorkar Jylla ban pynbeit ïa ka result D.El.Ed, une u nongïalam ka Seng u la ong, “ka Sorkar Jylla kam shym la lah ban pynbeit ïa ki kynrum kynram jong ka result Diploma in Elementary Education (D.El.Ed) kaba la shu sahteng mynta lah shi snem tam, hynrei phewse ka Sorkar Jylla ka ïalehkai pynban bad ka hok jong ngi ki nonghikai."

    “Lada kane ka Sorkar ka don shisha ka jingkitkhlieh balei kam leh ei ei halor ka result Diploma in Elementary Education (D.El.Ed) kaba ka la ïateh soskular bad ka NIOS ha kaba 7822 hajar ngut ki nonghikai kiba hikai ha ka kyrdan Elementary ki shah ktah mynta na ka jingleh thurmur jong ka NIOS bad lano kan sdang pat ban phah pyntbit ïa ki nonghikai kiba dang hap ban pyndep ïa ka Professional Qualification (D.El.Ed) ne ka ap haduh ba ka Sorkar Pdeng kan da pynmih hukum ban weng kam ïa ki,” bynrap shuh shuh u Bah Aristotle.

    U ong ruh ba u Mukul Sangma, Myntri Rangbah ka Jylla u la shu thok pylleiñ pylleiñ hapoh ka Dorbar Mang Tyngka ba dang shu kut shen jong ka Ingdorbar Thawaiñ ban pynkiew tulop shi spah na ka shispah ïa baroh ki nonghikai.

    “Ngi kwah ban shai kdar naduh u bnai bad u snem aiu ka Sorkar kan pyntreikam ïa ka jingpynkiew tulop, katno yn pynkiew haba u Myntri Rangbah u ong shispah na ka shispah,” ong une u Nongïalam ka MSSASA.

    Ha kaba ïadei bad ka jingdawa ki nonghikai 4th Teachers, u la ong, “balei ïa ki 1521 spah ngut ki 4th teachers kiba hikai ha ki SSA Upper Primary School la shu ieh beit ha ka jingsiew kaba tang T. 6000 hajar shi bnai naduh u snem 2013 haduh mynta, balei kine ki 1521 kim dei ki nonghikai, balei ka Sorkar ka shu kut tang ha ki jingkular ban pynkiew noh ïa ka tulop jong ki kumba la leh ïa kiwei pat hynrei shu heh tang ka kular ka kam pat ym ïohi haduh mynta.”

    “Kane ka jingsngap jar jong ka Sorkar Jylla ka pyni shaikdar ba kam kwah shuh ba ki nonghikai kin don ha skul bad pyndep ïa la ka kamram, hynrei ka pynbor ba ngin mih sha surok ban ïoh ïa la ka jong ka hok,” kynthoh u Bah Aristotle.

    Shwa ban pynwai ïa ka jingïalang, ki nonghikai ki la wiangding ruh ïa ka dur tyngshop jong u Mukul Sangma, Myntri Rangbah ka Jylla kum ka dak ban pynrem jur ïa ka bym pynurlong ïa ka kular ba u la khlei hapoh ka Ingdorbar dang shen.
Sha ka kyrdan College, mih ka sur na jingrakhe Jubili Rupa ka skul Kyntiew Shaphrang
13 April, 2017
Laitlyngkot, Ïaiong 10 : Ka sngi pynhap pyrda ïa ka jingrakhe Jubili Rupa jong ka skul Kyntiew Shaphrang Secondary, Laitlyngkot ka la pynmih ïa kawei ka sur, kata ïa ka jingdonkam ban kyntiew noh sha ka kyrdan College ïa katei ka skul kaba sdang mynshwa tang da 20 ngut ki khynnah skul ha u snem 1991.

    Kiba bun ki nongkren, kynthup naduh u Myntri ka tnad Public Health Engineering (PHE) Bah Prestone Tynsong ba dei ruh MLA barim ka thaiñ, nangta u MLA ka Sohra, Bah Titos Chynne bad kiwei kiwei ki la pynpaw ïa ka jingdonkam ban kyntiew kyrdan noh ïa katei ka jaka pule sha College.

    Na ka liang u Myntri haba kren kum u Kongsan u la ong, ba kim dei satia ban ap ïa ka sorkar ban sdang ïa ka College. “Peit ha Nongpoh, Mawkyrwat bad Sohra, hadien bun bun snem ba la seng ba ka sorkar ka sa ithuh ïa ki (kum ki Government College),” u la ong.

    Da kaba pynkynmaw ba ïa katei ka skul ruh la seng tang da ka jingnoh synñiang lang ki nongshong shnong hapoh ka jingïalam jong u sordar barim ka Elaka, (L) B Shabong, u Bah Prestone u la ong, “Lada don ka mon ym don kaba lah ban khang. Kiba ju bam kwai 500 tyngka lah ban ai noh 200 tyngka (na bynta jingdonkamka college) bad wat manga ba khlaiñ dih sikret ruh ngan pynduna noh na ka bynta ka college.”

    Ha kajuh ka por u la ong ruh ba katei ka skul ka don ha ka thup ba hakhmat eh ban ïoh ïa ka skim Asian Development Bank (ADB), kyrpang na ka bynta ki iing skul kiba paka bad kiwei ki jingdonkam kiban ïa hap katkum kane ka juk mynta.        Halor katei ka phang, u Bah Prestone u la ong ruh ba u long uba kloi ban treilang ryngkat ryngkat na ka bynta ban kyntiew ïa ka thaiñ baroh kawei.

    Ha kane ka sngi, u Myntri u la ïaroh ruh ïa ki nongseng kiba dei ki nongsynshar shnong kiba la ïohi jngai ïa ka jingdonkam ka jingnang jingstad na ka bynta ka bit ka biang jong ka lawei ki khun ki kti.

    “Ki dkhot ka Managing Committee ki lah ban wan kynduh ïanga namar ka vocational course kadei ka lad aikam ïa kito kiba donsap, kaba wat naduh ka sorkar pdeng haduh sorkar jylla ki shimkhia bha,” u la bynrap biang.

    U MLA ka Sohra pat u la ong ba kam don jingeh lada na ka liang ki nongmihkhmat, nongsynshar shnong bad ki paidbah ki ïa tylli lang ryngkat bad ka managing committee ban sdang ïa ka college. U la ong ruh ba hadien 25snem ka jingtreilang, ka skul ka la kiew arted kumba long mynta, kumjuh kan long ïa ka college lada ïa trei lang.

    Ha kane ka sngi, u Myntri u la ai mynsiem halor ka jingmaitphang jong u principal katei ka skul halor ka jingdonkam ban sdang noh wat ïa ki ‘vocational course’, ne ka jingai jinghikai pyntbit ïa ki samla ba kin lah ban sengkam sengjam khnang ba kin lah ban ieng ha la ki jong ki kjat. “Ka sorkar kam lah ban seng ITI haman laki jaka, kumta dei lyngba ki skul bad ki jaka ai jinghikai, ba ka sorkar lyngba ka tnad Labour ka ju kyrshan ban pynlong ïa kum kitei ki prokram,” u la ong.

    Kiba bun ki nongkren ki la ïathuh ruh ïa kiba bun ki jingeh halor ki jingïaid lynti jong ka skul tangba ki jop lut ïa kitei baroh da ka jingïatrei lang ryngkat ryngkat.

    Ha kane ka sngi la ïoh ruh ïa ka jingkren na u Principal ka skul, Babu LH Shabong, nangta na u Sirdar ba dei ruh president ka Managing Committee bad kiwei kiwei ha kaba la pynphuh da ki jingshad tynrai, ki jingrwai, ki jingshad, ki jingsam khusnam, ka jingpyllait ïa ki thup sah kynmaw bad ruh ka jingïathuh ïa ka histori lyngkot jong ka skul na ki khynnah skul barim ha ki sur jingrwai.

    Nalor ki nonghikai bad ki khynnah skul, la donlang ruh u MDC ka Sohra Bah Donevan Wahlang, MDC ka Langkyrdem Bah Jansing Tynsong, Bah Gavin Mylliemngap, ki Rangbah Shnong bad Rangbah Dong jong ka Elaka, ki nonghikai na kiwei ki skul bad kiwei kiwei.    La pynkut ïa katei ka jingrakhe da ka jingpynhiar noh ïa ka lama jong ka skul, da u Kongsan.

Byrthen u Myntri bym poi ki ophisar : Ha kane ka sngi u Myntri u la pynpaw ruh ïa ka jingbymsngewtynnad halor ka jingbym poi lang ki ophisar ka tnad pule puthi ha katei ka jingrakhe. “Kane ka bym lah ban long, ngan sa rah ïa kane ha ka sorkar,” u la ong da kaba bynrap ba ha ka jingshisha kitei ki ophisar jong kito ki tnad ki dei ban don lang ha katei ka sngi.

Imat ka Ishu bam dohmasi ka long mat         kaba eh tam ïa ka BJP ha Meghalaya    
S.N. Syiemlieh,Ex-Acting Sirdar Dwara            Nongtyrnem Sirdarship
13 April, 2017
             Lym kumta balei kan hap ban da kynthoh kat haduh ki lad pathai khubor, ban ong: Ynnai pynbor khang bam dohmasi. Kane baroh ka thew beit tang kumno ban pynthame bad pynbieit ha ka Election 2018 Kum uwei na ki Riew Rangbah Trai Shnong ka Jylla Meghalaya. Nga kren da kaba shai haba da lei lei phin nym lah ban pynbor lane khang ïa ki paid nongshong shong shnong ka Jylla Meghalaya, u Khynriam, u Pnar, u Bhoi, u War, ban ong phim bit ban bam doh ïa ka Masi, naba naduh ki longshuwa manshuwa ki la pynlong kum ka Riti ka Dustur ban bam doh, ym tang ïa ka doh Masi, hynrei ïa baroh ki jait doh u Khasi u ju bam, lait tang ïa ka doh briew te ym pat ju ïohsngew ba u Khasi un bam.

    Hynrei kumba long u thie u khar rithor pat katba kum ka riti ka dustur ka jong u kim ju bam doh la ka long ïa kano kano ka jaid doh kim ju bam. Ha baroh ki Jylla ka ri thor, lait tang ki Musalman kiba bam doh. Namarkata kan shem jingeh shikatdei ïa ki Nongïalam ka BJP hangne hapoh ka Jylla Meghalaya naba ha baroh ki bynta ka don ka jingïapher.

    La ka long ha ka ktien ka thylliej, la ka long ha ka bam ka dih, la ka long ha ka riam ka beit, la ka long ha ka jait ka kynja, ka shongkha ka shongman.

    Ki Nong Meghalaya haba ïathoh shongkurim, u Rangbah u hap ban leit sha ïing ka kynthei, katba u thie u Dkhar Rithor pat haba ïakyntiew kurim u Rangbah u leit shim ïa ka kynthei bad wanrah sha ïing la jong, ym tang katta u da pynkylla bad jait bad khong ha ka jait la ka jong (Kpa). Katba ngi ki Nong Meghalaya te em, dei hi ka kynthei ka ban bat ïa la ka kur, ka jait ka kynja.

    Te haba haduh katne ka don ka jingïapher, hapdeng, ki jylla rithor bad jylla rilum Meghalaya jong ngi, phi tharai ban ong kumba la ïohi ha ki lad pathai khubor:- Ba ki nong Meghalaya kin kyrshan tylli ïa ka BJP ha u 2018: Ha nga hi ngam sngewlah ngeit ïa kane ka jingong. Kane ka dei tang ka nia election ban pynthame ïa ki paidbah Nongkyndong ka Jylla Meghalaya. Nga ong da kaba shai, kane kam dei shuh ka por juk maw hynrai hapoh ka jylla Meghalaya hi nga lah ban ong ki la kham shemphang ki paidbah Nongkyndong ban jied ïa ki Nongmihkhmat sha ka Dorbar thaw aiñ ka Jylla Meghalaya ban ïa ki nong sor, ki paidbah nongkyndong ki dang bat ïa ki rukom, ki riti ki dustur. Katba ki nongsor pat naba ki la ïa kyrsum ktieh, ïa khleh jaktung naduh u laiphew jait bynriew u la ïa kyrsum ktieh lang hapoh Sor Shillong, ym ithuh shuh uno u Ri thor lane uno u riewlum, uno u Khasi, uno u Dkhar.

    Namarkata, ha nga hi watla ka lad pathai khubor ka ong:- Ba ki paidbah ka Jylla Meghalaya kin ai ka jingkyrshan kaba pura ïa ka BJP ha u 2018, ha nga hi te em ngam lah ban ngeit ïa kane haba da lei lei ruh kan nym lah ban long. Ngin sa ïa peit ïa u soh u ban mih ha u 2018 kan nym slem shuh ka por. U Riewpule bniah ïa ka Jylla Riewlum Meghalaya.
Hato ka UDP ka bud ïa ki nongrim treikam ka BJP; kylli u Dr Mukul
“Bishar bniah ïa ki nongrim ba phi ieng ko seng riewlum”
12 April, 2017
Shillong, Iaiong 11 : U Myntri Rangbah ka jylla u Dr Mukul Sangma mynta ka sngi u la kyntu ïa ki seng saiñ pyrthei riewlum ba kin da bishar bniah bin ba bin ïa ki nongrim ba ki ïeng ban ïa kaba suri kup snieh langbrot.

    Kane ka jingkren jongu ka long halor ka jingsngew khia ïa ka jingshim rai ka sorkar NDA ba ïalam da ka BJP ban rakhe ïa kata ka Digital India Day ha ka Good Friday kaba dei ka sngi ba kyrpang tam ba ki Khristan ha baroh kawei ka ri ki rakhe ïa ka Sngi jingshah iap jong u Trai Jisu halor ka Diengphna.

    “ Ka la pynkhih ïa ka mynsiem bad jingmut jongnga ban ai jingmut ïa ki paralok na ki seng riewlum bakin bishar bniah halor ki nongrim ba ki ïeng”. U la ong kumne namar u sngew kyndit ban ïohi ïa ki jingmih khubor na kawei ka seng riewlum kata ka UDP ba ka sngew biang ban ïatrei lang bad ka BJP namar kidei kiba ïahap jingmut bad ïadei bha ki rukom treikam. Halor kane u la ong kumno ka UDP bad ka BJP kin ïatrei lang?.

     “ Hato ka UDP ka bud ïa ki nongrim treikam ne ki agenda jongka BJP? U Dr Sangma u la ong kumne ruh halor ka nongrim ba uwei na ki nongïalam ka UDP u la pynpaw ba ka BJP ka dei ka party kaba biang bad sngew ïahap jingmut ban ïatreilang tangba u Dr Sangma u la ong ha ka juh ka por pat la kynthoh pyrshah ïa ka jingkhang pyniap bad bam doh masi ha kiba bun ki jylla”

    “ Haba kumne kumno kata ka BJP kan long ka party kaba biang bad ban pdiang da ka UDP kaba dei ka seng riewlum. La ka long kumta ka UDP ka dei ban pynshai sha ki paidbah ba ka don ki juh ki agenda kum ki jongka BJP, lym kumta balei kin shu thok shu shukor ïa ki paidbah ka jylla” ong u Dr Mukul.     U la ong “ Ka long kaba ma ban ïoh sngew ba ka UDP ka lah ban pdiang bad ïatrei lang bad ka BJP kaba mut ba ki riam thok ne ki long kum ki suri kup snieh langbrot ïa ki paidbah namar ha ka kyrteng jong ka seng riewlum la pynbieij ia ki paidbah katba ki agenda treikam ki long kum ki jong ka BJP hi”.

    Haba phai sha ki jingjia kiba jia ha kylleng ka ri, u myntri rangbah u la ong “Haba ka BJP ka la khlaiñ ngi la tip lypa ba kine kiei kiei baroh kin jia namar la dep thoh lypa ïa ki dak ha ki kynroh”.     Kin dang don bun ki jingjia ba ki paidbah kin ïohi sa ïano pat kin wanrah kum u President ka India, ïano kin dang pynlong Chief Minister ha ki jylla namar khlem da bishar bniah kiei ki ban long nongïalam kumno ka jinglong jongki hynrei la shu kyntiew beit sha ka shuki kumba la jia ha Utter Pradesh.

    Shuh shuh haba kynthoh ïa ki mat treikam ka BJP u la ong “ Hato mynta ngi la long kum ka Pakistan namar kumba paw ki dak ki shin ngi la iaid sha kata ka lynti da kine ki kam kiba la paw mynta. Ki la sdang ban sei kawei ka card hadien kawei pat na ka shadem jongki.

Sdang ka FKJGP da ka ‘Socio-Economic Movement’ ban ïakhun pyrshah mynder ha Jylla
12 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong 11: Ka Federation of Khasi Jaiñtïa & Garo People (FKJGP) hynne ka sngi kala pynsdang ïa ka ‘Socio-Economic Movement’ ban kyrsiew thïah bad ban pynkupbor ïa ka Jaidbynriew ha kaban ïakhun pyrshah ïa ka jingwan rung kyrthep ki Bar Jylla bad Mynder Ri hapoh ka Jylla.

    Ka FKJGP kala pyllait paidbah ruh ïa ka kot lyngkdop (Concept Note) bala ai kyrteng ‘Ka Jingkieng Diengjri’-kaba kdew ïa ka Jingshemphang, ka Jingïashah, ka Jingkitkhlieh, ka Jingskhem bad ka thong ban kyntiew ïa ka ïoh ka kot lem bad ban tei ïa ka Imlang Sahlang jong ka Jaidbynriew.

    Ïa kane ka kot lyngkdop la pyllait paidbah da uwei u Nongtreikam lajong ba pawnam ka Jylla u Bah Honsen Lyngdoh ha ka jing ïalang bala pynlong ha Dinam Hall, Jaïaw ha ka jingïadon ryngkat ki arngut ki President barim ka Seng u Bah Emlang Lytan bad u Bah Joe Marweiñ bad kiwei kiwei ki Nongïalam Sengbhalang kynthup ka NESO, KSU bad RBYF.

    “Ka Socio-Economic Movement ka dei ka movement jong ki paidbah bad ka dei ka lynti ba thymmai ban ïakhun pyrshah ïa ka jingwan tuid kyrthep ki Bar Jylla hapoh kane ka Jylla jong ngi” ong u Bah Wellbirth Rani, President ka FKJGP haba kren hapoh ka jingïalang.

    Ka FKJGP ka dei kawei na ki Sengbhalang ba khlaiñbor ka Jylla kaba la ieng ban dawa ha kaban pyntreikam noh da ki aiñ ki kyndon ba pyrrkhing ban tehlakam ïa ka jingrung kyrthep ki Bar Jylla bad ki Mynder ri.

    U Bah Wellbirth Rani ula ong ba lada kane ka Movement jong ka FKJGP ka long kaba jop, ka Jylla kan nym donkam shuh ban dawa wat ïa ka Inner Line Permit (ILP).

    Shuwa kane, u Bah Wellbirth ula ong ba ka jingïakhun pyrshah mynder kala sdang naduh u snem 1979 hynrei kane ka jingïa khih kala shu long tynneng bad long tang ka rukom namar ngi klet ban pynkhïah ïa ki daw tynrai jong kane ka jingeh. U ong “Haba bishar bha (post mortem) ïa ka jinglong jingman jong ka Jaidbynriew, ka kyrdan ba ka don bad kiwei kiwei, kala pynlong ïa nga ban hap pyrkhat thymmai”.

    U Bah Wellbirth u ong ba ka por kala dei ba ka Jaidbynriew kan hap kyndit thïah noh na ka jingleh bakla baroh, da kaba ai nuksa halor ka jingaiwai ïing sha ki Bar Jylla bad ka jingailad ba kin knieh ïa ka kamai ka kajih nalor kiwei kiwei. U ong “Lada ym don mano mano ruh ba kwah ban aiwai ïing ha ka dor kaba heh, ngi lah ban nym donkam satïa ban buh wat ïa ka Entry bad Exit Point”. Kat kum ka jingong jong u, “Dei ma nga maphi kiba khot ïa ki Bar Jylla ban wan sha kane ka Jylla. Ngi kloi ban jaka sah, ai dukan ba ki shong....Ka dei ka jingshisha ba kam dei satïa ka Sorkar Jylla kaba khot ïa ki Bar Jylla ban wan buhai shnong hangne”.

    Haba ban jur ïa ka jingdonkam ban trei beit ïa kano kano ka kam khlem ka jinglehraiñ, u Bah Wellbirth ula ong “Ka por kala dei ba ki briew jong ngi ba kin sdang ban trei hi noh ïa kino kino ki kam khnang ba kum ka Jaidbynriew kan lah ban knieh noh ïa ki kam ki jam na ki Bar Jylla”.

    Haba kren ha kajuh ka sur, u General Secretary Ban Dundee C Khongsit ula ong “Lada ki briew jong ngi hi kim lah ban trei shitom, kan nym don jingmut satïa ban don ïa ki Aiñ ki kanun ban tehlakam ïa ka jingrung ki mynder”. U ong ba lyngba kane ka Movement, ka FKJGP kan long kum ka nongïarap bad ban btin lynti ïa ki samla khlem kam khlem jam ba kin lah ha kaban ieng hala ki jong ki kjat.

    Haba pynpaw ïa ki jingshem jong ka jingwad bnïah jong ka Seng halor ka lad ïohkam ïohjam ha Jylla, u Bah Dundee ula ong ba ka Jylla ka donkam haduh 1.50 lak kilo ka doh masi ha ka shitaiew, 2 lak kilo ka doh syïar ha ka shitaiew, 1.16 lak kilo ka dohsnïang ha ka shitaiew bad 7.2 lak tylli ki pylleng ha ka shitaiew.

    “Hynrei sngewsih ba ngi dang hap shanïah na shabar ka Jylla. Kane ka dei kawei na ki lad ïohkam ïohjam bad kaban kyntiew ïa ka ïoh ka kot” ong une u Nongïalam haba pynpaw ba ka Seng FKJGP ka dang ïai pyrshang ban wad ïa ki lad ki lynti kumno ba ki briew jong ngi kin lah ban ieng hala ki jong ki Kjat. Kiwei pat kiba la ai jingkren ha kane ka sngi ki long u Bah Honsen Lyngdoh, Bah Emlang Lytan, Dr marco Mitri bad kiwei kiwei. Shuwa kane ka jingïalang, ka Seng kala pynlong ïa ka jingïaid Rally da ki kali kaba la sdang naduh ka Ophis treikam jong ka Seng na Mawlai Motsyïar bad ïaid lyngba ka Polo-IGP Point, Barik Point-Motphran bad la pynkut ha Dinam Hall, Jaïaw.

12 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaïong 11: Lai ngut ki Mishoneri kiba la sah da ki phew snem ha India bad trei na ka bynta ka bha ka miat ki paidbah baduk, ki la shah beh ha ka sorkar India, ha kaba ïa ka Visa (ka jingai jingbit ban sah ha India) ym shym la pynthymmai shuh bad la bthah pynban ïa ki ban mih shi syndon na kane ka ri.

    Kine ki laingut ki Mishoneri ki long u Father. Ignacio Galdos Zuazua, u nong Spain uba la wan sha India naduh ka snem 1951 kum u Mishoneri ban trei bad ka Jivan Jyoti Society ha Gujrat. Ka Visa ba la ai khatduh da ka sorkar ka long ha ka 11 tarik u Risaw 2015 bad kut haduh ka 11 tarik u Risaw 2016. Une u la pan ban pynthymmai ïa ka Visa jong u, hynrei ka sorkar ka la kyntait bad la bthah pynban ïa u ban mih noh na India.

    Kawei pat kadei ka Mishoneri kynthei, ka Sister Laurel Judith Seaton na Australia kaba la wan sha India naduh ka snem 1975 kum ka nongtrei kam bhalang bad ka Missionaries of Charity ha Bihar. Hynrei wat hadien 42 snem ba ka la shakri hapdeng kiba duk ba suk ha Bihar, ka sorkar u Modi ka la bthah ia ka ban mih noh na India, khlem ki daw kiba biang.

    Uwei pat udei u Aurele Andre A. Brys, u nong Belgium ba la sah ha India la 51 snem. U trei kum u nongïasyllok bad ka Ranchi Jesuit Society. Une ruh kumba long kitei ki arngut u la shah btah ban mih noh na India, da kaba ka sorkar ka la kyntait ban pynthymmai ïa ka Resident Permit jong u.

    Halor kane ka jingleh ka sorkar u Modi ïa kine ki Mishoneri Khristan, u MP ka Shillong u Bah Vincent H. Pala, u la thoh sha u Myntri Rangbah duh ka ri, u Narendra Modi ban pynpaw ka jingsngewkhia halor kane ka jingjia, kaba long ka jinglehbeiñ ïa ki Mishoneri kiba la trei na ka bynta ka bha ka miat jong ki paidbah. U Bah Pala, u la kyntu ïa u Modi ban tuklar ïa kane ka kam bad ban pynthymmai biang ïa ka Visa bad Resident Permit jong ki.

12 April, 2017
Shillong, Iaiong 11, 2017: Ka Meghalaya Veterinary Services Association, East Khasi Hill District Unit ha ka 7 tarik Iaiong 2017 ka la pynlong ia ka Farmers Workshop ne ka jingai jinghikai ia ki Nongri Jingri ha ka shnong Thangsning ha kaba la ia shimbynta da ki 200 ngut ki paid nongri jingri ka thain kiba la wan na Umtong, Umsham, Laitdiengsai, Nonghulew, Jatah, Nonglyer, Mynriah, Thangsning, Nongdaneng bad na Maitshaphrang SHG bad World Vision, Rableng.

I Bah T.Nongkhlaw, Sordar Shnong ka Thangsning i la ai khublei ia ka Association ba ka la ibit ban wanrah ia kane ka prokram ha Thangsning ha kaba bun ki paid nongri jingri ki don. U la iaroh ruh ia ka jingshakri ka Veterinary Aid Centre kaba don ha Thangsning bad i la kyntu ia ki bor ba halor ban kyntiew noh ia ka khnang ba kan nang lah ban ai ka jingshakri ba kham bha. Ha ka jingkren jong i Dr.W.M.W.Khongwir, i la pynshlur ia baroh ki nongri jingri ban trei shitom ha kane ka kam bad i la kdew ia ka jingdonkam ban pyniar ia ka kam ri jingri namar haduh mynta ka jylla jong ngi ka dang wanrah beit nabar ka jylla ia ka doh ne pylleng.

    Ha ka jingkren plie i kongsan i la iaroh shikatdei ia ka MVSA East Khasi Hills Unit kaba la shim khia ban pynlong ia kane ka prokram ha ka shnong Thangsning kaba long kawei na ka shnong ba bun ki nongri jingri. I la kyntu ia baroh ba kin ia trei shitom ha la ka kam kaba ai ka lad kamai kajih. Lyngba ka jingmang pisa ka sorkar kum ka lad jingiarap la lah ban pynlong ia kane ka workshop ha kane ka jaka bad i la kyntu ruh ia ki paid nongri jingri ba ki dei ban nang trei shitom shuh shuh ban kyntiew ia ka ioh ka kot jong ki.I la ong shuh shuh ba ka phang halor ka jingai kpa ne AI ha ki sniang ka long ka lad ka kabu ia ki nongri sniang ban pynduna ia ka jinglut jingsep ban ri niang kpa. I la ong ruh ba ka sorkar shen kan sa pyntreikam noh ia ka Livestock Mission ka ban long ka jingmyntoi kaba bun ia ki paid nongri jingri.Kum ki nongri jingri ki donkam ruh ia ka jingshemphang ban ri ia ki jingri ban wanrah shibun ka jingiohnong kum ki syiar Kuroiler ne kita ki dual purpose bird ban ri bad kha pylleng bad bam doh. I la pynshlur shuh shuh ia ki ba ka iew ka don beit ban pyniaidiew ia ki mar jong ki la ka long ka doh, ka dud ne ki pylleng.

    Hadien la bteng da ka bynta kaba ar ha ka Technical Session ba la pyniaid da i Dr.(Miss)P.Passah, Executive member ka MVSA, East Khasi Hills Unit, la ioh ia ki jinghikai ha kaba i Dr.Lofty Tyngkan, A.H & Veterinary Officer, ICDP, Upper Shillong i la batai bniah da ka power point presentation ia ka rukom ri ia ki sninag bad ka rukom ai kpa bathymmai ha ki sniang ba la tip kum ka Pig Management with special reference to Artificial Insemination ba la sdang mynta hangtei ha ICDP, Upper Shillong bad ka la pynhun jrut ia baroh ki paid nongri jingri kiba la ioh ka jingbatai ba bniah bad ruh ban ioh jingpynshai ia ki jingkylli jong ki. Ki paidbah mynta kim dei ban khuslai shuh nangno yn ioh niang kpa ban pynshongkha ia ki niang kmie jong ki hynrei kidei ban shim ia kane ka kabu ksiar ba ka sorkar ka la wanrah sha ki paidbah.

    Nangta la pynbud da ka jinghikai kumno ban ri ia ki Masi Ai-Dud ne ka Dairy Management ha kaba i Dr.(Mrs)S.Nongbet, A.H & Veterinary Officer,IDP, Upper Shillong i la batai bniah lyngba ka power point presentation ia ka rukom ri ia ki Masi dud da ka rukom ka jingstad saian ba mynta. Ka jinghikai jong i ka la pynkhih jingmut ia ki nongri jingri ban sdang ban ri noh ia ki masi dud ym ban shu hun ban ri tang ia ki masi local ne masi shnong namar don ki jaid masi dud kum ki Holstein Friesan kiba iahap bha bad ka jinglong ka jaka ha ri Khasi Jaintia jong ngi.

    Khatduh, la ioh sa kawei pat ka jinghikai kumno ban ri ia ki Syiar da ka jingmut ban trei ia ka kum ka kam business ne ka Poultry Farming as an Enterprise ha kaba i Dr.M.Tyngkan, Sr.A.H & Veterinary Officer, Manager Poultry & Pig Farm Mawryngkneng lyngba ka power point presentation i la batai sani bha ba kumno ma ngi ruh ngi lah ban ia kiew lang ha ka kam ri syiar kumba long lem kiwei ki nongri syiar sha ri thor kaba pynlong ia ka ri India ban long kawei na ki ri ba paw khmat ban pynmih pylleng bad doh syiar. I la pynshai shuh ba kumno ngin rat diengkhong ia ka jingjaituh, ka jingartatien bad ban pynduh jait ia kawei ka jingpang kata ka jingpang Ap ba balei ngi ju mlien ban buhteng ia kiei kiei; wat ban ri syiar ngi dang buhteng bad da kumne ngin ym sdang shuh lano lano ban ri syiar ha ka rukom ba ngin iohnong.

    Ha kaba kut la ioh ia ki kyntien ai khublei bad sngewnguh na iwei na ki nongri jingri bad na i Dr.B.K.Blah, Secretary, MVSA East Khasi Hills Unit. (MIPR).

Hadien ba la bishar bniah la lap ba une number u dei ha ka kyrteng u Bah Olson Syiem (9863097030) bad uwei pat ha ka kyrteng Danny Syiem (9863097658),” la ong shuh shuh u Bah Michael ha kane ka ejahar.

Approved Supplier.,” ong u Bah Michael bad bynrap, “u TIN No.17030873088 ba la thoh wat ha ka Quotation hadien ba la tohkit na ophis ka Sales Tax bad na ka Website jong kane ka ophis um don satia. 12 April, 2017
Shillong, Iaiong 11 : U Myntri Rangbah ka jylla u Dr Mukul Sangma u la kob ba ka Congress kan wanrah ïa ka sorkar kaba khlaiñ bad ba ïaineh shuh shuh ha ka jylla hadien ka elekshon 2018.

    “ Ngin ïoh ïa ka sorkar kaba skhem kaba lah ban wanrah ka jingpynkylla dur shuh shuh ïa ka jylla Meghalaya bad kane ka jylla kan long kum ka nuksa ïa kiwei ki jylla ha ka ri” ong u Dr Mukul Sangma.

    U la kular ruh ba ka Congress kan pyndep lut ïa kiwei ki kular kiba ka la khlei sha ki paidbah ha ka por elekshon bad ki nongrim treikam jongka sorkar MUA-II ki long halor ka manifesto jongka party hi wat hapdeng ki diengpynkiang kiba bun bah.

    Halor ka jingpynkhreh ïa ka Elekshon, u Dr Sangma u la ong ka long ka rukom ba ka Congress kan hap ban ïakhun pyrshah ïa ka BJP namar lait na ka Congress ym don kiwei pat ki party kiba lah ban ïakhun ne ïa ai reng ïa ka BJP. “ Nga tip shai ba kin pyrshang kat lah kat ïai ha kane ka jylla hynrei ka Congress ruh ka long kaba la pynkhreh lypa” ong u Dr Mukul.

    Lada phai sha ka ri hi baroh kawei, u la ong “ Lada ka Congress ka tlot, ka BJP kan ïai khlaiñ tang katta ngin sa ïohi shuh ïa ki dak ba la thoh lypa ha ki kynroh. Namar tang shu tlot ka Congress ka lawei jongka ri ka don ha ka jingma kumta u la ong ka Congress kaba la synshar ïa ka ri naduh mynshwa haduh mynta bad dei na ka jingsynshar ka Congress ba ka long kumne kumba long mynta kan ïai ïakhun tyngeh bad kan nym ran dien da lei lei ruh namar ki paidbah kin sa ïohi bad kin sa sngewthuh hi”. U la ong ruh ïa kine ki agenda ba rieh jongka BJP dei ban wad bniah bad sei madan ryngkat ka jingpynsngewthuh sha ki paidbah ïa ka lawei jongka ri.

    U la ong ka jingphai sha kane ka thaiñ shatei lam mihngi kam mut ba ka peit ban ïoh tang ïa ka jingsynshar hynrei ka thong ka long ban pynthame ïa ki paidbah ka ri ba ka BJP ka dei ka party kaba biang namar wat ki paid ka thaiñ shatei lam mihgi ruh ki la pdiang ïa ka. Na kata ka daw ba ki nongïalam ka BJP na kane ka thaiñ ruh ki ïaid iew bha namar ka thong jongka BJP ka long da kumwei pat na shalyndet.

    Haba phai sha ka Nagaland, u la ong ki nong Meghalaya kim dei kum ki Naga, namar ki nong Meghalaya ki kwah ïa ka roi ka par, ka sorkar kaba skhem bad ka jingsynshar paidbah kaba shisha.

    Haba kren ha kane ka sngi kum u kongsan, u Deputy Commissioner ka Ri Bhoi, u C.P Gotmare u la pynpaw ïa ka jingsgewnguh ïa katei ka kynhun kaba la wan ai ïa ka jingshakri da la ka mon sngewbha na ka bynta ban pynduhjaid ïa kajingpang bampong.

    Namarkata, u la ong ba kane ka dei ka kabu ba lyngba katei ka kynhun kaba wan ban ai ka jingshakri kaba da ka mon sngewbha, ki paidbah ruh ki dei ban shim bynta ha kane ka prokram bad ruh ban mih shakhmat na ka bynta ban shah sumar khnang ban dup lap ha ka por kaba biang lada kino kino ki nongshong shnong kiba don ïa kane ka jingpang bampong, u la bynrap.

Da ka jingjop ïa ka Lajong pynkhreh ka Mohan Bagan ban ïoh rah ïa ka I. League
12 April, 2017
Shillong, Iaiong, 11: Ka Mohan Bagan kaba la don lypa ha kane ka nongbah ka pynkhrehbha ïalade ban jop ïa ka Shillong Lajong FC kum shi bynta ban lah ban pynurlong ïaka thong ban ioh ban rah biang sa shisien ïa ka nam lahduh jong ka I. League.

    Ka jingiakhun hapdeng kine ki ar tylli ki kynhun la buh ban long mynta ka sngi ha J.N Stadium. Polo.

    Kine ki ar kynhun ki rung sha kane ka jingïakhun hadien ba ki la ioh ba kin ïa khur ïa la ki nam jop ki jong ki na ki jingïalehkai ba dang shu dep, ha kaba ka Mohan Bagan ka la lah ba kan pynliem ïa ka East Bengal da 2-1, ka Shillong Lajong FC ka la lah ba kan pynliem noh ïa ka DSK Shivajians da 3-2.

    Ka daw ba pynlong ïa ka Mohan Bagan ba kan khreh ban ioh rah biang ïa ka nam lahduh kane ka lympung ïalehkai ka jia long hadien ba ka la lah ba kan jop ia ki artylli ki klob ïalehkai bna nam bad ba radbah bha ha kane ka lympung ïakhun kata ïa ka East Bengal bad kumjuh ïa ka Bengaluru FC.

    Haba ïakren bad ki lad pathai khubor, u Sanjoy Sen coach ka Mohan Bagan, u kam ba ka kynhun ka jong u ka ïai don ha ka thong ban ioh ban rah biang sa shisien ïa ka nam lahduh kane ka lympung, haka juh ka por u la ong ruh ba nangne sha khmat man la ki jingïalehkai kiba ka klob kan ïakhun ki long beit kum ka phainal naka bynta ka jong ki.

    Ban shu ïakren sngew ba ka long kaba suk, hynrei u Sen u sngewthuh bad u tip ba kam long kaba suk ban jop ïa ka Lajong ha ïing jong ka, namar kum ka kynhun kam lah tang ba kan shu peit ngor tang ïa uwei u nong ïalehkai ba kynsai ka Lajong ne ia u Dicka, pynban kan hap ban long kaba phikir ïa kiwei pat ruh ki samla ialehkai kiba ha kano ma kano ka khyllipmat kiba lah ban shna kam ia ka liang ba ki iakhun pyrshah.

    Ka khubor kaba pyn sngewtynnad ia ki arngut ki coach ka long ba kim don jingeh eiei ha ka liang ki player namar baroh ki don hapdeng ka met kaba koit ba khiah bha.

    U Thangboi Singto Coach ka Lajong, ka resol kaba u kwah na kane ka jingiakhun ka long ka jingjop, namar ba ka lai poiñ kan lah ha kaban pyntikna ïaka kynhun hi baroh kawei ba kan ïai neh ïalade ha ka kyrdan kaba saw jong kane ka lympung ïakhun.Pynban haba u buddien bha ïa ka rukom ïalehkai ka Mohan Bagan bad ia ka thong ba ka don naka bynta ban rah ïa ka nam lahduh kane ka lympung, kan pyn long ïa u ba un hap ban pynkhreh janai bha ïala ka jong ka kynhun bad maham ïa ki player ba kim dei satia ban leh kam kai, pynban naduh kaba sdang haduh ban da kut jong ka jing ïakhun kidei ban ïalehkai bha.
Ap ka jingma na u drok
12 April, 2017
Ka jingma ka ap bha mynta ïa ki khun samla na u drok, uba san kynsan u la ioh ban rung ha ka met ka longrynieng kiba bun ki khun samla jong ka jylla khamtam lei lei ha kane ka nongbah, wei shisien ba la ngat ha une u jingdih ba sniew la eh shisha ban bthat na ka jingim kaba ka lawei kaba phyrnai kaba ki khun samla ki ap khmih lynti kan shu kut noh tang ha shiteng por.

    Kumno u drok u ioh ban wan, ka jubab ka shu long ba kino ma kino ki kam ba sniew, kim don jingeh satia ïa ki ban ioh ban rung, namar ki buit kiba har rukom la lah ha kaban pyndonkam naka bynta ban pynpoi ha ki ksang kti kiba bun ki khun samla, kiba wei shisien ba ki la ngat, ki sdang ba kin ïa sam lem sha la ki paralok ba ïajan, nangne pat u drok u suhthied bad par kylleng sawdong.

    Ïa ka thymmei jingwan rah ha ka ïew ïa die ïa thied burieh pat ïa u drok ka dei shisha ka kam kaba eh bad ba jwat bha, kaba haduh mynta mynne, wat la ki bor pulit ki la trei shitom ban lap ïa ka tynrai pynban ka jingtrei ka shu ïai long tang ha kaban ioh kem ïa ki nongpynïaid ïew, hynrei ym ïa kita ki briew kiba shalan bad pynpoi tuh ïa une u jait jingdih uba mynsaw.

    Kumta haba shem bad iohi ïa ka jingpyndonkam palat ïa u drok, ka imlang ka sahlang, ka shnong ka thaw bad ki seng niam baroh, ki king baïong lem ka khlieh ba hato aiu eh la don ha u drok, kaei kaba ki khun samla ki iohnong lada pyndonkam ïa u, la u tei ia kaba bha ne wanrah ïa kaba sniew, ka jubab ka long ba ki samla ki tip ba dei beit tang ka jingsniew, kaba pynthohbria kai ïa ka jinglong ba shi dur ba shi sur ka jong ki, kaba ha ki akher jong ka sngi shu sah jit kai ha ka imlang ka sahlang sah ïathuh khana kai ha ki marjan ki marpa ha la shong ha la thaw.

    Nalor kata, ka jingma lei lei ka long ba haba la kyrni palat ka jingpyndonkam ïa u drok ka long ba ki khun samla ki kylla long ka jingma ïa ka imlang ka sahlang, namar haba la kyrni bad bym lah shah shuh, haba ym ioh pisa sdang sa ka tuh ka thiem, ka lute na ki ïing briew, kaba don u pud uba poi wat shaduh ka kam ban pynïap briew, namar ha ka jingtieng la leh ïa ki kam bym poi pyrkhat.

    Khyndiat hap ban pyrto ïa ka jingtrei ba jar jar bha jong ki bor pulit, khlieh la ka sngi, ki pynap ia ki shrip ki jong ki bad ki ïai kem ïa ki nongdie ia ki drok, kaba shiban ka kham tyngkan bha ïa ki nongshalan ban husiar ioh ma ki ruh ki ngat ha ha ka ruh nar jong ka aiñ, pynban kaba kham sngew noh mynsiem ka long ba ïa ki nongdie ne ïa ki nongpynïaid ïew ïa u drok, ka aiñ briew kam biang satia ban pynshitom ïa kum kine ki briew.

    Ha kiwei ki ri jong ka pyrthei khamtam lei lei sha ki bynta jong ki ri Arab, ïa ki nongdie ne shalan ïa u drok, ka aiñ da shisha ka long kaba tyngeh bha, kaba wei shisien ba la biang ki sakhi satar kiba biang, ka jinghap ban shong phatok ka long da kiba bun bun ki snem, nalor kata ki jaka ba set ïa ki, kidei da shisha kaba pynrah shkor bha ïa ki briew kiba la ngat.

    Hynrei haba phai ha ka ka jylla, katno ngut kita ki briew kiba la shah kem ki shong ha phatok mynta, kiei ki jait jingpynshitom ïa kum kine ki briew, namar katba nang mih ki sngi, I pynban ba ka kam khaiï drok dei kum ka lad seng kam seng jam, shisien la shah kem I kumba ioh shongthait , kaba hadien lada lait na phatok la sdang biang ban leh ïa ka juh ka kam.

    Nalor ka jingtrei borbah ki Pulit la donkam ïa ki shong ki thaw ba kin shim lem ïa ka jingbah khlieh naka bynta ban hikai ïala ki khun samla ban long kiba peitngor bad kiban kiar na ka jingpyndokam ïa u drok, ka jinghikai ka dei ruh ban sdang shwa na la ïing, ha kaba donkam ban buddien ïala ki khun ki kti ban khmih bha ïa ka ïaid ka ïeng ka jong ki, ki jait paralok kiba kumno ki ïajuh ïalang, la ka don ne em ka jingipher ha rukom jinglong ka jong ki naduh ba ki ïalang paralok thymmai.

    Ki shnong ki thaw kin donkam ban peitngor pat ïa ka rukom ïa juh ïa lang, ha ki lynti ki syngkien, kin khmoh bniah ïa ka ïaid ka ïeng, khamtam lei lei ha ki jaka ba lam kynjah, namar ha kum kine ki jaka, ki kylla long ki shlem ban ïa phyrngop bha ha ka jingdih ia u drok.

    Nangta ki jaka pule kum ha ki kolej kidei ki jaka ba kum ki khun samla ki juh ngop bha, kiba shisien ar sien ki ai ei da la ka jong ka mon sngewbha, hynrei haba la kyrni pat sdang ka ïalang lok kynhun ban ïa pynngop lang sa ïa kiwei pat. Ha kum kine ki jaka ki bor ba dei khmih ki donkam ban pynjur bha ïa ka jingïasyllok bad ki khun samla, ha kaba donkam ban pynlong ïa ki jingïalang ban sneng ban kraw bad ban kyntu ïa ki khun samla ba horkit hordang dei ban kiar na u drok, namar sisien ba la ngop tang kata ka jingim ruh kan shu bijai ei.
Kaei kaba ap ïa ngi ki Khasi Pnar
L.G.Laloo
12 April, 2017
     Halor kane ka mat wat lada ngi la jam palat ïa ka 45 snem kum ka jylla, ngi ïohi ba ka long kaba eh ban sngewthuh ïa ki jingmut jingpyrkhat ym tang jong ki Nongïalam hynrei wat ki paidbah ruh. Kat shaba phai yn ïohi ba ñiar ki ban pyrkhat khia ïa la ka Ri ne ka Jaidbynriew hynrei tang na ka bynta ka malade suda. Naduh ki Seng Saiñ Hima, Seng Niam, Seng trei mon sngewbha bad Seng Bhalang kim ïa pher kawei na kawei bad nalor nangta sa ka ïa kdew kti uwei ïa kawei ban pynksan ïa ka MA-NGA. Baroh ki ïohi tang ïa u thngiat jong kiwei ym ïa la u khung. U Nongthaw ïa ka jingrwai ‘Khynriam, u Pnar, u Bhoi, u War u dei u Paid Khasi ba ïar’ u thaw ïa ka da ka jingkyrmen ba kane ka jingrwai kan pyrsad mynsiem ïa ka jingïalong kawei khlem da ïit shiah ïa ki jingïapher ha ka ktien, ka niam ka rukom ne ka jaid ka kynja. Hynrei putet kam long satia kumta bad ka paw pynban ba ka nang pynheh ïa ki kharai jong ka jingsngew kyrpang hapdeng para dong, para shnong bad Para Hima ne para Khasi -Pnar.

    Mynta katba nang jan sha ka snem 2018 bad lyngba ki Print & Electronic Media yn ïohi ba tang shu la kham paw sha khmat baroh la ïa kwah long Syiem (kata MP, MLA bad MDC) bad ñiar ki ban hun tang ban long ki Nongthung Syiem (King maker). Ki Seng Saiñ Hima ki mih kum ki tit bad ki Nongïalam jong kawei pa kawei ka seng lait noh ka Congress ki kren ïa ka jingkylla. Ha kino kiba la mad ïa kine kiei kiei naduh ba la ïoh ïa la ka jong ka Jylla ki la dei ban kylli- KYLLA ïA KAEI? Hato ngim ïohi ba lyngba kine ki 45 snem kumno kine ki Nongïalam ki la ïalam ïa ngi?Hato ngi matlah? naduh u Chief Minister haduh ki MLA la ha ka Ruling ne ka Opposition haba ki kren ïa ka roi ka par ka unemployment, ka jingkoit jingkhiah hato ki kren da kaba pyrkhat khia ïa ka lawei jong ka Jylla? ne ki kren tang ba la shu prompt da ki agent jong ki kiba draft ïa ka speech katkum ka advice ong ki kynrad. U paidbah uba long ka ultimate power ha ka jingshisha um dei shuh ban dang shah pynngop namar u la tip bad mad lut ïa baroh ki jingshisha. U la dei ban sngewthuh ba na ka bynta ka lawei jong ka jaidbynriew ha kane ka kynti, ha man la ki dong bad ki shnong la dei ban wad ïa ki Leader kiba i kop shisha ban long ki Statesman bad ki Legislator, kiba kloi ban sacrifice ïalade na ka bynta ka Ri bad ka Jaidbynriew. Ym tang katta la dei ban wad ïa ki briew kiba don ka vision namar ban shu shaniah ha kiei kiei kiba kine ki lei san snem kumba ka la long haduh mynta yn ym poi shano shano ruh. Ngi la ïohi ba ha ki bnai kiba la dep jong kane ka snem 2017 ki khun ki kti jong ka Jaidbynriew kiba ïakhun ïa ka HSLC Examination ki la kot sha ka 80 hajar tam, nangta lada kheiñ lang sa ïa baroh ki nongpule ha baroh ki laiñ jingpule ha ka Jylla kin poi da ki lak tang ha ka shisnem. Kumta lada ngim jied ïa ki Nongïalam kiba don ka vison, shano ki khun, ki pyrsa jong ngi kin leit bad ha ki 10 snem ki ban wan kaei ka ban jia ïa u thab u dap, u kup shiliang sem shiliang u bym lah ban ïa compete bad ka por.

    Lada u paidbah u ngam jylliew bad jied shiah ïa ka jingpynïaid ïa ka synshar khadar un ïohi ba kine ki Nongïalam jong ngi kiba mynta ki leh ïa kiba bun kiei kiei khlem pyrkhat hynrei tang ban pynsyrwa ïa ka pisa jong u paidbah. Kumno ki kren ïa ki jait pa ki jait ki awareness programme kiba katba nang hikai nangpaw kumba ka jingsniew ka nangroi. Kum ka nuksa, mano ban phohsniew ba ha ki shnong Khasi khamtam kum ha Mawlai yn ïoh kem nongdie bad nongdih drok? Nangta bishar haba ki kren ïa kita ki Riti Dustur ki da sngewthuh ne shu kren tang ban lait jynhaw. Haba ki kren pat ïa ka roi ka par, ka jingsahdien ha ka liang ka pule puthi, ka jingroi ha ka bamsap bad ïa ka jingïuhroit ïa ka hok jong ki kynthei ki khynnah bad kiwei kiwei, hato ki da sngewthuh halade ïa kaei kaba kum ki nongïalam ki dei ban leh? 65 tylli ki snem ki la ïaid bad la ai ha ngi ïa ka District Council ba ïada bad preserve ïa ka culture jong ngi, kum ka jaidbynriew, hynrei haduh mynta, mih aïu? Lada dei ba pynïaid da ki bym dei ki Khasi dang don hok ban kynnoh. Hynrei haba da u jaid u kur la jong ïano yn kynnoh ne kdew kti? hato ym la paw tang ka jingarsap suda? Ki tymmen Khasi ki ju hikai ba ngin ym shaniah ha u dieng pyut. Hynrei na kiei kiei kiba ngi la mad hato ngi lah ban len ba kine ki Nongïalam jong ngi kim dei kita ki dieng pyut? Tang khyndiat ngut eh napdeng jong ki kiba la pyrshang shisha ban trei hok ïa ka kamram kaba u paidbah u la bynshet ha ki na ka por sha ka por hynrei na ka jingïapait ïa pra hapdeng ki para Nongïalam ym lah pynmih soh ei ei ruh em. Kine wat la kim don shuh hapdeng jong ngi mynta hynrei ki la buh ïa ka dak ha u Maw ba ïoh kumno kumno don na ki longdien kiba kwah ban buddien. Ka por ka la nangïaid stet bad lehse na ka jingkiew ha ka thoh ka pule ka Ri ka kyrmen ba lah ban mih ki Tirot Sing bad ki Kiang Nangbah, ki B.Pakem, ki T.H.Rangad ha ka lawei jong ka political arena jong ka Jaidbynriew . Hynrei dang jngai namar ha ka juk tynneng te ym lah shuh ban tip kumno kan long bad lada shu heh tang ka ktien. Ym lah khlem da kdew bad ïanujor kum ka nuksa ïa ka Rukom im jong kiwei kiwei ki para Riewlum jong ka North East kum ki Naga bad ki Mizo. Kine khamtam ha ka liang ka shongkha shongman ne ka riam ka beit, ka ktien ka thylliej lada ki don hapoh ne shabar shnong yn ïohi ba kim ju klet ïa la ka jong katba ma ngi ki Khasi Pnar ngim long kumta. Haba nga pule ïa ka kot jong I Bah Spiton Kharakor kaba i ñiewtang ïa ki jaid bad ki kur Khasi-Pnar, nga kum kylli halade nangne sha khmat, kaei kaba ap ïa ngi ki khun Khasi-Pnar ha ka lawei jong ngi.

    Kat shaba phai tang ki sohkyrdot suda kiba lada uwei u law, uwei pat u teh pynsohsat. Ha ka taïew ba la lah la wan u peon na Post Office ban wad ïa ka address jong iwei i kong iba ai jaid Kharlaloo. Kane ka la pynlong ïa nga ban pyrkhat lada ka long kaba suk ïano ïano ban kylla Khasi tang ba la buh da ka ktien KHAR NA KHMAT te ïaei pat yn ïakren? Nangta shuh shuh la wan sa kawei ka jingmutdur ïa kane ka jingkylla jait khlem aiñ khlem kanun bad ruh ka jingtang jait ka la kylla long ka political venture ban pynheh ïa ka vote bank jong kano kano ka party? Ki Seng Bhalang bapher bapher ki kren bad pyrshah ïa kata ka influx of foreigner bad ki dawa ïa kata ka ILP hynrei lada khlem kano kano ka aiñ kaba pyrkhing halor kane yn ym lah ban leh ei ei wat lada pynpait ïa ka khlieh ha u maw ruh bad ka jingkylli kaba mih kan shu long, Kaei kaba ap ïa ngi ki Khun Khasi-Pnar ha ki snem ki ban dang wan.
Rung phainal ka Bateithymmai ha ka ïakop ‘Yes i Am’
Shillong, ïaiong, 11: Ka Samla Bateithymmai Nongrum ka la poi mynta ka kynti sha ka kylla ïakhun phainal ha ka lympung ïakop pynisap ‘Yes i Am” Zing Tv Channel.
    Ka All Meghalaya Dancers Association (AMDA) ka kyrpad sngewrit ïa ki paidbah nongshong shnong ka Jylla khamtam ïa ki Dorbar Shnong ba kin ai jingpynbna lem lyngba ki tynghung shnong da kaba kyrpad lem ïa ki paidbah ba kin’vote’ ïa i samla Bateithymmai Nongrum.
    “Ngi kyrpad ruh ïa ki sengbhalang bapher bapher ka jylla ba kin shim lem ïa ka jingbahkhlieh ban pathai khubor sha ki paidbah khamtam sha ki thaiñ nongkyndong ki bym pat da tip bha kumno ban ai ‘vote’ lyngba ka Facebook,” ong u kyrwoh ba la phah da u Bah Darwin L. Mawphlang, General Secretary ka AMDA.
    Ban ai vote ïa ka samla Bateithymmai Nongrum, ki paibdah ki lah ban plie ïa ka Facebook account lajong bad ai jingkynthoh (comment) ha ka “link jong ka Yes i Am” kaba thoh ‘Yes i Am Bateithymmai Nongrum” bad ban tip kham bniah ki paidbah ki lah ban wad jingtip na ki nongïalam ka AMDA ne ka samla Bateithymmai Nongrum ha u phone number: 8575667940-7085486196-9436309032.
    Kum ban shu kdew, ka AMDA dang ha ka 30 tarik u bnai baladep ka la pynlong da ka jingïalang paidbah ha Motphran hapdeng u slap bajur ban pan jingkyrshan na ki paidbah ba kin ai jingkyrshan ïa ka Samla Bateithymmai Nongrum
    Ka AMDA ka ai khublei kyrpang ïa ki paidbah nongshong shnong ka Jylla kiba la leh shitom ban ai vote ïa ka Samla Bateithymmai Nongrum bad kumjuh ïa ka shnong Mairang Pyndenumiong lyngba u Sordar uba la pynlong ïa ka jingïalap paidbah kumno ban ai vote ïa kane ka samla donsap.        Ka Seng ka pynpaw ruh ïa ka jingsngewsih namar ka jingbym patiaw ka Sorkar Jylla halor ki dorkhas ba la pynsngew na ka por sha ka por.
Sei ka NPP da u Bah Erwin ban aireng na Shillong North
Shillong, Ïaiong 11: Ka National Peoples Party (NPP) kala pynbna ïa ka kyrteng jong u Bah Erwin K Syiem Sutnga, Advocate kum u kyrtong ka Party ban aireng ha ka elekshon MLA-2018 na Shillong North Constituency pyrshah ïa ka Myntri ka koit ka khïah Kong Roshan Warjri.
    Ka NPP kala thaw ruh ïa ka Organising Committee jong ka 17 Shillong North hynnin ka sn gi ha ka jingïalang bala pynlong hapoh ka Ïingsah u Bah Erwin ha Umsohsun.
    Kane ka jingïalang hadien ba shong bishar bha ïa ka jinglong jingman jong ka saiñ hima sima ha Jylla, kala rai ba ka NPP ka dei ban pynieng kyrtong na Shillong North ha kaba ka kyrteng u Bah Erwin kala mih kum ka jingtyrwa ïa kaba la mynjur ba un long u kyrtong ha ka elekshon MLA-2018.
    Kane ka jingïalang kala shim ïa ka rai ban thaw shuwa ïa ka Adhoc Committee ba kynthup ïa u Bah Shaiphar Rani kum u Chair man, Bah Gordon Kharshandi Vice Chairman ka Northern Sector bad Mohan Lilani Vice Chairman ka Southern Sector, Bah Andrew Donald Marwein kum u Secretary, Bah Robinson Kharkongor Chief Organisation Coordinator, Bah Sharailang Mawlieh Chief Organiser I/c Northern Sector, u Jiren B Marak Chief Organiser I/c Southern Sector bad ka Depika Deb kum ka Treasurer.
    Ka Adhoc Committee jong ka Youth Wing ka kynthup ïa u Terral Marwein Chief Organiser, Royalstar Tymthai Publicity Secy, Patrick Diengdoh bad Bankynsai Lyngkhoi kum ki Asst Publicity Secy bad i Chief Organisers I/c Womens Wing i dei i Kong Aidalin L Lyngkhoi. Nalor kane la jied ruh ïa ki Joint Secy haduh 12 ngut bad 14 ngut ki Executive Member ki ba mihkhmat na ki 39 tylli ki Polling Station.
Leit kai pyngngad u MP ka Tura ha Shnongpdeng
Shillong, ïaiong, 11: U Conrad K. Sangma, MP ka Tura ha ka 7 tarik mynta u bnai u la hiar leit shangkai pyngngad sha Shnong Pdeng kaba long kawei na ki jaka jngohkai pyrthei ba pawnam ha ka thaiñ Riwar.
    Ïa u Conrad la synran lang da u Dr. W.R Kharlukhi, State President ka Nationalist People’s Party (NPP), u Bah Octamewot Lamin, President ka District ha ryngkat ki nongïalam ka Amlarem Block kynthup ruh ïa u Ma Bnai Syngkrem, Rangbah Shnong ka Shnong Pdeng bad kynthup ki dkhot ka Dorbar Shnong.
    U Conrad ha kane ka sngi u la leit jngoh ruh ïa ki jaka ïalehkai, Scuba Diviing, Ziplinging bad Clip Jumping kiba don ha kane ka jaka jngoikai pyrthei da kaba ïasyllok bad ïaphylliew jingmut bad ki nongïalam shnong khnang ban kyntiew shuh shuh ïa ka jingitynnat jong kane ka jaka jngohkai pyrthei bapawnam ha ka jylla.
    Ha kajuh ka por u la kular ban ai ka jingïatreilang bad ki bor shnong ha ki khep ba donkam bad kyntu ruh ruh ban ïatreilang ban wanrah ïa ka jingkhuid jingsuba hapoh ka shnong ka thaw ban ai jingïada kaba paka na ka bynta ka jingshngaiñ ïa ki nongjngohkai pyrthei. Ha kane ka sngi, u Conrad u la noh synniang nalade sha ka pla tyngka jong ka Dorbar Shnong.

Shillong, ïaiong, 11: Ka Joint Action Committee on Social Organisation kaba long ka shatri jong ki saw tylli ki sengbhalnag ba kynthup ïa ka CSWO, PPM, HYM, RBPM, ki la kyntait ba kim shym la kdew kti ne kynnoh eiei pyrshah ïa ka KSU ne RBYF ba ki donkti ban shim pisa na ka Bharat Petroleum Corporation Limited (BPCL).

Buddien u Bah Ardent ban pynbha surok Laitkor-Laitlyngkot
Shillong, Ïaïong 11: U MLA jong ka Nongkrem, u Bah Ardent Basaiawmoit, u la leit ïakynduh ïa u Myntri Rangbah ka jylla, u Dr. Mukul Sangma ban buddien halor ka jingpynbha ïa ka surok na Laitkor- Pomlakrai sha Laitlyngkot, kaba long ka surok kaba la sniew bad pynshitom ïa ka leit ka wan ki paidbah, khamtam eh ba kane ka thaiñ kadei kaba bun ki briew ki im ha ka rep ka riang.
    Ha kane ka jingïakynduh u Bah Ardent u la kyntu ïa u Myntri Rangbah ban pynsted noh ïa ka jingpynbha ïa kane ka surok, la kumno kumno ban sdang noh ïa ka kam shuwa ka jingwan u slap ka lyiur. Na ka liang u Myntri Rangbah, u la ïathuh ba ka sorkar lyngba ka tnad PWD, ka la pynkhreh ban pynbha noh ïa kane ka surok bad ka dang sah satang ban pynbiang ïa ki katto katne ki jingdonkam.
    Lah ban kdew hangne ba u Bah Ardent u la rah ruh ïa kane ka kam ha ka dorbar tyngka ba dang shu dep, ha kaba u la dawa na ka sorkar ban pynbha ïa kane ka surok, kaba long ka surok kaba donkam bha jong ki briew ka thaiñ bad kumjuh ruh kaba ju pyndonkam ki briew ba leit sha Laitlyngkot, Pynursla shaduh Dawki. Ha katei ka dorbar, u Dr. Mukul u la kular ban pynbha noh ïa kane ka surok, khamtam eh ïa ki katto katne ki jaka kiba la sniew palat.

Shillong, ïaïong 11: Ka lyer elekshon ha jylla ka la sdang ban beh suki suki, ha kaba ki Seng Saiñhima, ki la nang pynkhreh ban wad ïa ki kyrtong kiba biang ban mih madan ha kane ka lympung synshar khadar.
    Uwei na kine ki kyrtong uba lah ban mih ha kane ka elekshon 2018, udei u Samla rangbah Shemborlang Rynjah uba lah ban mih madan na Pynursla pyrshah ïa u Bah Prestone Tynsong, MLA ka Seng Congress uba long ruh u Myntri ka sorkar jylla.

ka Seng. Dei ha ka por ba u don ha KJWA, ba u Bah Shembor, u la pyllut por ha kaba ïarap ïa ki samla ha kaba wad kam wad jam lyngba ki Competitive Exam. U la ïadon bynta ruh ha kaba btin lynti ïa ki samla kumno ba kin nang kiew shaphrang ha ki jingpule jong ki sha ki kyrdan kiba kham sha jrong.
    Nalor kine jingbtin lynti ïa ki samla, u Bah Shem, u la ju ïadon bynta ruh ban ai jingkren bad ai paper ha ki Seminar kiba ïadei bad ka ïap ka im jong ka jaidbynriew, nangta ula ïadon bynta ruh ban kdew lynti ïa ki jingtreikam ka sorkar ban wanrah ïa ki Policy bad ki aiñ ban ïada bad pynkhlaiñ ïa ka jaidbynriew. Nalor kane une u rangbah u don ruh u khulom uba nep ha kaba u la ju noh synñianglyngba ki article sha ki kot khubor, magazine bad kikot kiba long ki symboh pyrkhat kiba kordor shisha.

U Bah Shemborlang udei na ka shnong Lyngkyrdem bad u shongkha ha Laitlyngkot. Mynta u bat kum u Joint Secretary ka HSPDP bad la sngewthuh ba u lah ban pan ticket na kane ka Seng.

Shillong. Ïaiong 11: Ki Pulit ka East Khasi Hills kila hïar hynne ka sngi sha thaiñ Diengpasoh ban tohkit ïa ka jingïap jong kawei ka Longkmie hala ka jong ka Ïingsah bad bala tep da ki bahaïing hasem khlem da pyntip sha ka Aiñ.
    Ki Pulit ki ïathuh ba hynnin ka sngi kila ïoh khubor ba kawei ka Longkmie kala dkhat jubor ïala ka jingim hala ka jong ka ïingsah bad ki bahaïing pat kila tep noh ïa ka met jong ka. Ki ong ba ki bahaïing kila lap ïa ka metïap hynnin ka sngi bad la suba jur ba kane ka longkmie kala ïap kumba ar sngi eiei.
    Hynrei ha ka jingtohkit, u Medical Officer ka Diengpasoh PHC ula ïathuh ba kane ka Longkmie kala ju wan teng sha u ban phah pynhap khun.
    Halor kane ka jingshem, ki Pulit kila register case bad ka jingtohkit mynta kala ïaid shakhmat. Ki Pulit ki lah ruh ban khlong bïang ïa ka metïap na ka bynta ban leh ïa ka post mortem ïoh don kano kano ka daw halor ka jingïap jong ka.
