Hapdeng ka jingphuh jingphieng la kut noh ïa ka Shad Suk Mynsiem ba 3 sngi
Poi haduh 481 ngut ki Kynthei bad 547 ngut ki Shynrang
11 April, 2017
Shilong, Ïaiong 10: Ka Shad Suk Mynsiem kaba 106, kaba dei ka shad ban ainguh aidem ïa U Blei Trai Kynrad, u nongbuh u nongthaw ka Seng Khasi Kmie, Mawkhar Shillong kaba la long ha ki lai sngi lynter ka la poi noh sha kaba kut mynta ka sngi ha lympung Weiking, Jaïaw hapdeng ka jingphuh jingphieng bha ryngkat ka jingai lad ka mariang.

    Ka jingwan ïashim bynta jong ki nongshad ka long ba ki kynthei ki nongshad baroh ki long haduh 481 ngut bad ki Shynrang ki long 547 ngut ba kynthup ïa uwei u riew rangbah ba la don 88 snem ka rta u bah Belin Thabah ba dei napoh ka shnong Umsaw, Sohïong bad haba kheiñ kyllum ki nongshad baroh ki long 1028.

    Ki riew pawkhmat ba la poi ban sakhi ïa kane ka shad ki kynthup naduh u Lat ka jylla u Banwarilal Purohit, u Chief Justice ka Meghalaya High Court u Dinesh Maheshwari, ki nongmih khmat paidbah ba kynthup ïa I Kong Roshan Warjri myntri ka sorkar jylla ba dei khmih ïa ka tnat ka koit ka khiah, ki MLA ba kynthup ïa u bah A.L Hek, Bah Jemino Mawthoh, ryngkat ki President bad Secretary jong ki tnat ka Seng Khasi bad ki nongïalam ka Seiñ Raij, ïa kaba la nang pyniphuh iphieng shuh shuh da ka jinghiar ban sakhi da u paid ba wan khmih kai.

    Hadien ba la kut jong ka jingshad la ïoh pat ïa ka dwai ka phirat kaba la ai da u Rgh Romeo Mawrie uba la shim syndon ïa ka bynta ban pynhap ïa ka lama jong ka Seng Khasi.

    Na lympung Weiking la pynlong ïa ka jingïaid kjat ban wanphai sha ïing seng ha Mawkhar Shillong, ha kaba u Rgh Bantei S. Rumnong, President, ka Seng Khasi, Kmie, u la ai khublei ïa la ki para kur ki parakha, najan bad na jngai bad ïa ki nongshad kynthei bad shynrang kiba la wan ban pynphuh pynphieng ïa kane ka shad mynta ka snem.

    Haba ïakren bad u Mawphor u rangbah Belin Thabah u ong ba u long u briew uba sngewtynnad ban ïa shim bynta ha kum kine shad ki kmen, kaba bunsien u la juh mih lympung ban shad ha ki lympung ba dei jong ka shnong.

    “Ha ka por ba nga dang samla, nga la juh wan teng ba ngan shad ha kane ka Shad Suk Mynsiem” la ong u rangbah Belin katba u dang shongjah thait ïalade shipor.

    Kum ka dak ka jingsngew burom ïa kane ka jingwan ban ïashim bynta ïa u rangbah Belin Thabah la pynithuh syndon ïa u hakhmat u Lat ka jylla u Banwarilal Purohit uba la kitbok kit rwiang ïa u ba un nang ioh ïa ka met ka phad ba koit ba khiah bad wan ïashim bynta sha kane ka shad ka kmen.
Kob ka UDP ban lehbha ha u 2018 ba beh ka lyer pyrshah Congress ha Jylla
11 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong 10: Ka United Democratic Party (UDP) hynne ka sngi kala kam ba ka don ka lad ïa ka Party ban tam shakhmat ha u 2018 namar ka jingbeh jong ka lyer pyrshah Congress haba batai lypa ruh ba ka lawei ba dum kan ap ïa ka BJP ha Jylla.

    “Ngi kyrmen skhem ba ka UDP kum ka seng riewlum ba heh duh ha Jylla, kan tam shakhmat ha ka elekshon MLA 2018 namar ka jing beh jong ka lyer pyrshah Congress ha Jylla” ong u Dr Jemino Mawthoh, General Secretary ka UDP hynne ka sngi.

    Haba pyntip ba ka UDP kala pynkhreh shaid shaid na ka bynta ka elekshon MLA, u Dr Jemino ula ong ba ka Party kala trei shitom ha kaban pynthikna ba kan dup poi sha ka thong.

    Ka UDP kan sa pynlong ïa bun tylli ki jingïalang hapoh ka Jylla ka ban sdang naduh ka 11 tarik Ïaiong bad kine ki jingïalang kin long ha Songsak, Rongjeng bad Tura ha ka 11 tarik bad 12 tarik Ïaiong bad ha Khliehriat, East Jaiñtia Hills ha ka 15 tarik Ïaiong. Kat kum ka jingong jong u, ka UDP ka don jingkyrmen bha ban ïoh khur ïa ka jingjop ha Ri-lum Jaiñtia.

    Hadien kine, ka UDP kan sa pynlong ïa ka jingïalang Central Executive Committee ha ka 17 tarik Ïaiong, ka ban ïakren halor ki kam ba ïadei bad ka elekshon MLA.

    Ha kawei pat ka liang, une u General Secretary ula ong ba ka Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) kan dang hap ban ïaid ïa ka lynti kaba jngai bha hangne ha Jylla Meghalaya.

    “Ngim don eiei ban ong halor ki jingkren u Myntri Rangbah Duh ka Ri ba ïadei bad ka roi ka par. Hynrei kaei kaba jia ha ka Ri baroh kawei khamtam halor ki kam ba ktah ïa ka Niam kum ka jingkhang ot doh masi, nga sngew kan ktah jur bha ïa ka BJP hapoh ka Jylla” ong u Dr Jemino haba bynrap “Kiei kiba jia ha ka Ri kin ktah jur bha ïa ka BJP hangne ha Meghalaya bad kumjuh ruh ha kiwei ki Jylla ka thaiñ Shatei Lam Mihngi kum ka Mizoram bad Nagaland”.

    Lah ban kdew hangne, ka UDP ka dei kawei na ki seng riewlum ka Jylla kaba iatreilang bad ka BJP hapoh ka kynhun NEDA.

    U Dr Jemino ula pynpaw ba ka UDP ka dang long kaba kloi ban iatreilang bad kino kino ki Party kiba ïasngewthuh jingmut. U ong “Lada ki Party ki kloi ban iatreilang kan bha eh hynrei lada kim trei, ngi hi ngin ïaid beit hala ka jong ka lynti”.

    Haba kylli halor ka Seng saiñ Pyrthei ba thymmai ka Peoples Democratic Front (PDF), une u Nongïalam ka UDP ula pynpaw ïa ka jingartatien ba ki paidbah kin pdiang.

    “Ka PDF ka lah ban tuh ïa bun bah ka Vote jong ka Congress hynrei ngam tharai ba kan don ka jingkylla ha ka Vote jong ka UDP” ula ong.

    Ha kajuh ka por, une u Nongïalam ka UDP ula pyntip ba arngut ki MDC barim na Ri-lum Jaiñtia ba kynthup ïa u Bah Kor Syngkli bad Bah Welcome Dkhar, kila mynjur ban iatreilang ha kaban pynthikna ba ka Party kan lah ban leh bha ha Ri-Lum Jaiñtia ha u snem 2018. Ula kyntu ruh ïa ki Nongkyrshan ba kin iawan lang sha ka jingïalang ban long ha Khliehriat West Community Hall ha ka 15 tarik, ïa kaban sa don lang ki Nongïalam ka Seng Kmie bad na ka District.

Jirang, Ïaïong 10: Shi snem shuwa ka elekshon MLA, ka Seng NPP na Jirang ka la ïoh ïa ka jingkyrshan kaba donkam shisha bad kata ka long haba arngut ki MLA barim kane ka Constituency, ki la pynpaw ba kin kyrshan ia ka kyrtong ka seng ha kane ka elekshon.

    Katkum ka khubor ba la phah da ka Seng, la ïathuh ba kine ki arngut ki MLA barim ki long u Rev. Gerson Lyngdoh bad u Bah Snowmik Kalwing. Kine ki arngut ki rangbah ki la ïadon lang ha ka jingïalang ba la pynlong da ka Seng NPP ha Umsong mynsngi Saitjaiñ.             Ïa kane ka jingïalang la pyllong kum shi bynta ban pynkhreh ïa ka elekshon sha ka Ingdorbar Thawaiñ ha u snem 2018. Ia kane ka jingïalang la pyllong da ka seng National People’s Party, Ri Bhoi District Committee. Ha kane ka jingïalang, la wan ban ïashim bynta bad pynshit pynshngaiñ da ki hajar ngut ki nongkyrshan jong ka seng na kylleng ki shnong ki ba hap hapoh u pud u sam jong ka Jirang Constituency.

    Ïa ka jingialang la pyniaid da u Bah Sranly Wahlang, u ba long ruh ha ka juh ka por u Adhoc Secretary jong ka seng na ka Western Circle jong ka Constituency. La iadon ryngkat ruh u National President ka Party, u Conrad K. Sangma, u ba long ruh u MP jong ka Lok Sabha na Tura Parliamentary Constituency , nangta u Dr. Charles Reuben Lyngdoh, General Secretary ka Party, State Unit bad u Bah Bimol Saikia, uwei na ki riew rangbah ba pawkhmat na Byrnihat. Ha kane ka jingialang la ioh jingkren na kiba bun ki riew rangbah u Bah Sevenman Roy Thangkhiew bad u Bah Wesley Doloi, ki President jong ki Unit bapher bapher bad na ki Mahila Unit jong ka party. Uwei na ki riew rangbah ka thain, u Bah Snowmik Kalwing, uba long ruh u MLA barim haba ai jingkren u la pynpaw ia ka jingkyrshan ba pura ia ka seng bad u khmihlynti ba hapoh ka jingialam jong ka seng NPP u don ka jingkyrmen ba kan don ka jingkylla ha kiba bun ki liang hapoh ka jylla baroh kawei. Ha kane ka jingialang, u Secretary jong ka party i/c Ri Bhoi u la pynskhem ia u Bah Wesley Doloi kum u President jong ka Party Western Circle bad ia u Bah Sranly Wahlang kum U Secretary jong ka Western Circle. Ha kane ka jingialang la ioh ruh ban pynskhem ia ki nongialam jong ki primary unit jong ka party na Nongladew, Umsong, Umrit, Wahsynon (Jirang), Nongbirthem, Umsohbar, Umtasen, Mawdem, Upper Bagan, Dihal Bagan, Kushwa, Harlibagan bad kiba bun ki unit jong ka party da u National President jong ka party.

    Haba kren ha kane ka jingialang, I Kong Wandashisha Wahlang, iwei na ki samla ba pawkhmat jong ka thain Jirang I la pynpaw ia ka jingthmu jong I ban ia aireng ha kane ka Elekshon ka ban wan. I la ong ruh ba ka jingthmu jong I ka long ban shakri ia la ka dong ka thain ka ba la shah iehnoh khunswet bad kaba dang sahdien ha baroh ki liang. I la ong ruh ba wat hadien ki phew snem ba ngi la ioh la ka jong ka jylla, ka thain Jirang baroh kawei kam pat lah ban ia kot kyrdan bad kiwei pat ki dong ki thain jong ka Jylla. Kane ka pynpaw shai ia ka jingbym kitkhia jong ki nongmihkhmat bad ki nongialam jong ka thain. I la pynpaw ruh ia ka jingbynniaw ia kane ka jingsahdien jong ka dong bad ka thain bad I la banjur ba kane ka dei ka por kaba biang eh ban wanrah ia ki jingkylla na ka bynta ka roi ka par. Namarkata I la iawer ia ki riew rangbah, ki longkmie bad khamtam eh ia ki samla ba kin iamih shakhmat ban saindur thymmai ia ka dong ka thain, ban kyntiew ia ka roi kapar, ka ioh ka kot, bad ka longbriew manbriew ha ka imlang sahlang hi baroh kawei. I la kyrpad ruh ia ia baroh ki nongshnong shnong ka thain ba ngin kyndit bynriew bad pyrkhat thymmai noh na ka bynta ka lawei ba phyrnai jong ki longdien khnang ba ngin ia kiew shaphrang ha baroh ki liang.

    U MP ka Tura sha Lok Sabha, u Conrad K. Sangma habakrenkane ka jingialang u la ai khublei iaki nongialamjong ka party ha RiBhoi District kiba la trei shitom ban pynkhlain ia ka party. U la iaroh ruh ia ki rangbah jong ka Jirang Constituency kiba la wan shakhmat ban kyrshan ia ka party ha kane ka kynti kaba mynta. U la iathuhruh ba kum ka party ki don ia ka jingkyrmen ban lehbha ha kane ka Elekson ka ban wan na ka bynta ban wanrah iaki jingkylla ha ka Jyllahi barohkawei. U la kynthoh ia ka jingbymkitkhlieh bad jingbymshimkhia jong unongmihkhmatka thain ban wanrah iaki kampynroi ha kane ka thain. U la pynpaw ruh ba kum kinongmihkhmat ymdei ban don kano kano ka jingniew shilliang iaki paidbah hynrei ka kamram jong uNongmihkhmat ka long ban shakriiakipaidbahymbakipaidbah kin shakri ia U. U la kynthoh ruh ia ka jingbymler kam jong kane ka sorkar ba mynta hapoh ka jingialam U Dr. Mukul Sangma, kaba la ka ktah shi katdei eh iaki nongshongshnong hapoh ka jylla. U la ongruh ba kane Ka Sorkar ka dei kaSorkar ka bym lerkam tam ha ka histori jong ka Jylla.

    Ha kaba khadduh eh u la kyrpad iaki paidbah ha Jirang constituency ba kin aiia ka jingkyrshanba puraia ka Party ha kane ka kynti. U la kular ruhbalada ka party ka poi sha ka thong, na ka liang ka jongu un pyrshang ban iarap kyntiew ia ka roi ka par jong kane ka thain. U National President jong ka party u la pynpawbana ka liangjong u, u la kular ban aii a ka jingkyrshan bapura ia I Kong WandashishaWahlang ha kane ka kynti kaba mynta bad kyrmen ruh ban in poi sha ka thong jong ka jingjop.

11 April, 2017
Shillong, ïaiong 10: U Moderator ka Presbyterian Church of India u Rev Ladawngliana haba kren kum u kongsan ha ka jingialang ban ai khublei khatduh (Valedictory service) ia ki samla pule Bachelor of Divinity (B.D) ka John Roberts Theological Seminary, Mawklot Shillong ula buh iaka jingkylli kaba khia da kaba u ong, "Haei nga don bad nga dei u ei? Ha kaba ula ong ba kane kam dei tang iaki hynrei wat ia ki nongialam Balang bad kumjuh ruh iaki khristan.

    Ula ong ba ka jingbuh ia katei ka jingkylli ka dei hadien ba kum u nongialam Balang ne wat kiwei ruh hadien ka jingbishar bniah ia ka jinglong jingman ka imlang ka sahlang la iohi ba kam i don shuh ka jingkyrmen, lada phai sha ka jingjot jingpra ki iing ki sem, ki shnong ki thaw, da kaba u ong, "Ki iing ki sem ki jot ki pra namar ba kam don shuh ka jingieid hapdeng jongki bad ruh ba kam don ka jingniewkor ia kiwei, bad kane ka pyni shai kdar ba kum ki briew ngi pynjot bad pynsepei iala ka jingim tang na ka bynta kiei kiei ki bym don jingmyntoi."

    Ka jingkylli ba mano ban leit shaki, kumta ula kyntu ia ki samla pule kiba la dep pule bad kiba dang pule hapoh kane ka shlem jinghikai ban shakri ha ka kam U Kynrad, ula ong ba kin long ka sakhi sha kiwei lyngba ka jingim ha ka doh bad khamtam ha ka jingim ba kynja mynsiem khnang ban wanrah biang ka jingkyrmen bad jingsuk ia ka imlang ka sahlang bad ka ri baroh kawei, kumba kila ioh iaki jinghikai bad jingtip lyngba kane ka jaka pule, khnang ba kin long kum kita ki shakri kiba pyndonkam ia ka sap (talent) kaba u Kynrad u ai, ym ba kin long kum u shakri uba buhrieh iala ka jong ka sap.

"Ngi donkam ka jingiatreilang ban sopspaiñ sa shisien ia ka imlang sahlang kaba la duh iaka jingkyrmen lyngba ka jingling jingim kaba bha, ka jingim kaba myntoi sha kiwei bad ba ngin long ka khubor kaba bha," ong u Rev Ladawngliana da kaba bynrap, ba kum ki samla pule BD kila ioh shibun ki jingmyntoi ha ka liang ka jingling ba shimet jongki (jingling mynsiem) ne wat ha kaba iadei bad kiwei ki bynta.

Nalor kane ula kynthoh ruh ba kum ki shlem ai jinghikai ban shakri iaka kam u kynrad ki duna bha ban sei shisha kita ki shakri ki ban don iaka jingling mynsiem, ka jinglong kaba bha bad ka jingmyntoi sha kiwei, namar ka imlang ka sahlang ka donkam ia ki ba kin long ka jingkylla.

Ha kane ka sngi na ka liang u President ka Governing Body ka JRTS u Rev T.Mukhim ula ai ia ki Certificate sha ki 40 ngut ki samla kynthei bad shynrang kiba la dep ban pule iaka Bachelor of Divinity (B.D) bad ruh sha ki ba puyndep iaka Lay Leadership. Katba na ka liang u Tbn.T.L Rapmai ula buh ka jingduwai kaba kyrpang na ka bynta kitei ki samla ba kin nang kiew shaphrang ha kaba ban ai ka jingshakri ia ka kam U Kynrad.

    Ha kane ka sngi ka kong L.Lyngdoh Ex-Secretary Jingiaseng Kynthei KJP Assembly kala pyllait paidbah ruh iaka Seminary Magazine. Nalor kitei ki prokram la pyniphuh iphieng lyngba ka jingrwai kaba kyrpang na ki samla pule B.D.

    Ha kane ka sngi la iadon ryngkatlang ki nongialam ba hakhlieh ka PCI, ki Pastor ka KJP Assembly, KJP Synod Mihngi, KJP Synod Sepngi, ki Nonghikai ka JRTS, ki kmie ki kpa, kiba ha iing hasem jong ki samla ba pyndep iaka jingpule B.D, kibad kiwei kiwei.

    La mih ruh ka jingkynnoh ba ïa ka thup kyrteng ba ki Rangbah Shnong ki phah, ka Block kam pdiang satia hynrei ka la aiti bad phah jied beit ha ki briew jong u MLA.

    Da kaba kynthoh ïa ka rukom treikam jong ka Block, u Bah Marconi u ïathuh ruh ba watla ki Rangbah Shnong ki la phah ïa ka kyrteng sha ka Block Ranikor hynrei na ka liang katei ka ophis pat ka aiti kylla ha ki nongïalam jong utei u MLA ban leit ai ïa ki jingïarap.

    Ki nongïalam ka seng ki la kynthoh ruh ïa ka rukom treikam jong ka Block, kaba khlem lah satia ban ai jingkheiñ ïa ka jingdon ki shnong kiba shah ktah ha katei ka jinglynshop jong ka mariang.

    “Na ka liang ki ophisar ka Block ki dei ban leit hi, ym ban shu phah kylla ha ki briew jong u MLA,” u la ong da kaba bynrap ba wat ha Block ruh ka don ka jingleh shilliang ïa ki nongïoh jingïarap.

    Halor katei ka rukom treikam, ka KSU ka la byrngem ruh ban leh syndon da kaba tyngeh ïa ka ophis jong ka Ranikor Block bad ruh ïa kitei ki nongïalam jong u MLA kiba la nud ban leh politik ïa ka kam ïap kam im jong ki nongshong shnong ka thaiñ.

    Ki nongïalam ka Seng ki ïathuh ruh ba don ki shnong kiba watla ka jingjulor ka poi sha ka 50 tylli hynrei la shu jied ban ai jingïarap tang 2-3 tylli ei ei.

    La ïathuh ruh ba kito kiba ïoh jingïarap don kiba ïoh kawei ka borti, kawei ka mok, u khaw ar shang bad don ruh kiba ïoh da ki tyrpar.

    Na ka liang u Truewell Lyngdoh, general secretary ka KSU South West Khasi Hills, u la ong ba ka long kaba bynñiaw ban ïohi ïa ka jingtuklar jong ki briew u MLA haba ïadei bad ka jingsam ïa ki lad jingïarap sha kitei ki lanot.

    “Ha ka jingshisha u BDO u la dei ban leh hi haba ïadei bad ka jingsam ïa ki jingïarap. Kum u ophisar um dei satia ban sngap ïa ki briew jong u MLA khamtam haba ki Rangbah Shnong ki wanrah hi ïa ka thup kyrteng jong kito ki lanot,” u la ong.    

    La kynnoh ruh ba wat haba ki nongïalam ka Seng ki leit ban wad jingtip na ka ophis jong ka Block, la phah pynban ïa ki ban ïa kynduh ïa kitei ki briew jong u MLA.

    Ha kajuh ka por ka Seng ka la pynbna ruh ban khang lut ïa ki tamasa leh kmen ha ka District kynthup naduh ki beach festival bad kiwei kiwei. “Ngi la rai ban khang lut ïa ki tamasa lehkmen ha ka distrik namar ka sorkar ha kum kitei ki tamasa ka pynlut da ki lak bad klur hynrei na ka bynta ki lanot shah lynshop mariang pat kam don pisa,” ong kitei ki nongïalam ka Seng.

Hap husiar ka bam tit, bun ki bym ithuh ïa u tit buid.....
11 April, 2017
Ka jingduh ei ki mynsiem briew tang na kaba bam ïa u tit buid kam dei shuh ka jingjia kaba thymmai ha kane ka jylla namar la ju ïohi man la u snem khamtam ha kine ki aiom sdang Lyiur. Dang ha u snem ba la dep ruh kawei ka longiing hajan Mawsynram ka la duh bun tylli ki mynsiem briew tang na katei kajuh ka daw, kata ba ki bam ïa u tit buid.

    Ka jingbun kiba ïap na kaba bam tit buid ka la dei ban pynkyndit bynriew ïa ngi ki paidbah ba sngewtynnad bha ban bam tip ba donkam ban da husiar haba leit kheit tit na ki khlaw, ïoh lehse watla kim dei ki tit ba bud hynrei ïoh ki dei pynban ki tip ba par ki bseiñ ne ki kynja khñiang ba long bih. Watla katei ka jingjia ba ïap na kaba bam tit buid la ju ïoh sngew na kapor sha ka por, hynrei haduh mynta ngim pat ïoh ïa ki lad jingtip ba bniah na ki skul bah ne na ki doktor ki ban ïa noh synñiang ne pynshai kham bniah halor katei ka phang, kumno ban ai jingsumar ban lait na ka jingmynsaw ne khamtam eh na ka sni jong ka jingïap.

    Kum ka jingtip, ha ba don mano mano ba ïoh bam tit buit, ngi ju ong ba ki dei ki “tit biah bsein” don ruh ki ba ong ba ha ka por ba dang shu slap bad mih tit ym pat long ban bam tit nyngkong namar u dang jaboh bad u slap um pat sait ïa ki bih ki ba lah ban don ha u tit. Kine ki long tang ki jing pyrshang jong ki riew tymmen ban pyrshang ban wad ïa ka daw bad ban pynhun ïa ka jing bym tip bniah jong ka jing ngat bih na u tit, hynrei ngim pat lah ban pynshisha la kine ki long ki ba dei ne ki ba lait.

    Ka ju long ha ka jinglong briew jongngi bangin pyrshang ban batai klumar ïa ki daw ba ngim lah shemphang, kum ka jing kynnoh aibih, men-ai-ksuid, menshohnoh bad kiwei kiwei. Hynrei haduh mynta mynne ym ju lah ban pynshisha la kine kidei ne em, wat ki pulit ki ba la kem ïa ki ba shah kynnoh ruh kim pat ju lah pynshisha ka shu shong beit tang ha ka jingring dur, bad jing mut dur jong ngi ka ba la pynhiar pateng ha ka jingmut jingpyrkhat jong ngi lyngba ki jing ïathuh khana pateng la pateng naduh dang lung ka jabieng bad ka ba pynlong ba kan shong tynrai ha pyrkhat pyrdaiñ.

    Ban pynshai paidbah kam long satia kaba suk khamtam haba baroh ki paidbah ka jylla kidei kiba bam tit. Kumta, bun ruh kin ym kheit ïa u tit phylla u ba ngim pat ju bam mynno mynno ruh bad ngin kiar na kum kine bad ban kheit tang kito ki ba ngi la tip bad tikna ba kidei kiba la ju kheit bad ju bam pateng la pateng.

    Ha kiba bun ki nongkyndong, ki kmie ki kpa ne ba la san ki ju batai thik pa thik ïa ka jingïapher hapdeng u tit bam bad u tit buid, da kaba pyni ba ka don ka jingïapher baklybak naduh ka dur jong u, ka rong bad ka jingheh, hynrei la katta ruh bun kiba dang bakla, tangba ka shong pat ha kito kiba la san ban peit bniah ynda la rah sha iing ban jied bha khnang ban ym shet lang ïa kitei ki tit ki bym long bam.

    Na ka liang ka sorkar ruh ka la dei ban pynmih da ki kynja jingpynbna ban kyntu ïa ki paidbah ba kidei ban peitngor bad husiar bha haba ki bam ïa ki tit khnang ba kin lait na ki jingjia kiba sngewsih kiba lah ban shim wat ïa ka jingim jong ki khun, kurim ne ki baieit ba thoiñ jong ki.

    Kawei pat ka phang ka long ba ka tnad ba peit ïa ka bam ka dih ba kadei ban da peitngor bad pyrkhing wat ïa ka jingdie ïa ki tit ha iew, ban khanglad ïoh ka don kano kano ka jingpyrshang wat ban die ïa ki tit bym long bam bad ba ïoh ki mynsiem ba lui lui ki shu kylla long ki langkñia.
“Halor Ka ‘Wah Umkhrah”
I. R. Dkhar
11 April, 2017
     Halor ka Kot kaba I Kong Esther Syiem, Nonghikai NEHU ba la thoh halor ka Wahumkhrah kaba la ai kyrteng, ‘Memoir in Water Speaks the Wah Umkhrah’, ba la mih ha U Nongsaiñ Hima Tarik 25 Rymphang, 2017, ha kaba la ong ruh ba kane ka kot ka don khyndai tylli ki khana lyngkot kiba la pynshong nongrim halor ka jingjot jingpra jong ka Wahumkhrah bad ka jingpynpaw ruh jong ka jingsngew jong ki briew kiba sah marsyndah jong kane ka wah, nga sngew ban ai burom bad jingïaroh ïa itei ki Kong Syiem iba la pynmih ïa katei ka kot, bad ruh ban pynpaw ei ei ha kaba ïadei bad ka Wahumkhrah. La ong ruh ha katei ka Khubor ba la pyllait ruh ïa ka Kot Poitri kaba kyrteng, ‘Many Sides of Many Stories’ ba la thoh da I Kong Syiem ha ka workshop kaba ar sngi ha NEHU.

Wat lada ngim ïohi bad tip aïu la thoh ha katei ka Kot, hynrei la sngewthuh, kumba la paw ha katei ka Kotkhubor, ba ka thoh shaphang ka jingjaboh ka Wahumkhrah mynta, ym kumba long mynshuwa. Kane ka wah ka la kylla long kum ka nala, ka dei namar ka jingleh khlemakor da kaba bret, theh bad pyntuid jaboh jabaiñ ki briew, ym tang kiba shong ba sah hajan katei ka wah, hynrei naduh ka tyllong jong ka na Nongthymmai, na Umpling, Nongrah, Pynthorumkhrah, Demseiñïong, Nongmynsong ter ter shaduh Mawlai ba la pynlong ïa ka Wahumkhrah kumba ka long mynta. Phim lah leh eiei shuh ha kane ka por, namar la bun tang ki ïing ki sem, khamtam kiba la shu shna be aiñ ne ym tip ki ïoh permission ne kim ïoh, kiba shna harud wahumkhrah. Ha ka jingshisha, la dei ban leh ei ei naduh mynshuwa shuwa ban ai permission ïa ki briew ban shna ïing. Ngi la pynpaw lyngba ki Kotkhubor ïa ka jingdonkam ban pynlong ïa ka jyngai-jingtip, jinghikai bad jingpynshai paidbah ne ka awareness programme ha sawdong jong kane ka wah naduh kitei shnong kiba ker tawiar ïa katei ka Wahumkhrah. Hynrei ym ïohi ba la don kum kata. Lada don ruh, tengkhat lano eh, kata ruh naduh ki por mynshuwa. Ym don ka jingpynkynmaw bad jinghikai man ka por. Ka jingpynjaboh ïa ka Wahumkhrah ka sdang naduh ka tyllong jong ka hi da ki briew kiba shong basah bad kiba pyntuid ïa ki jakhlia jakhlaid na ïing na sem jong ki bad ka jingbret pathar jong ki briew ïa ki jaboh jabaiñ hapoh kane ka wah. Ngim lah leh ei ei shuh, katkum ka jingïohi jong nga, namar ki briew kim kheiñ kor ïa ka jinglehkhuid, ïa ka jingmana, ïa ka jingnang jingstad kaba ki la ïoh halor ka jingkoit jingkhiah bad ka jingïatiplem jong ki. Haduh mynta, ngi ïohi ba ki nongshongshnong kim salia ban bret pathar ïa ki ñuit ki ñier, ki kot ki sla, ki plastic, ka eit ka jaboh bad kiwei kiwei ha lynter kane ka wah. Ha ka jaka ba kin pynlang ïa ki ñiut ki ñier, ki jaboh jabaiñ ha ki jaka-jaka ha la ki ïing-ki-ïing ne ki jaka ba la buh bad ai ha ki kali kit ñiut, ki bret pathar pynban ha ki lynti synkien. Ki kmie ki kpa ruh, ngam tip, ikumba kim hikai lane salia ban hikai ne ban sneng ban khraw ïa la ki khun ki kti jong ki ha kaba ïadei bad ka jinglehkhuid ka ban wanrah ïa ka jingkoit jingkhiah ha ki shnong ki thaw bad ka imlang sahlang.

     Kaba donkam mynta, kaba nga kwah ban ai jingmut, ka long ba dei ban pynsngew sha ki shkor jong ki Nongmihkhmat ba kin leh ei ei bad ka Sorkar ban ai ka awareness ha kitei ki shnong ki thaw sawdong jong ka Wahumkhrah. Nangta ban thaw ki lad ki lynti da kaba buh skhim kumno ban pyrkhing ïa ka jingsumar khuid bad ka jingpynkhuid na ka por sha ka por ryngkat bad ki Dorbar Shnong khnang ba kan nym long shuh shuh kaba kham sniew bad kham ma ïa ka Wahumkhrah bad ïa ka jingkoit jingkhiah nangne shakhmat, ym tang ïalade ne la ki jong ki ïing ki sem la jong, lym kumta long lehnohei bad ka shu long tang ka jingkynmaw ïa ka mynnor jong ka Wahumkhrah. Shuh ki don ki NGOs bad ki Seng Treimon Sngewbha, kum ka SSSS, CSWO, KSU, etc. etc. ba ki dei ban pynsngew sha ki bor Sorkar halor katei ka phang.

    Sa kawei kaba nga kwah ban ai jingmut hangne ka long ba namar bym don ka Land Policy, Housing Policy, etc. ki briew ki shna ïing, shna dukan, shna karkhana, etc. lehse beaiñ harud katei ka Wahumkhrah. Nangta ka jingshna ïing ha ki pynthor bad harud ka Wahumkhrah kaba la pynlong pynban ïa ka pynthor – ka jaka rep – da ki ïing ki sem, ki karkhana, etc. Haoid, lah ban ong ba ka jaka ka dei ka jaka shimet, ki die ki thied katba mon, hynrei donkam ban don ka civic sense bad ka aiñ da ka Sorkar ka ban khang na ka bynta ka jingbha jong ka shong ka sah, ka imlang sahlang, ki lum ki wah, ka mariang sawdong sawkun (environment) bad kiwei kiwei ki jingbha jingmiat ïa u khun bynriew. Lada ai lad lut ïa kiei kiei baroh ban leh katba mon, shano ngin ïa poi.
La dep ring bor ding ka sorkar sha ki 13,000 ki shnong bym don bor ding
Shillong, Iaiong 10 : Ka tnad pynmih bor ding ka India ne ka Ministry of Power jong ka sorkar pdeng ka la jam sa uwei u maw mer ha ka jingpynïoh bor ding ïa ki shnong sha ki thaiñ nongkyndong.
    Namar na ki 18,452 tylli ki shnong kiba ym pat ïoh bor ding ka la lah ban ring bor ding mynta 13,000 tylli na ka skhim Deen Dayal Upadhyaya Gram Jyoti Yojana (DDUGJY)
    La buh thong ba ïa ki 4,481 tylli ki shnong ki bym pat ïoh bor ding kin sa ïohi noh ïaka jingshai jongka bor ding elektrik naduh ka 1 tarik Jymmang 2018. Ïa ki jingtip ba kham bniah shaphang kane la buh lut ha ka website bad ïa kine ki jingtip lah ban peit na kino kino ki bynta ka ri.
    Ka jingbuh jingthoh kaba dang shen halor ka jingring bor ding elektrik ka long GARV ha ki Mobile App bad ha ki web portal pat https://garv.gov.in/garv2/dashboard/main. Hangne phin ïohi ïa ka jingmang ban pynbiang bor ding ïa kawei pa kawei ka shnong na ka DDYGJY bad kumno la pyllait pisa ruh sha ki jylla. Kane kan ïarap ïa ki paid nongkyndong ban bud dien ïa ka jingtrei ban pynpoi bor ding sha ki shnong jongki ha ki bynta bapher bapher jongka ri.

Nongstoiñ, Ïaïong 10 : Ha kine ki sngi ki pulit jong ka tnad pynïaid kali ka West Khasi Hills ki la sdang ban pyntrei kam pyrkhing bha ïa ki aiñ na kabynta jong baroh ki nongñiah kali kata naduh ki kali kamai sor,ki Tourist,ki trok,bad ki kali jong ki riew shimet khnang ban lait na kino kono ki jing jia ba sngewsih kum ki aksiden bad kiwei kiwei. Ka jingpyntrei kam ryntih ïa ki aiñ na ka bynta ki nongñiah kali ki long kum ka jingdih duma ha ka por ba dang ñiah kali bad kit ïa ki nongleit nong wan, ka jing kren mobile phone katba dang ñiah kali, ka jingpynpah palat ha pdeng sor bad ha ki jaka ba jan ki skul bad ki jaka ba don paitbah, ka jingthang ïa ki light kiba thaba, ka jingpyn bun palat ïa ki jingtah dur ba laiphew jait bad ka jing bym pyndon kam jong u nongñiah ïa u seat belt ha ka por ba u ñiah kali bad kiwei kiwei kiba long pyrshah ïa ka Indian motor vehicle Act.     Halor katei ka jingrei kam pyrkhing jong ki pulit pynïaid kali ha sor Nongstoiñ na ka liang ki paitbah, ki sengbhalang bad ki synjuk jong ki nong ñiah kali ki la dei ban ai ka jingïatrei lang kaba khlaiñ bha bad ban ai ruh ka jingkyrshan kaba khlaiñ ïa ka tnad pulit khnang ba kan nym pynthut ïa kiwei pat ki para nongñah kali,ki paitbah kiba ïaid ba ïeng, ki khynnah skul, ki nong ashong dukan, bad kiwei kiwei.
    Ha kjuh ka por kumba ka long haduh mynta ki dang don bun bah ki nongñiah kali kami sor (Local Taxi) ha Nongstoiñ ki bym nang satia ban burom ïa kiwei pat ki kali kiba ïaid ha katei ka sor nalor kata ki ba shu pynpah horn klumar wat ha ka por ba don ka jingdheng kali kaba malu mala ruh.
    Kumta lymda don ka jingïatrei lang bad ki pulit pynïaid kali kan shem shitom ban wan rah ia ka jingïaid beit ïaid ryntih hynrei kan wan rah pynban ïa ka kynrum kynram.

Sahkut kali da ki kynta ba siang rong ka sorkar ïa ka surok bha
Shillong,Ïaïong 10: Ki paidbah ba leit jingleit lyngba ka surok 7 mer,Upper Shillong mynta ka sngi, ki la lyngngoh hi ngaiñ ïa kaei kaba ki la lap mynta ka sngi, haba ki ïaid lyngba kane ka surok.
    Ka daw ka long ba ym tang ba ki la ïakynduh ïa ka jingsahkut kali kaba da ki kynta, hynrei ki la ïohi da la ki khmat ïa ka jingsiang rong ïaka surok kaba dang bha. Ka bynta kaba la siang rong kadei ha surok 7 mer ha ka jaka ba don ka jaka shong ki shipai suiñ ka Eastern Air Command.
    Ki paidbah ki la mad ïa ka jingeh kaba khraw, haba kiba leit bad hiar bad ba kiew na kane ka surok ki la sahkut haduh lai bad saw kynta.
    Kane ka jingsahkut kali jong ki, kala pynïohlad ïa ki ban pyrkhat, balei ba ka sorkar ka siang rong ha ka surok kaba dang hha kum kane.
    Uwei u rangbah uba dei ban leit sha Pynursla bad ki khun ba dang rit, u la pynpaw ka jingbitar ïa kane ka jingleh ka sorkar kaba pynbha ïa kane ka surok kaba dang bha bad jlih bha. “Kaei kane ba ka sorkar ka leh, haba sha nongkyndong ki don bun ki surok kiba la jot rathai, ka sorkar ka ong ba kam don pisa, katba ïa kane kaba bha ha Sor pat ka pynbha?”, u la ong.
    Ki don kiwei ruh kiba dei ban leit sha West Khasi, South West Khasi ki la pynpaw ka jingsngew bynñiaw ban ïohi ïa kane, namar ba ki wan na ki shnong kiba ka surok kalong kum ka surok kulai, hynrei ym shym la pynbha, kat ïakane kaba ha Sor pat la pynbha. “Kane ka pynpaw shai kdar ïaka jingleh shiliang khmat jong kane ka sorkar,kaba pyrkhat tang ïaki nong sor, katba ïa ki nongkyndong pat ka iehbeiñ”,ki laong.
    Ladon napdeng kiba sahkut kali,ki la ïathuh ba ki khun jong ki, ki la thngan bad ki la shu ïa pan biskit na ki shipai kiba don ha katei ka jaka.

Kiew ki nongwan jngohkai na Bangladesh sha wah Umngot
Shillong, Ïaiong 10 : Ka jingdon ka wah Umngot ha Dawki, kadei ka jingsarong ïa ka jylla hi baroh kawei hynrei haba phai pat sha ki nongjngohkai, la i kumba bun pynban na Bangladesh kiba pynlut ïa ka por bad bor ban wan peit ïa ka jingithiang bad ka jingkhuid jong katei ka wah kaba don ha khappud.
Watla bun ki shnong Meghalaya kiba don ha syndah jong katei ka wah Umgot kim da myntoi haduh ktta ktta na ka kam jngohkai pyrthei hynrei, la ïohi pat ba ki jaka bad ki nongrit kiba don ha Bangladesh khamtam kito kiba shi kilometer ne tam, mar shilliang bad ka Dawki i kumba ki kiew stet na ka jingbun ki nongwan jngohkai.
    Ban khring bad pynsuk ïa ki nongwan jngohkai, kitei ki shnong Bangladesh kiba don kumba katto katne kilometer na ka wah Umngot ki la pynïeng syndon da ki jaka kyrpang na ka bynta kitei ki nongwan, kynthup wat ïa ki jaka pynieng kali ruh.
    “Kiba wanpeit ïa ka wah Umngot kumba ngi ïohi, ki don bun shah na Bangladesh ban ïa kiba wan na kane ka thaiñ jongngi, ong iwei na ki longkmie ha Dawki.
    Uwei pat u rangbah u la ïathuh ba ki shnong kum ka Kuchigram bad Admedpur kiba don tang kumba 1-2 kilometer na u pud India - Bangladesh ki don bun tylli ki jaka thiah pyngad ne resort, nangta sa ka three star hotel ha Pratappur na ka bynta kito ki nongwan kai kiba la kham bit khambiang, kiba wan ban pynlut por ban wan peit ïa ka jingitynnad ka mariang ha Meghalaya - India.
    Iwei pat i longkmie Khasi ba wankai i la kdew ïa ka jingdon ki jait lieng ba harukom kiba per ha katei ka wah sha shilliang pud bad ruh ïa ki jaka bam kiba bun ryngkat ka jingkren bynñiaw ba ha u pud lajong pat don tang kiba die jingbam khutia kiba ym ïa kot bor ban nujor bad kito kiba die sha shilliang pud.
