Lap ka CAG ba ïohnong palat 7.17 klur ka kompani na ka jingpyndait HSRP
Ba pynheh dor palat pud ka Transport Deptt
10 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong 09: Ka Comptroller & Auditor General of India (CAG) kala lap ba ka kompani ba pyndait nomber plate High Security Registration Plate (HSRP) ka la shu ïohnong ei kha ma kha haduh T.7.17 klur na ki Nongshongshnong ba don kali jong ka Jylla tang namar ka jingpynheh dor palat pud jong ka Sorkar Jylla ïa ka bai plate.

    Ki Nongshongshnong ba don kali jong ka Jylla kila hap ban siew bun shah ka dor ban ïa ka Jylla Meghalaya haba pyndait ïa ka nomber plate HSRP, kaba la pynïohnong ei kha ma kha khlem iahap shuh ïa ka Kompani.

    Ka M/s Shimnit Utsch India Private Limited ka dei ka kompani kaba pyndait ïa u nombor plate HSRP hapoh ka Jylla hadien ba ka iatehkular bad ka Tnad Transport ka Jylla ha u bnai Nairing 2005. Ha Mizoram ruh, kane ka kompani kala ïoh ban pyndait ïa ka HSRP hadien ka jingiateh kular ha u nohprah 2011. Hynrei kane ka kompani (M/s Shimnit Utsch India Pvt Ltd) kala shim la la ka jong ka dor bai HSRP ha kine ki artylli ki Jylla bad ka jingïapher kala long hapdeng T.14.43 bad T.736.29 kawei ka nombor plate.

    Hangne ha Jylla Meghalaya, ka dor bai HSRP na ka bynta ki kali arshaka ka long T. 682.43, ïa ki kali rit bad kali heh ka long T. 1681.29 hynrei ha Mizoram pat ka dor na ka bynta ki arshaka ka long T.668 bad ka kali rit bad kali heh ka long T.945 tyngka. Ka jing pyndait ïa ka HSRP kala treikam naduh u bnai Ïaiong 2007. Ka CAG ha ka kaiphod jong u snem ba kut ha ka 31 tarik Lber, 2016, kala lap ba ka Sorkar Jylla khlem da bishar bha ïa ki dor ki mur ha kiwei pat ki Jylla, kala ailad ïa ka kompani M/s Shimnit ba kan ïohnong palat na ka jingshim heh dor.

    Ka kaiphod ka ong ba ha kine ki juh ki snem, haduh 1,64,864 tylli ki kali bapher bapher kila pyndait HSRP hapoh ka Jylla. “Haba nujor bad ka Mizoram, ka kompani kala shu ïohnong ei kha ma kha haduh T.7.17 klur” ong ka kaiphod haba pynpaw ba ka Tnad Transport ha u bnai Risaw 2016, kala kdew ba ka jingiatehkular ba ka M/s Shimnit ka dei kaba la iateh hynriew snem mynshuwa shuwa jong ka Mizoram bad namar kane ka daw kam shym la ïohlad satia ban ianujor.

    Ka CAG kala kyntait ban pdiang ïa ka jubab jong ka Tnad Transport namar ka shem ba ka Tnad wat hadien 11 snem ba iateh kular ruh, ka tnad ka khlem leh eiei ban pynhiar ïa ka dor ka mur na ka bynta ban pyndait ïa ka HSRP bad kane kala ailad ïa ka kompani ban ïoh khnoit dor heh ïa ki nongshongshnong ba don kali.

    Ha kajuh ka por, ka CAG kala pynpaw ruh ïa ka jingbym lah jong ka Sorkar Jylla ban kynjoh ïa ka thong ban pynthikna ba baroh ki kali ba don ha Jylla ki dei kiba pyndait ïa ka HSRP. Ka CAG ka ong na ki 2,63,541 tylli ki kali bala register hapoh ka Jylla tad haduh u snem 2015-2016, tang 1,68,335 tylli ki kali (64 %) ki dei kiba la pyndait ïa ka HSRP. Kumta, 95,206 tylli ki kali ba ïaid ha kylleng ki surok ka Jylla da kiwei pat ki nombor plate kila pyn kheiñ ïa ka hukum jong ka Sorkar Kmie bad wanrah ïa ka jingduh khajna ba kot haduh T.0.32 klur.
Kyrshan ki paidbah bad ki seng ïa ka jingdawa Kolej Sorkar ha East Jaiñtia Hills
10 April, 2017
Khliehriat, Ïaiong, 09: Ki paidbah, ki sengbhalang bapher bapher ki la ai jingkyrshan bapura ïa ka Jaintia Student Movement kaba la lam khmat ban dawa na ka Sorkar Jylla ban wanrah noh kawei ka Kolej Sorkar ha East Jaiñtia Hills District.

    Da ki spah ngut ki paidbah ki la wan ïashim bynta ha kane ka jingïalang kaba la long ha Khliehriat, East Jaiñtia Hills District ha ka sngi saitjaiñ. Ki sengbhalang ba kyrshan ïa kane ka jingdawa ka JSM ki kynthup ïa ka East Jaiñtia National Council, Hynñiewtrep Achik National Movement, Hynñiewtrep Youths Council, All Jaiñtia Youth Welfare Organisation-EJZ, Khasi Jaiñtia National Union, Meghalayala People United Front (MPUF), ka AJPM bad kiwei kiwei.

    U Ma Leningstar Rymbai, President JSM haba kren ha kane ka jingïalang u la pynpaw ïa ka jingsngewkhia halor ka jingkiew ki khynnah ba pep skul shiteng por da kaba pynpaw ïa ka daw ka long namarba ki kmie ki kpa kim donlad shuh ban kyrshan skul ïa ki khun khamtam ha ki College barem dor (Private College).

    U la kyntu ïa ki paidbah nongshong shnong jong ka East Jaiñtia Hills District ba kin ai lem ka jingkyrshan ïa ka seng khnang ba kan dup lah ban ïaid shakhmat.

    U ïathuh ba ka seng ka ladep phah ïa ka jingthoh sha ka Kong Roshan Warjri, Myntri ka tnat Higher and Technical Education ka Sorkar Jylla, sha ka Deborah C. Marak, Myntri ka tnat School Education and Literacy, sha u Ma Justine Dkhar, MLA ka Khliehriat, uba long ruh u Parliamentary Secretary.

    U pynpaw ruh ba ka seng ka ieng na ka bynta ka lawei ki khynnah bad ki samla pule ha ka District ki ban ïoh jingmyntoi lada don ka Kolej jong ka Sorkar.

    U Samla Daman Lathong, President ka HYC-JHD u la kyntu ïa ki paidbah ka distrit ba kin long kiba ïohi jngai na ka bynta ka lawei jong ki khun ki kti. U la ong ruh, lada ki briew kim nang ban pyrkhat sani bha kan wanrah ïa ka jingsahdien, ka jingshahrem, ka jingduk, ki jingsniew bad kan wanrah ruh ïa ka jingsahbiej.

    “Ngeit skhem ba ka JSM kan kit ïa kane ka lyngkor haduh kaba kut”bad u kyntu ruh ïa ki paitbah ba kin ai ka jing kyrshan ïa ka JSM.

    U Samla Sambormi Lyngdoh, General Secretary EJNC u la ong ba ka jing dawa ban ïoh ïa ka College Sorkar ka dei ka jingmyntoi jong uba bun ba lang bad ka dei ruh na ka bynta ka lawei jong ki khynnah. U la ai mynsiem ïa ki nongïalam ka JSM ba kin ïakhun haduh kaba kut da ka jingkyrshan ki paidbah ka East Jaiñtia Hills District.

    U Samla Wanshwa Suting, President ka AJYWO-EJZ u la pynpaw ka jingsngewkhia halor kito ki khynnah kiba hap ban pep skul noh shiteng por tang namar ka jing duk bym lah shuh ban kyrshan na iing. U la ong ba ha East Jaiñtia Hills District ki la don shibun bha ki skul bad ynda kine ki khynnah ki la pyndep ïa ka skul ki hap ban sangeh noh namarba ki kmie ki kpa kim lah shuh ban kyrshan ban phah pule kham shalor ha ki Private College kiba rem dor ha kaba ka baibam (Scholarship) ba ïoh kam ïahap satia bad ka bai siew College.

    U Bah D.Laloo, President ka MPUF u la khot lang ïa baroh ki paitbah ka East Jaiñtia Hills District ban ieng lang kawei ban kyntiew ïa ka pule puthi ha ka District. U la kyntu ruh ïa ki paidbah ba ki dei ban long kiba stad ha kaba jied ïa ki Nongmihkhmat khnang ba kan ym wanrah ïa ka jingbabe bad ka jingduhnong ka District.

    Ka kong Piarina Nongtdu, ka la kren da ka jingjaw ummat bad jingdap mynsiem haba ka ai ïa ka jing kyrshan ïa ka JSM. Kane ka longkmie ka la pynpaw ba ka dang kwah bad thrang ban pyndep ïa ka jingpule B.Com hynrei ka daw ka long namar ka jingbym lah shuh ban kyrshan ban leit pule sha Jowai. Kane ka longkmie ka la ong ruh ba kan long ka jingmyntoi kaba khraw kham tam ïa ki baduk lada ka Sorkar kan wanrah ïa kawei ka College ha East Jaiñtia Hills District. La ïoh jingkren ruh na kiwei kiwei ki nongïalam jong ki Sengbhalang.
Hato ki kor ki bor Electronic Voting Machine ki long kiba thikna?
10 April, 2017
New Delhi, Iaiong 9 : Ha kine ki snem ba la dep, la mih bun ki jingkylli bad kiwei ki jingkhuslai jingmut jingpyrkhat shaphang ka jinglong jingman ki kor ki bor Electronic Voting Machine jong ka Election Commission ka ri India. Ha kaba ïa dei bad kane ka phang, ka Election Commission jong ka ri, na kawei k por sha kawei pat, ka la pynsngew bad pynthikna ba ki Electronic Voting Machine jong ka Election Commission ka Ri India, ki long kiba skhem, kiba khlaiñ, kiba thikna bad kiba ym lah ban pynbakla ïa ki.

    Kine ki long ki jingbatai kiba kham bniah ha kaba ïa dei bad kiba bun ki jingkylli ba la buh da ki paidbah na kawei ka por sha kawei pat, kiba ïa dei bad ki jingshna, ki jingpyndait ïa ki bynta bapher bapher kiba don ha ki Electronic Voting Machine bad kum juh ruh ïa ki lad ki lynti kiba kham pyrkhing ba la shem da ki bor Sorkar naduh ban shim ïa ki machine, kumno ba buh ïa ki ha ki jaka bapher bapher shuwa ban pyndonkam.

    1. Ka mut aiu da kaba ong ban pynbakla ïa ki EVM?

    Ka jingpynbakla ïa ki EVM

ka mut, ka jingpynkylla ïa ka software program kaba kynthup ïa ki microchips jong ka Control Unit (CU) lane da kaba thep khnang da kiwei pat ki Microchip ha ka Control Unit, kaba khura ban pynlong ïa ki budam ha ka por ba khniot ba kin ym pat rung ha ka Control Unit.

    2. Hato lah ban pynkylla ïa ki EVM jong ka Election Commission of Ri India?

“Em”. Kane kam ym lah ban long dalei lei ruh. Ïa ka M1 (model one) EVM machines la shna haduh ka snem 2006. La shim lut ïa baroh ki lad jingïada ban pynlong ïa ka MA model kaba lait na kano kano ka jingpynbakla. Ka jingkam jong ki katto katne ba ki EVM ki don jingbakla ka long kaba khlem nongrim bad kaba ym don jingshisha.

Dei halor ka jingai jingmut jong ka Technical Evaluation Committee ha ka snem 2006, ba la pynmih ïa ka EVM M2 model bad pyndonkam ïa ki haduh ka snem 2012, ha kaba la sdang ruh ban pyndonkam ïa i kot thep vote barit ne Ballot Unit kum i jingpynshisha bad ïa ka por thep vote.

    Ki EVM jong ka Election Commission, ki long kita ki kor ki bor kiba ym don kano kano ka jingïapyndait bad kiwei pat ki kor ki bor computer. Ki trei hi ïa la ka jong ka kam bad kim don kano kano ka jingïasnoh bad ka lad pathai jingtip ne Internet ne bad kine kino ki jingtrei kam network ha kata ka por. Dei na kane ka daw ba lah ban ong da kaba sngewskhem ba yn ym lah ban pynbakla ïa kine ki kor ki bor.

    Ki EVM ka Election Commission of India (ECI), kim don kano kano ka jingïadei bad kiwei pat ki kor ki bor bad kim lah hi ruh ban don kano kano ka jingtrei kam bad kiwei pat.

Dei na kata ka daw ba yn ym lah ban ban pynbakla ïa ki EVM, da kino kino ki lad lyngba ka jingtrei kam Wireless lane Bluetooth namarba ka Central Unit kan ym pdiang ïa kita.

    Hato ki nongshna ki lah ban pynbakla ïa ki EVM ka ECI?

Kaba ym lah ban long.

    Ka jingshna ïa ki EVM ka long hadeng ka jingpeit pyrman kaba pyrkhing haduh katta katta, kham tam lei lei ha kaba ïa dei bad ki Software. Ïa ki machine la shna ha ki snem bapher bapher naduh ka snem 2016. Hadien ba la dep shna ïa ki, la pynpoi pat ïa ki sha ki jylla bad ka district bapher bapher na ka bynta ban pyndonkam. Ki nongshna ïa ki EVM kin ym lah shuh ban tip shaphang kine ki machine namarba la shna ïa ki na kawei ka por sha kawei pat. Kin ym lah hi ruh ban tip shuwa ka por, uno uta u kyrtong elekshon u ban ïa khun ïa ka jingjied nongmih khmat bad kiei kita ki kyrtong ki ban ïa khun lang bad u ha kata ka por khnang ban kan ïa dei bad ka machine. Ka Election Commission ka ai ruh ïa ki Serial numbor ban buddien ïa ki jingtrei kam jong ki kor ki bor. Kane ka pynthikna ban ym lah ban pynbakla ïa ki EVM.

    4. Halor lah ban pynrung ïa u Trojan Hourse ha u chip jong ka Control Unit ?

    Ka jingthep vote, kawei hadien kawei, ka pynlong ïa u Trojan Hourse ban shah kyntait. Ki kor EVM ba la shna da ka Election Commission ka Ri India, ka pynthikna ban yn ym lah da lei lei ruh ban pynrung ïa u Trojan Hourse. Kane ka long na ka daw jong ki jingtrei kam bakhlaiñ ha ki EVM.

5. Hato dang pyndonkam ïa ki EVM barim?

    Ïa ki EVM M1 model, ïa kiba la shna haduh ka snem 2006, la pyndonkam haduh ka snem 2014. Ha ka snem 2014, ïa ki EVM kiba la dap 15 snem bad namarba ha ki M1 model ym lah ban pyndonkam ïa ki VVPAT (voter-verified paper audit trail), ka Election Commission ka la shim ïa ka rai ban ym pyndonkam shuh ïa ki. Ïa kane ka jingpynduh pyndam noh ïa kine ki EVM kiba ym long shuh ban pyndonkam la leh ha khmat jong ki Chief Electoral Officer jong ki jylla, lane ki nongmihkhmat jong ki karkhana ba pynmih ïa ki.

6. Hadien ba la pynjot pynsniew ïa ki EVM, hato dang lah ban pynkylla ïa ki khlem ka jingïohi jong kiwei pat.

    Ki EVM thymmai M3 Model ki lah ban kem ïa ki tiar ba la dep pyndonkam teng. Shen yn sa ïoh ïa ka jingpyndonkam ïa ki EVM model M3. Ka Technical Experts Committee kan dang peit bniah ïa kane, shuwa ban pynmih bad pyndonkam paidbah ïa ki. Ka Sorkar jong ka ri, ka la pyllait peisa haduh 2000 klur tyngka ban thied ïa ki EVM model M3, kiba don ïa ki jingdonkam baroh.

7. Kiei kiba don ha ki EVM ban pynthikna ba ki lait na ka jingpyndonkam bakla?

    Kiei kiba pynlong ïa ki EVM ban lait na ka jingpynbakla. Ka jingshna ïa ki EVM ka long kaba da phikir haduh katta na ka liang jong ka jingpyndonkam ïa ki kor ki bor bad ïa ki bynta bapher bapher kiba kynthup ïa ka one time programmable (OTP) microcontrollers, dynamic coding of key codes, ka tarik bad ka por ba khniot ïa u budam, advanced encryption technology bad EVM-tracking software ban buddien hangno ki EVM ki don bad baroh ki machine ki dei ban long 100 na ka 100 kiba lait na kino kino ki jingduna.

8. Hato ki EVM ki dei ruh kiba pyndonkam ia ki tiar nongwei?

    Kaba long mar khong pong ïa kata, ka India, kam shym la pyndon kam ïa ki EVM ba shna na bar ri lane pyndon kam ïa ki tiar jong ki haba shna ïa ki EVM. Ki EVM jong ka ri, ki dei kiba shna da ka artylli ki Public Sector Unit kum ka Bharat Electronics Ltd., Bengaluru bad Electronics Corporation of India Ltd., Hyderabad. Kine ki artylli ki Public Sector Union jong ka ri, ki shna bad pynmih hi ïa la ki jong ki tiar na ka bynta ki EVM hapoh ka ri.

9. Hato dang lah ban don kiba leh thok ha ki jaka ba buh ïa ki EVM?

    Ïa ki EVM la buh ha ki District Headquarter da kaba khang da artylli ki tala bad ka jingpahara kaba biang. Yn ym don ba ïoh lad ban tur shaba don ki EVM. Ha ka por ba ym long elekshon, ka don ka jingpeit jingjngoh ïa ki EVM da ki DEOs bad ai jingtip sha ka Election Commission ka Ri India

10. Hato ki jingkynnoh ba don jingpynbakla ïa ki EVM ki long kiba shisha?

    Ka don ka jingsngewthuh bakla halor kane ka phang. Kawei kaba dei ban sngewthuh, ka long, ba ka jingpynlong ïa ki jingjied nongmihkhmat sha ki Municipal Board le Coporations lane ha ka jingjied nongmihkhmat Panchayat, ki dei kiba pynlong da ki Sorkar jylla, ym da ka Election Commission. Kine kiba pynlong ïa ki jingjied nongmihkhmat ki thied hi la ki jong ki EVM. Kane kam dei ka jingkitkhlieh jong ka Election Commission ka Ri India.

11. Kumno ban leh ban peit ba ki EVM ki long kiba lait na ki jingpyndonkam bakla?

    Ka jingpeit jingkhmih banyngkong ka long da ki engineer jng ka BEL bad ECIL kiba dei ban pynthikna ba ki bynta bapher bapher ki dei kiba bha bad ka jingpynthikna ba man la kawei pa kawei ka EVM ka dei ban long kaba trei kam bha hakhmat jong ki nongmihkhmat. Dei ban pynlong ïa ki jingjied thep vote Mock poll jong ki1000 nongthep vote bad dei ruh ban ring Video ïa kane.

Dei ban ïa khleh lang ïa ki EVM shuwa ban rah sha ki jaka thep vote.

Dei ban buh ha ki jaka baskhem hadien ba la wanrah ïa ki na ki jaka thep vote.

Dei ban buh jingkheiñ ïa ki EVM ryngkat bad u ID number.

2. Lah ban lehthok?

Kane ka jingkylli kam dei ban mih. Kane ka long ba la shim lut ïa baroh ki lad ki lynti ban pynthikna ba ki EVM ki long kiba bha bad kiba lait na kino ki jingduna.

13. Balei ki ri shai jong ka pyrthei, ka America bad ki ri Europe kim treh ban pyndonkam ïa ki EVM bad don kiwei pat ki ri kiba dang pyndonkam ïa ki?

Kitei ki ri kim treh shuh ban pyndkam ïa ki EVM ha ka por jied nongmihkhmat namarba ki ïa kynduh jingeh. Kitei ki EVM ki long kiba la shna ha kata ka rukom bad ki don ki jingïadei bad ki kor ki bor komputor, kiba la ban shah pyndonkam bakla. Ka jinghap ban pahara ïa ki EVM ruh lehse kan ym long ka kam kaba suk na ka bynta jong ki. Ki EVM ha ri India kim don jingïasnoh bad kino kino ki kor ki bor komputor.

    Ka India ka don la ki jong ki EVM. Katba ka America Netherlands, Ireland & Germany ki don ki direct recording machines ba ki pyndonkam ha ka por ba jied nongmihkhmat. Kawei kaba dei ban sngewthuh ka long ba ka India ka don la ki jong ki aiñ ban pynlong elekshon ba kata ka jingjied ïa ki nongmihkhmat ka dei kaba da thikna.

Ha kaba ïa dei bad a Netherlands, kane ka ri kam don kita ki kyndon kumno ban buh, ban rah ban rong bad ban peit ba ka jingbuh ïa ki EVM ha ki jaka kiba skhem, shngaiñ bad kiba thikna. Ki EVM ba shna ka Netherlands, ki pyndonkam ha Ireland bad ka Germany. Ha ka snem 2005, ka Ïing Bishar jong ka Germany ka la shem ka jingpyndonkam ïa kita ki EVM ka long pyrshah ïa ki Riti Synshar jong katei ka ri. Dei na kane ka daw, ba kine ki ri mynta kim pyndonkam shuh ïa kine ki EVM ba shna da ka Netherlands

    Ban shu ïa nujor kulmar bad kiwei pat ka long kaba bakla.

14. Ki long kumno ki VVPAT machine?

Ka Election Commission ka Ri India ka la pynlong ïa ka jingjied nongmihkhmat ne elekshon ha ki 107 tylli ki constituency bad 9 tylli ki Lok Sabha constituency da kaba pyndonkam ia ka jingtrei Voters Verified Paper Audit Trail (VVPAT). Ka jingpyndonkam ki EVM model M2 bad EVM Model M3 ryngkat bad kaba pyndonkam ïa jingtrei kam VVPAT kan wanrah ïa ka jingshaniah ha ki paidbah bad ka jingtrei kaba khuid kaba suba hapdeng ki nongthep vote.

Gopajit Das, IIS

Media & Communication Officer

PIB, Shillong
Shongkun ka Shad Lakhempong ka Raid Nongtung ha Umpowin
10 April, 2017
Nongpoh, Ïaïong 09: Ban dang ïai pynneh pynsah ïa la ka riti ka dustur katkum ka jinglong tynrai ba la ïalam naduh ki Longshuwa ki Manshuwa, ka Dorbar ka Raid Nongtung mynta ka snem ruh ka la bteng ban pynlong ïa kawei na ka shad Tynrai ba la tip kum ka ‘ Shad Lakhempong’ kaba dei kawei na ka Shad Tynrai hapoh ka Raid Nongtung ba hap ha Ri Bhoi District.

    Ïa kane ka shad Lakhempong la pynlong ha phyllaw ka Mangkathiang Upper Primary School, Umpowin, ha kaba u Dr. Dr. D.D Lapang, MLA ka Nongpoh bad uba dei ruh u Myntri rangbah ba rim ka jylla, u la wan ban shim bynta kum u kongsan bad u Myntri ka tnad Art and culture, u Bah R.V Lyngdoh kum u symbut kongsan.

    La sakhi lang ruh ha kane ka jingshad tynrai ka Raid Nongtung da ka jingdon lang u Deputy Commissioner ka Ri Bhoi, C.P Gotmare, u SP ka Ri Bhoi, u R. Singh, u Acting Syiem ka Hima Mylliem, u Paiem Ricky Nelson Syiem, u ADM ka Ri Bhoi, u Bah D.P Kharsati bad kynthup ruh kiwei kiwei ki riew rangbah na ka District.

    La pynphun pynphieng ruh ha kane ka sngi da ka jingwan shim bynta shitrhem ki khun ki hajar na ka Raid Nongtung ba kynthup na ki 22 tylli ki Shnong ba hap hapoh ka Raid Nongtung bad ryngkat ki khun samla kiba la shim bynta ha kane ka jingshad, kaba dei kawei na ka shad tynrai ne ka shad lehniam ka Raid Nongtung.

    Kum ban pynpaw, kane ka Shad Lakhempong, ka dei kawei na ka shad tynrai ba ka Raid Nongtung ka la lah ban pynim biang mynta la shiphew snem kynthih, hadien ba bun na ki khun ki hajar ka Raid ki la klet ïa la ka shad tynrai, kaba dei katkum ka jingshimkhia jong ki nongialam ka Raid Nongtung.

    Haba kren ha kane ka sngi kum u kongsan, u Dr. D.D Lapang u la ai a jingiaroh ïa ka Raid Nongtung kaba don kata ka jingkitkhlieh ban pynneh pynsah ïa la ki riti ki dustur bad ki jinglong tynrai kiba la longdoh longsnam hapoh ka Raid.

    “Kane ka jingpynlong ïa kane ka shad tynrai, ka long ruh kum ka jingkyrsiew thiah ïa ki khun ki hajar hapoh ka Raid, ba ki dei ban niewkor ïa la ka tynrai, namar kano kano ka jaid bynriew kaba ym don la ka riti ka dustur ne ka jinglong tynrai ka dei ka jaid bynriew kaba ïap” la ong u Dr. D.D Lapang.

    Shuh shuh, u la kyntu ruh ïa ki paidbah ka Raid ba kim dei ban klet ïa la ka tynrai hynrei ba ki dang dei ban pynbit pynbiang bad ban dang pynjanai shuh shuh ïa baroh ki riti ki dustur ne ka jinglong tynrai, namar lada kum ka jaid bynriew ka lah ban pynneh pynsah ïa la ka tynrai kane kan ïarap ym tang ban im ka jaid bynriew, hynrei kan long ruh kawei na ka lad ban kyntiew ïa ka ioh ka kot ki paidbah ha kaba bun na ki briew kiba nabar kin wan ban lum jingtip ne ban peitkai lada ngi lah ban leh ha kata ka rukom kaba janai ïa kane ka shad tynrai jong ka Raid kumba long lem kiwei kiwei ki shad tynrai ba paw ha ka pyrthei, u la bynrap.

    Ha kane ka sngi la ai jingkren ruh da u Myntri ka Art and Culture, u Bah R.V Lyngdoh, uba la pynpaw ïa kajuh ka jingkmen ban ia don bynta bad ki khun ki hajar ka Raid Nongtung ban sakhi ha katei ka sngi ba ki la lah ban pynlong ïa kane ka shad tynrai kaba long shi bynta ban pynneh pynsah ïa la ka tynrai hapoh katei ka Raid.

    Ha kawei ka bynta kum u myntri u la kular ruh ban iarap halor ka dorkhas ba la phah da ka Raid kaba ki la pypaw ïa ka jingdonkam ban ker sawdong ia u Maw Buh Shyieng ba don ha Ummat bad kumjuh ruh ka Community Hall bad ka Jaka shad tynrai kaba paka ba ka Raid ka donkam na ka bynta ban pynneh ïa ki riti ki dustur kiba don hapoh ka Raid Nongtung ha Ri Bhoi.
La 13 tarik jingïalang paitbah ha Langpih
10 April, 2017
Nongstoiñ, Ïaïong 9 : Naduh ba ka ophis jong ka Khasi Hills Atonoumous Distrct Council (KHADC) lyngba u Chief Executive Member (CEM) u Bah Pynshngaiñ Syiem ka la pynbna bad aiti ha u Bah Phlowing Syiem Nongbah ïa ka dulir ba la pynim biang ïa ka Hima Nongmynsaw kaba la jah naduh shispah snem tam mynshuwa.             Katei ka jingleh jong u CEM ka la pyn lyngoh pat ïa ki paitbah ka Hima namar ha shuwa ba utei u Bah Phlowing Syiem Nongbah un ïaid shakhmat ïa katei ka kam um shym la lum ïa ki paitbah ka Hima ban pynshai bad pynsgewthuh kaei ka jingïapher hapdeng ka Hima Nongmynsaw bad ka Raidmynsaw.

    Na ka liang ki sordar jong ki shnong kiba hap hapoh katei ka Hima ki la ong bad pynshisha ba haduh mynta baroh kawei ka Hima ka dang don ha pdeng ka jingïa kajia bad ka jingshah tap pud bad ki ar sorkar ka Meghalaya bad Assam haduh mynta kim pat lah ban ïapynbeit.

    Nalor kata ki la ong ruh ba naduh u snem 1979 mynba ki paitbah katei ka thaiñ naduh Mawdangsnam, Langpih, Umwali, Umtap, Mawlan, Umwahsiang, Nongma, bad kiwei kiwei ki la kylla phetwir na ka jingshah khynra ha ki pulit Assam na ka liang kiitei ki jait Syiem Nongbah kim shym la ïeng ban lum ïa ki paitbah ban ïada ïa ka it ka Hima, ka khyndew ka shyiap bad wat haduh u snem 1986-87 ter ter ba ki Nepali ki la sdang ban wan rung jubor bad knieh ïa ki kper ki phrah ,ki lyngkha ki risai ruh ym don kita ki syiem Nongbah kiba ïada hynrei tad ha kine ki sngi ba ki la ïohi ba ka suk ka saiñ ka la wan phai biang ki la sdang ban mih pyrthei.

    Kumta halor katei ka bynta na ka liang u Bah Hindro Samakha Sirdar ka Hima Raidmysaw haba pyntip ha u Mawphor mynta ka sngi u la ïa thuh ba ma u ryngkat ki sordar jong ki 62 tylli ki shnong kiba hap hapoh katei ka hima ki la iakut ban pynlong da ka jingïalang paitbah ha Langpih ha ka 13 tarik mynta u bnai bad hakatei ka sngi la khot lut ia baroh ki paitbah ka Hima kynthei, shynrang, khynnah bad samla ban wan ha katei ka jingïalang na ka bynta ba kin pynshai halor katei ka bynta.

    Ha kajuh ka por u Bah Samakha u la ïathuh ba naduh ba ki Syiem Nongbah kim don shuh ki nonghiar pateng ban shimti ïa ka synshar khaddar ïa katei ka Hima la peit shipor da ka u Syiem ka Hima Rambrai bad la thung da ki Myntri kiba dei ki nongshong shnong ba pura napoh katei ka Hima Raid Mynsaw.Nalor kata u la ïathuh ruh ba u Myntri ba nyngkong eh u dei u (L) Jessesingh Snar na ka shnong Mawdiangsnam.

    Ha dien jong u Jesse la thung ïa u Bah Phrikshon Kharlyngdoh na ka shnong Umtap kum u Myntri bad ter ter bad u Bah Hindro Samakha ruh u la sha jied kum u Myntri naduh u snem 1984 bad dei tad haduh u snem 2009 ha ka por ba u Bah K.P.Pangñiang u la shah jied kum u MDC ha kaba u la bat ruh kum u Excecutive Member ba peit ïa ki Elaka ba u la pynskhem ïa ka Hima Raidmynsaw kum kawei na ki Hima Sirdar ba thymmai ha West Khasi Hills kaba hap hapoh u pud u sam jong ka KHADC bad haduh mynta u Bah samakha u dang long hi kum u Sirdar ba pura jong ka Hima.

    Ha kajuh ka por u la ong ba ka jing leh jong ka KHADC ka long ka bym shong nia bad ka bym don nongrim namar ha shuwa ba kan pynkylla kyrteng kat ïa ka Hima ka la dei ban pyntip ha u kum u Nongsynshar khang ba un lum ïa ki paitbah ban ïa pyrkhat kumno yn leh hynrei ka jingïaid lait jong u Bah P.N.Syiem ïa u kum u nongsynshar bad ruh ïa ka Dorbar Hima ka loang ka ba beaiñ bad ka jing pynkheiñ im im peit peit ïa ka riti synshar paitbah jong u khun Khasi.

    U la pyni nuksa ruh ba wat haba ka sorkar ka don kam ban shna ïa ki surok ,ki ophis bad kiwei kiwei ki jing donkam na ka bynta ka jingmyntoi u paitbah ka dang hap ban pan jingbit (No Objection Certificate) na u Sordar shnong ne u trai jaka lei lei kat ka jingpynkylla kyrteng ïa ka Hima hato hap ban shu leh da ka bor tang namar ba u long CEM?.

    Khatduh eh u Bah Samaklha u la ong ba hato u Bah P.N.Syiem u tip ne em ba ki don da ki phew bad ki spah ngut ki khunlung khynnah kiba la dep ïoh ïa ki Certificate na ki shnaong ba pher kiba don hapoh ka Hima bad ki ban sa pyndonkam da kitei ki certificate kiba don ïa ka Muhor jong u sordar shnong na ka Hima Raidmynsaw Sirdarship bad lada la pynkylla Nongmynsaw Syiemship la hap bnan leh da ka Affidavit bad hap pynlut pisa da ki hajar tyngka hato katei kam ktah ïa kiba duk ba suk.?

    Katei ka jingleh jong u Bah P.N.Syiem ka wanrah pynban ïa ka kynrum kynram bad ka jing ïapait ïa pra hapoh ka hima baroh kawei u la ong.
Ïoh jingkoit ki riewngeit ha ka jingïaid pilkrim na Umsiang sha Orlong Hada
10 April, 2017
Shillong, ïaiong, 09: Hapoh ka jingpynïaid jong u Phadar Auggie Khrawlang Warbah, ki paid u Blei jong ka St. Francis D’Assisi Catholic Church, Umsiang ki la pynlong ka jingïaid pilkrim banyngkong eh da ka kjat na Umsiang sha Orlong Hada, ka Eco-Spirituality Centre, ha kaba ki Brother (Franciscan Missionary Brothers), ha ka sngi Saitjaiñ.

    Watla ka long ka sien banyngkong, la don palat 100 ngut ki nongleit pilkrim kiba la shim bynta da ka jingriewblei.

    Ki mat ba kham phylla na kane ka jingïaid pilkrim ka la jia, baroh shi taïew ar taïew, ka bneng ka ju slap hynrei haba la saiñdur ïa kane ka jingïaid pilkrim, u Ph. Auggie u la ong ha kato ka sngi ba la sdang ka jingïaid pilkrim, kan ym slap bad ka bneng kan long ka bapyngngad. Kane ka la jia shisha da ka jingshah skhor u Blei ïa ki jingduwai ki riewngeit.

    Kawei na ki longkmie, ka Kong Emilia Jalong, ka la ong, “Phadar, ngam ju lah ban ïaid kjat palat shi mer, namar tang shu ïaid slem palat, nga la king khlieh, hynrei ha kane ka kynti mynta, nga sngew ba nga la ïoh jingkoit.”

    Kawei pat ka nonghikai, ka Kong Pynhunlang Nongbsap, ka la ong, “kane ka dei ka sien banyngkong ba nga ïohlad ban duwai bad ïaid kjat artat. Naduh mynta, lada u Phadar Auggie u ong, ‘ïa ngin ïa ïaid ar ne lai sngi ruh, nga long ka bakloi ban shim bynta.”

    Ka Kong Labinia Kharwar ka ong, "nga khlem thait ei ei ha kane ka sien ïaid bamynta bad nga sngew pynngad bha ka mynsiem." U Bansaiñpynïar L. Mawdkhap u ong, "ka long ka bashoh mynsiem bad ai bor shisha ïa nga."     La don ruh kiwei pat ki briew na kiwei pat ki kynhun Balang kiba la wan shimbynta lang ba kynthup na ki riewngeit Presbyterian, Hindu bad ki niam Tiwa.

    Ha kane ka jingïaid pilkrim, la don ki jaitbynriew bapher ba kynthup ïa ki Khasi, ki Tiwa (Lalung), ki Nepali, ki Assamese, ki Naga, ki Karbi bad kiwei kiwei ha ryngkat ka jingsynran lang ki riewniam, ki longkpa, ki longkmie, ki samla shynrang bad kynthei bad ki hep barit.Ki sakhi bad ki jingïohmad (Testimonies and Experiences) na ki nongïashim bynta ki pynpaw kumne harum.

    U heprit Bashan Jalong, 9 snem, “nga sngewtynnat ba nga la ïohlad ban duwai, ban ïaid pilkrim bad khamtam ban rah ïa ka diengphna u Jisu. U samla David Matlai, , 14 snem na ka niam Hindu, ong, “nga sngewkmen ban ïoh duwai ha u Jisu. U Jonis Pumah, 16 snem na ka Balang Katholik u ong, “nga sngewkmen ba nga ïoh duwai katba dang ïaid, kaba ngam ju tip ba ngi lah ban leh kumta. U Boshan Rai, 16 snem u Nepali na ka niam Hindu u ong, “nga sngewnguh ïa u Blei namar u la ai ïa kane ka lad ban ïaid pilkrim. Nga kmen ba ngi ïa duwai bad ruwai katba ngi dang ïaid. U Jeres Lamare, u ong, “nga sngewtynnat ba khlem don ka jingpynthut ei ei, wat lada baroh shikatta ka la ju slap jur …” Ka Ruphina, Hamti Khorai, Run Sakra, Biona Pumah, bad Candi Lamare ki la pynpaw da kaba ong, “ha jingim jong ngi, ngim pat ju ïohmad kum kane ka jingïaid pilkrim. Ngi sngewkmen shisha, bad ngi da thrang ban shim bynta shuh shuh ha ki por ban sa wan.”

    Katto katne na ki dkhot ka Seng longkmie Sub-district Umsiang ki la ong, “kane ka jingïaid pilkrim ka la ai mynsiem shisha bad pynkhlaiñ shuh shuh ïa ka jingngeit jong ngi. Ngi sngewnguh ïa u Phadar Auggie Khrawlang Warbah, wat tang hapdeng ar bnai ka jingdon jong u hangne, u la lah ban lum lang bad pynïaid ïa kane ka jingïaid pilkrim ka bakyrpang jong ngi. Ngi sngewnguh ruh ïa u Bro. Pyndapbok Sohkhlet, i Sr. Sanaphisha Nongrum bad ki nonghikai basah lang bad Phadar, babu Bansaiñpynïar L. Mawdkhap, i Kong Pynhunlang Nongbsap bad Kong Labinia Kharwar, kiba la ai mynsiem lang.”

    Kane ka sngi ka dei ruh ka jingplie ïa ka Taïew Bakhuid ne ka Taïew jong ka jingshah shitom jong u Jisu.

    “Ngi sngewnguh kyrpang ruh ïa u Bro. George, Superior, u Bro. Orlando Wanñiang bad u Bro. Joseph, ki Brodar kiba don ha Orlong Hada, ba ki la pdiang sngewbha ïa ngi da ka jingkmen bakhraw,” ong u Phadar Auggie.

    Hadien ba la wanphai na Orlong Hada, u Ph. Auggie u la pynlong ka jingduwai pynkut ryngkat bad ka jingkyrkhu da ka diengphna u Jisu bad baroh ki nongleit pilkrim ki la kular ban leit pynpur bad ïalap ïariew ïa kane ka jingïohmad bakyrpang jong ki ïa u Blei.
Da ka jingphuh jingphieng pynkut ka Seng Khasi Nonglang ïa ka SSM
10 April, 2017
Mawkyrwat, Ïaïong 09: Ka Seng Khasi Nonglang, South West Khasi Hills District, Mawkyrwat mynta ka sngi ka la ïoh ban pynkut noh ïa ka Shad Suk Mynsiem (SSM) ba ju pynlong shi sien ha ka shi snem hapoh madan shad jong ka Seng Khasi Nonglang ha Nonglang.

    Kumban shu kdew khyndiat ba kane ka Shad ka kmen ka long ka jingkynmaw bad ka jingainguh u Khun-Khasi Khara kaba shisien shi snem ïa U Blei Trai Kynrad Nongbuh Nongthaw ban neh la ka hok la ka Riti.

    U Bah K. Erius Syiemlieh, Secretary Seng Khasi South West Khasi Hills u la long kum u kongsan ha ka ban pynhap ïa ka Lama jong ka Seng Khasi Nonglang ha ka jingïadonryngkat u Bah W. Biam, ADC South West Khasi Hills District,ki riew rangbah, ki nongshad na kylleng ka thaiñ South West Khasi Hills District bad ruh na ki wei pat ki District kum na East Khasi Hills District, bad na West Khasi Hills District.

    Ha kane ka sngi saitjaiñ jong ka taïew kaba dei ka sngi ban sdang ïa kane ka Shad Suk Mynsiem na ka liang ka Seng Khasi Nonglang ka la ïoh ruh ban plie ïa ka jaka shnong ki nongpeit kai (Gallery) ba la noh synñiang da u Ma V.H. Pala, MP jong ka Lok Sabha kaba shongdor T. 2 lak, ha kaba la plie ïa kane da u Samla Kynpham Kharlyngdoh, Muktiar jong ka Supreme Court ha ryngkat ka jingïadonlang u President ka Seng Khasi South West Khasi Hills District u Bah Taiparlin Kharlyngdoh, u Johnsing Iawphniaw, Secretary ka Seng Khasi Nonglang lem bad kiwei kiwei ki riew rangbah, ki longkmie longkpa bad ruh ki hep kiba rit.

    Haba ai jingkren ha kane ka sngi, u Samla Kynpham Kharlyngdoh u la ai khublei ïa baroh kiba la ïawan ha kane ka lympung, u la kitbok kitrwiang ruh na ka bynta ka Seng ba kan ïai bteng ban pyni ïa la ka jong ka riti dustur ha kiwei ruh. Shuh shuh ula ong ruh ba lyngba kane kan long kum ka khubor ban pyntip lem sha kiwei shaphang ki ar tylli ki bynta, kita ki long ka Jingnang jingstad, bad ka jingsumar ïa ka Mariang. Shuh shuh u la ong ruh ba kane ka sngi ba mynta ha kaba na ka liang ka Seng Khasi Nonglang ki la rakhe ïa kane ka Shad Suk Mynsiem ka dei kawei na ki kolshor bad ka riti ka dustur kaba ma ngi ka jaitbynriew u khun khasi ngi ju kynmaw naduh ki por ba jah kaba dei kawei na ki jingshad ba paw nam ym tang hapoh ka jylla hynrei wat ha Ri hi baroh kawei.

    Na ka liang u Bah Taiparlin Kharlyngdoh, President ka Seng Khasi South West Khasi Hills District ula pynkynmaw ba kane ka sngi 8 tarik mynta u bnai ka dei ka sngi kaba sah jingkynmaw namar ba dei ha kane hi ka sngi ba u Bah D.K. Dkhar, IAS, DC jong ka West Khasi Hills District, Nongstoiñ ha ka 8/04/2005 ula ïoh ban plie ïa ka ïing jong ka Seng Khasi Nonglang bad mynta ka 8/04/2017 na ka liang u Samla Kynpham Kharlyngdoh, Muktiar ka Supreme Court ula ïoh ban plie ïa ka Gallery jong ka Seng Khasi Nonglang ha kane hi ka juh ka madan.
Byrthen ki paidbah ka thaiñ Maweit ban ym ïashimbynta MLA Election 2018
10 April, 2017
Nongstoiñ, Iaiong 9: Ki paidbah nongshong shnong ka thaiñ Maweit baroh kawei, kiba la mad bad ïai mad ïa ka jingeh kaba khraw namar ka jinglong jingman jong ka surok, ki la byrthen ban ym ïashimbynta satia ha ka Election MLA ka ban long ha u 2018.

    Ki riew paidbah jong ka thaiñ ryngkat ki nongïalam jong ka seng HynñiewtrepAchik National Council, ki la pynpaw ba watla kam pat dei ka rai ba khatduh, hynrei lada ka sorkar Jylla ka shu sngap mynthi halor ka jingud jingnam jong ki paidbah, kim banse ban weng ïalade na ki Election ha ka Jylla.

    Kumban shu pynkynmaw ba ha u snem 2014 ba la pynlong ïa ka Election MDC, ki paidbah jong kane ka thaiñ ki la kyntait ban ïashimbynta ha ka Election bad don bun ki polling station kiba ka jingthep vote ka poi tang khyndiat ngut.

    Ka daw ka dei halor ka jingsngap mynthi bad jingkyntait jong ka sorkar ha ka liang ka roi ka par, khamtam eh ka surok kaba long u bud lum ka roi ka par jong ki paidbah ka thaiñ.

    U Bah Ricky Sohlang President jong ka seng HANC, u la pynkynmaw ïa ka sorkar ba lada ka shu sngap mynthi sah, na ka liang ka seng bad ki paidbah kin kyntait shisyndon ban ïashimbynta ha kino kino ki Election kiba long ha ka Jylla.

    Ka surok Maweit ka dei ka surok kaba la rim tam ha ka Jylla bad la sdang pyntrei ïa ka naduh ki snem 1963-64 ei ei ha ka por jong ka sorkar Assam. Hynrei haduh mynta kane ka surok ka dang sah kumjuh bad mynta ka aiom slap lei lei ka jinglong jingman jong ka, ka la nang sniew nang sniew.

    Kumban shu pynkynmaw biang hangne, ki sengbhalang jong ka thaiñ Maweit lem bad ka seng HANC seng kmie, ha ka jingïalang paidbah kaba la long ha u snem 2015, ki la shim rai ba lada ka sorkar jylla kam lah ban leh ei ei, ki paidbah kim banse ban bteng biang ban boycott ïa baroh ki Election ba kynthup ïa ka Election MP, MLA bad MDC.

    Ka seng HANC kan sa lum ruh ïa baroh ki para sengbhalang, ki sordar shnong, bad baroh ki paidbah ka thaiñ ban shim rai halor kane ka kam, kata ban kyntiew ïa ka surok Nongstoiñ-Maweit-Wahblei-Kulang-Nongjri kaba jngai kumba 37 kilometer. Dang ha u snem ba la dep, ki la phah ruh ïa ka memorandum sha ka sorkar pdeng ban kyntiew
Dawa ka AMSSASTA ïa ka NIOS ban pyn pas ïa ki nonghikai D.El.Ed
10 April, 2017
Shillong, ïaiong, 09: Ka All Meghalaya SSA School Teachers'Association (AMSSASTA) ka dawa na ka National Institute of Open Schooling (NIOS) ba ka dei ban pyn pass ïa kito ki nonghikai SSA kiba ïakhun ïa ka D.El.ed training jong u snem 2014-2015 hynrei kiba ka la leh thurmur ha kaba pynmih ïa ka result jong ki, kum ka jingbakla ha kaba kyntiew ïa ki marks ha kaba don na ki nonghikai kiba la shah thoh ‘absent’ ha ki sobjek kiba la ïaleh hynrei la kyntiew pat ha ki sobjek kiba khlem ïaleh, don pat na ki nonghikai kiba ïoh ïa ka Marksheet ha kaba khlem pyndap ei ei ha Internal Mark.

    “Namar tad haduh mynta ka NIOS kam pat lah ban pynbeit ïa ka jingbakla. Kane ka jingthurmur jong ki bor pynïaid jong ka NIOS ka ktah jur ïa ka kawei jong nonghikai skul. Ki nonghikai kiba ïakhun ïa ka eksamin ki la pyndep lut ïa ki jingdonkam baroh hynrei ki bor pynïaid eksam hi kiba thurmur, kumta ka dei hok ïa ki nonghikai ban pas,”ong u Bah L. Marngar, President ka AMSSASTA.

    Ha kaba ïadei bad kane ka AMSSASTA hapoh ka jingïalam u Bah L. Marngar, President ka Central Body ka la ïakynduh ïa u Director ka DERT ha 28 tarik, u bnai baladep ban dawa shimkhia kloi ïa kane ka kam.

    Ka AMSSASTA ka la dawa na ki bor badei peit ka NIOS ba ka dei ban pynbeit kloi bad ban pynmih noh shisyndon ïa ka result kaba beit, khnang ba kan ym buh jingeh ïa ki nonghikai.

    U Bah Marngar u ïathuh ba u Director ka DERTu la pyntip ba ka NIOS ka la shimkhia ïa kane ka kam bad kan pynmih noh shen ïa ka result kaba beit jong ki nonghikai kiba ïakhun ïa ka training D.El.Ed training 2014-15.

    Kane ka synjuk ki nonghikai SSA ka la pynkha ïa ka shnat treikam jong ka AMSSASTA Umden Unit na ka bynta ka jingshakri khambha ïa ki nonghikai SSA. Ki nongkitkam kane ka Unit ki kynthup ïa u President Bah Phrin Kleiñ, Vice President Bah B Ryntathiang, Secretary Kong Suzilian Khymdeit, Asst Secy Bah Bistokan Timung, Finance Secretary Kong Kyrmen Lapang. La pynskhem ïa ki nongkitkam da u Bah L. Marngar President ka Central Body.

    Ka seng ka kyrpad, lada don kino kino ki para nonghikai SSA kiba shem jingeh kin sngewbha ban ïakynduh ïa ki nongïalam kane ka Unit.
Ban jop ha Sohra, da u kyrtong monlang kwah ki Congress ha u 2018
10 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong 09 : Ki nongkyrshan ba radbah ka Congress ha Sohra ki la kyntu ïa ki bor bahalor jong ka party ba kadei ban sei da u kyrtong mon lang ha kane ka elekshon MLA na katei ka constituency khnang ban ïoh ïa ka jingjop ba donburom.

    Da kaba ïaroh ïa ka rukom treikam jong u president ka East Khasi Hills district congress committee, Bah Kennedy Khyriem kumba la paw ha ka jingïalang dang shen ha Shella Constituency, kitei ki nongïalam Congress ki la kyrpad ba dei ban leh kumjuh ha Sohra ruh.

    “Ban ïoh ïa ka jingjop ba donburom ha u 2018 ngi donkam da u kyrtong monlang uba ki paidbah ba dei bad bym dei Congress kin kyrshan,” ong kitei ki nongialam party bym kwah pynpaw kyrteng ha ka kyrwoh..

    Ki la pynpaw ruh ba ha Sohra hi haduh mynta ki paidbah ki dang don ka jingshaniah ha u Dr. PW Khongjee, u MLA Congress ba nyngkong eh ba ka Sohra ka ïoh (watla u rem noh ha u 2013), namar u don bha ka jingkyrmen ban jop ha kane ka kynti ruh.

    Kawei pat ka phang ba ki kdew ka long ba u Dr. Khongjee u dei u trai constituency nalor ba u dei ruh u briew uba baroh ki la don lypa ka jingshaniah ha ka rukom treikam.

    Ha kajuh ka por, ki la kyntu ruh ïa ki bor bahalor ka Congress ban pynkhlaiñ bad pynthymmai noh ïa ki nongkitkam jong ka Block Congress ha Sohra khnang ba kin ïoh ban sdang noh da ka rukom treikam kaba thymmai bad ban pynkhreh ha ka rukom kaba dei na ka bynta ka elekshon MLA kaban sa long shen.

    Lah ban kdew hangne, ba watla u Dr. Khongjee u la shah rem noh ha ka elekshon MLA 2013 hynrei ula trei borbah pat ban pynjop donburom ïa u kyrtong MDC Bah Donevan Wahlang.

    Kumba long haduh mynta hi, la ïoh jingtip ba utei u MDC ruh u thmu ban aireng lang bad ban ïa knieh tiket Congress bad u Dr. Khongjee.

    Dei nakata ka daw ba kitei ki paid Congress ki kwah ba ka party bahalor kadei ban rai beit ïa u kyrtong monlang kham kloi khnang ban ym mih ar kynhun ynd la dei ka elekshon.
Ba hap ïaid lyngba ki pipe um na surok kali, yn shimpor ban ïoh um na GSWSS - III
10 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong 09 : Ki jingeh kiba mih na ka jingpynïaid ïa ki pipe um kadei ka dawbah ba ka tnad Public Health Engineering (PHE) ka lah ban shimpor ban pyndep ïa ka jingpynpoi um lyngba ka Greater Shillong Water Supply Scheme (GSWSS) Phase-III.

    Haba pyntikna ïa katei, u Myntri ka tnad PHE, Bah Prestone Tynsong u la ong ba bun na ki pipe um ki hap ban ïaid lyngba ki surok kiba don ha ka nongbah bad kiwei kiwei.

    Katkum ka jingong jong u, ki don haduh 12 tylli ki jaka sam um (zone) ha kaba lai tylli la pyndep bad khyndai tylli kiwei pat ki dang sahkut shiteng kynthup ïa kito kiba ha ka thaiñ Mawlai. U Myntri u la ïathuh ruh ba la dep bthah ïa ki ophisar ha ki Division ba kin pan ka jingïatrei lang bad ka tnad Public Works Department (PWD) bad ruh ki Dorbar Shnong khnang ba ka kam kan ïaid stet.

    Da kaba pyntip ba ïa ka pisa kaba sah baroh kaba long 43 klur la dep ban ïohpdiang da ka tnad, u Myntri u la ïathuh ba ki don ka jingkyrmen ba ïa katei ka Phase - III jong ka GSWSS yn ïoh ban pyndep khlem da pynslem shuh.

    La ïathuh ruh ba namar ba ïa katei ka projek la bei tyngka da ka JNNURM, ka don ruh ka jingdaiñ kuna da ka sorkar pdeng namar ka jingbymlah jong ka jylla ban pynlong ïa ka elekshon Municipal ha ka jylla. Tang namar katei, la ong ba ka la don ka jingshah khate haduh 18 klur tyngka, bad ïa katei ka pisa hap ban buria ne pyndap da ka sorkar jyllla, u la ong.

    Halor ka jingkylli, u Myntri um shym la ai satia ïa ka por ne u bnai ban pyndep noh ïa katei ka projek khamtam haba ka por ba la buh thong ban pyndep kadei ha u Lber mynta u snem, ka la kut lypa.

    Lah ban kdew hangne ba ki don katto katne ki sengbhalang kiba la dawa ban pynlong da ka jingtohkti CBI halor ka jingsuba bamsap ha ka tnad PHE haba ïadei bad ka jingpyntrei ïa ki projek sam umbah ha ka jylla.

    Hynrei halor kane, u Myntri u la ong ba shen hi mynta u bnai un sa khot ïa ka jingïalang pyrkhat kam bad ki ophisar ban pan jingshai halor ki projek ba sahteng ha ka jylla hadien ba la shimti kum u Myntri thymmai katei ka tnad.

    Kumban shu pynkynmaw, ïa katei ka projek la buh thong ban pyndep ha u Jymmang 2011 ha ka jingmang ban pynlut 193.50 klur ha kaba ka bhah naka sorkar pdeng ka long 174.15 klur bad ka bhah na ka sorkar jylla pat ka long 19.35 klur. Ka la don ruh ka jingkyrmen ba lada lah ban pyndep noh ïa katei ka projek, yn sa lah ban pynduna ïa ka jingtyrkhong um ha ka jylla.
Ka “Sawdong Lyngwiar Dpei`ka lynti ban tem ia ki kam sniew
10 April, 2017
`Ka kam leh isynei, ka sdang shuwa na la rympei` ka dei shisha ka kyntien kaba shong sbai shong rupa bad kaba kit jingmut lada uwei-pa-uwei un puson ne pyrkhat ia kine ki kyntien.To ngin ia phai khyndiat shaphang ka imlang ka sahlang la ka long ha ka raid kihima ne ha ka jylla hi baroh kawei. Ka jingkylli ka mih hangne balei kein katba dang mih ki sngi bad ki snem la ïohi ba dang mih bun shuh shuh ki jaïid jingsni ew kiba ha rumkom ha ka imlang ka sahlang ne wat ha ki ing ki sem kabala buh jingma shisha ba ka bor jong ka jingsniew ka la trei borbah ha kine kisngi.

    Habangi phai sha ki Khubor ne ki Telivision bunsien ngim ju ïohsngew shuh ia kita ki sur kiba ai mynsiem ne kaba kren shaphang ka shongsuk shongsain ne shaphangka bha ka miat ha ka imlang ka sahlang, hynrei la ïohsngew bad ïohi sa tang ki kam lehdonbor, ki kam thombor, kam dih droks bad ki kam sniew kiba ha rukom. Hynrei ka jingkylli ka mih hangne, hato, man la uwei-u-wei ba la kot ia ki borsngewthuh ne ki bor pyrkhat,ki ju puson mo ba balei ki mih kine ki kamsniew kiba ha rukom ha ka imlang ka sahlang kaba la pyntad dor ia ka hok longbriew manbriew bad haduh ka akor ka burom kaba la hiar dor arsut kaba laïohi ba I kumba ain Blei ne ka aïin Briew kam don shuh.

    Naka por sha ka por, ki mih ki kam tuh ki kam thiem, ki kam pyniap, ki kam lute,ki kam leh beijot ne lehdon bor ia ki kynthei ki khynnah ha kaba kam don shuh kata ka jingshngain ha ka imlang ka sahlang khamtam ia ki kynthei ki khynnah.Khyndiat pat lah ban ong hangne ba man la uwei-pa uwei u la dei ban puson ialade shimet halor ka jingkynrei kine ki kam sniew kiba la ktah shisha ia kashongsuk shongsaïn ha ka imlang ka sahlang jong ka jylla. Yml ah ruh ban len bunsien haba ïohi ia ki kam sniew la ka long ha ki Kot Khuborne ki kor Telivision la ïoh sngew tang kata ka jingkren ia kyni hapdeng ki para briew bad ka jingkhnium kaba mih na ka shyntur kaba ki da sngew pangnud ba kynrei ki kamsniew. Ka jingkylli ka mih pat hangne. Hato, katno ngut kiba ju puson nepyrkhat na ei ka tynrai jong ka jingsniew ka wan bad balei ba ka jur ki kamsniew ha kine ki sngi?

    Sngew Sangsot ba ki briew ha kine ki sngi la ka long naduh ki khynnah, ki samla bad haduh ki tymmen ki san tang namar ka spah pyrthei bad ba ki ia beh ia kata ka ‘Rongphong Pyrthei” bad kim don por shuh ban puson ne ban pyrkhat halor ki tynrai ba ka jingsniew ka sdang ban mih. Hynrei ki la shuh ia beh ia kata ka spah pyrthei bad ki klet noh ban puson ne ban bishar ia ka tynrai ba ka jingsniew ka mih kaba la ktah shisha ia ka shongsuk shongsain ha ka imlang ka sahlang ha ka jylla bad ka ri.

    Kum ban shu ong, ka Jylla Meghalaya ka dei ka jylla kaba bun tam ki Kristan bad nai ia kren ia kata ka bynta, namar la ka long ka niam Kristan ne kino kino ki niam ba kynthup naduh ki Hindu, ki Muslim, ki Sikh bad kiwei kiwei ki jaïid niam ruh. Ka tynrai jong ka jingngeit bad ka jinghikaïi ka niam ka long hi shi bynta ban im hok im sot bad ban long kita ki ki jingthaw kiba don ia ki iktiar ban wan rah ia ka shongsuk shongsaïin ha ki ing ki sem ne ha ka imlang ka sahlang, Phewse!!!!! Da khongpong ha kine ki sngi ka jingsniew ka la shong kulai ha man la uwei-pa uwei u Briew kiba la klet noh ia la ka jong ka tynrai kiba la pyrshang ban beh ia ka Rongphong bad ki jingkwah brai kaba la pyntroin shisha ia ka hok LongbriewManbriew.

    Nai da iatai sani shaphang ki tynrai ba ka jingsniew ka mih, hynrei to ngin ia phai dien khyndiat ban puson kumba ong kine ka Kyntien, `Ka kam Leh isnei ne ka kam babha ka sdangn a la Rympei” khnang ba ngin sngewthuh ba balei ba kynrei ki kam sniew kam smeh ha kine ki sngi. Kum ba ban ktien,ha kine ki sngi kano kano ka longing longsem kim don por shuh ban hikai ia laki khun ki kti ha la rympei “ Sawdong ka Lyngwiar Dpei` namar ba ki la ia beh ia ki rongphong jong kane ka pyrthei bad kim don por shuh ruh ban shim ia la ka jingkitkhlieh ia ki khun ki kti ha kaba ki la ai mon khlem da tehlakam ha la ing la sem. Bad ym donkam hi ruh ban ia puson halor ki daw ba ki jingsniew ki la kynrei ha kine ki sngi, Ngi lah ban kren shai sha ka pyrthei, dei tang namar ba ki kmie ki kpa ne ki Longkni Longkpa ha kine ki sngi kim don por shuh ban sneng ne kyntu ia la ki khun ki Pyrsa ha la ing la sem bad ki khun ki kti ki la im laitlan katba ki mon ha kaba ki la sdang ban leh na I kam sniew I barit bad kan sa pur pat haduh baki jingsniew ki la kiew skong ha kine ki sngi.

    Kumba ong kaKyntien, I jingjaw um barit, ka pyndap ia ki phnieng ka Duriaw” ka la urlong shisha, namar tang na ka daw ba ki Kmie ki kpa ne ki Longkni ki Longkpa kimdon por shuh ban tehlakam ia ki khun ki kti ne ki Pyrsa ba ki la im laïitlan kala pynlong ruh ia ki ban kin dang shlur ban leh ia bun bah ki kam sniew kiba la ktah ha ka imlang ka sahlang. Namarkata, To nai ia wad shuh ia kiwei pat ki daw ne ki tynrai ba ka jingsniew ka mih, hynrei to kum ki Longing Longsem ne ki Kmie ki kpa ngin ia pyrshang ban hikai noh ia la ki khun ki Kti ha la ka jong ka Rympei, namar dei tang ha la Rympei lah biang ban sain dur ia ka hok long briew man briew ne ia ka akor ka burom kaba ngi lah ban iada na bun jaid ki kam sniew kam smeh ha ka imlang ka sahlang.

    Kano kano ka ing kaba don ia ka jingiatylli, ka jingiangewthuh jingmut bad kajingiaiet ba mar kylliang ka don kata ka jingtieng burom ban leh ia ki kam sneiw, hynrei lada kano kano ka ing kaba ia pait ia pra ym lah ruh ban len ba ki mih bun ki jingiapait ia pra ha kaba ki kam sniew ruh ki don hangta naba ymdon uta u ‘Shabuk’ kumba u Nonglur u pynkohnguh ia ki Masi ha ba ki lur ia ki lyngkha ban pyndep ia ka kam.
“BUROM KA RI KAN NEH TYRSEM, LA KA RITI HA KA SHAD SUK MYNSIEM”
(Païa B. Synrem)
10 April, 2017
“Shad ‘theisotti bad ’rangkynsai don-a-kor,
Ban khraw la ka nam, ban sah la ka burom;
Kan paw ha pyrthei – Riti, hok ba kordor,
Ka Shad Suk Mynsiem kan sakhi shijunom” .
(H. Tesslett Pariat - Ka Jingrwai Seng Khasi kaba 98)

    Ki khanatang, ki khanaNiam, ki parom, ki paju bad ki khana pateng ki ïathuh ïa ngi ba ka shad ka kmen tynrai jong u khun Khasi Khara ka la don naduh kulong kumah, naduh ki sngi bad ki por jong ka Tangnub Tangjri haduh ki por ba u Khasi u la seng it seng hima, seng raid seng muluk, seng shnong seng thawpateng la pateng. Kawei na ki daw kiba u Khasi u pynlong ïaka shad ka kmen ha la ki longshnong longthaw, longraid longmuluk, ki longit longhima ha kylleng ka Bri u Hynniewtrep ka long ban ainguh aidem ïa la U Blei Trai Kynrad Nongbuh Nongthaw halor ki jingkyrkhu ki jong U. Kane ka shad ka kmen ka don ryngkat ïa ki jingleh rukom kiba long ki bynta jong ka Niam.

    Haduh shiteng jong ka spah snem kaba khad khyndai, ka jinglong ba kyrpang jong ka jaidbynriew Khasi ka ïai neh khara ha la ka jinglong ba hara jong ka. Ka Niam ka rukom ryngkat bad ki riti ki dustur, ka shad ka kmen bad baroh kiei kiei kiba long ki tynrai jong ka jaidbynriew ki ïai long bad ïai neh kumba la seng nongrim da ki longshuwa manshuwa ïa kiba la da sawar bad matang thik-pa-thik. Hynrei ka ‘erlangthari jong ka jingsynshar nongwei jong kito ki por ka la sdang ban wan paswut ïa ki katto katne ki bynta jong ka pyrkhat khasi ba tynrai. Hapoh ki khyndiat phew snem jong kane ka jingwan lynshop kaba beh kyrthep, ka jaidbynriew ka la sakhi ïa ka jingsynjor jong ka pyrkhat nylla ha ki katto katne ki parakur ki parakha kaba la ktah ïa ki riti ki dustur khasi tynrai.Kumju ruh, ka shad ka kmen tynrai, kaba ju long ka shad ainguh aidem ïa la U Nongthaw U Nongbuh ha la ki it ki hima, ki raid ki muluk, ki shnong ki thaw ka la sdang ring swai ring sdot bad poi ruh haduh u pud ba kin duh kin dam noh ha ki katto katne ki bynta bad ki jaka jong ka Ri. Dei ha kum kane ka por kaba ka jaidbynriew ka ïakynduh ïa ka saw ka sian, ki Rangkynsai , ki Khrawpyrkhat jong ka jaidbynriew ki ïeng rangbah jwaiñ da ka jingkit khlieh ban seng ïa ka Seng Khasi ha u snem 1899. Ha ka kotkhubor “U Khasi Mynta” kaba la mih ha u Lber, 1900 ka thoh kumne; “La seng ïa ka Seng Khasi halor ka nongrim ban kyrsiew ïa ka jingmut ki para Khasi bad ban da ruh na ki jingïalam bakla…”. Ka Seng Khasi ka sngewdei ban don ruh ïa ka jingkitkhia haka ban pynneh pynsah, pynsan pynbha bad pynitynnad ïala ki riti ki dustur bad ban pynkhie im ha ka mynsiem bad ka jingmut jingpyrkhat ki khun Khasi ba kin ieit, kin burom, kin ñiewkor bad kin tip bha ïa ki. Dei halor kane ka jingshisha, ba ka Seng Khasi ka la shim ha lade ïa ka jingkit khlieh ban pynlong ïa ka shad ka kmen tynrai bad ka la ïoh ïa ka nam ka kyrteng da “KA SHAD SUK MYNSIEM.”

    Ïa kane ka Shad ka Kmen ba la sdang pynlong da ka Seng Khasi la sdang nyngkong ha ka kyntoit shnong Mawkhar ha ki snem kiba kham mynshuwa hadien ba la seng ïa ka Seng Khasi bad ha Lympung Weiking pat ka la sdang nyngkong eh ka 14 bad 15 tarik u Ïaiong, 1911. Ka Seng Khasi ka la nangheh nangïar, ki tnat Seng Khasi ki la nang ïa mih bad ïa roi ha kylleng ka Bri u Hynñiewtrep. Ha ka aiom Pyrem jong man la u snem, ki tnat Seng Khasi ha kylleng ka Bri U Hynñiewtrep, ki pynlong ïa la ki Shad Suk Mynsiem ha la ki jong ki shnong ki thaw ban pynpaw ïaka jingsngewnguh ïa la U Kynrad Nongthaw shisien shisnem ïa ka jingkyrkhu kaba U la thehsei bad ban buh ruh ïa ka kyrpad kyrpon ba Un dang theh sei kyrhai bad byllai ki jingkyrkhu ha ki snem bad ki por ban dang wan.

    Ha shuwa ban hiar sha Lympung Weiking, ha baroh ki lai sngi ba pynlong ïa ka Shad Suk Mynsiem, naduh ki por mynshuwa, ju pynlong ïa ka jingduwai kaba kyrpang ha ka phyllaw jong ka Ïingseng ïa kaba ki longtymmen longsan jong ka Seng Khasi ki da buh kyrpang ha ryngkat ka jingïadonlang ki ‘riew rangbah, ki longkmie,ki samla, ki khynnah, ki nongshad shynrang bad kynthei ha la ka riam shad tynrai bad ki nongput ki nongtem. Kane ka jingduwai ka don ha ka ïa ka jingmut kaba jylliew kaba phalang ïa ka pyrkhat Niam ba tynrai jong ngi u khun khasi khara. Haba baroh ki la ïaïeng ryntihlangkhrui, U Nongduwai uba long uwei na ki Rangbah jong ka Seng un sdang ïa ka jingduwai kumne:-

“A! Blei Trai Kynrad! U Nongthaw U Nongbuh, la ïa poi mynta, kumba la ïa buh, ban ïa mih ka shad ka kmen. Trai Kynrad! Da ka suk Mynsiem, ngi diangti ïa ka jingieit jingisynei jong phi baroh shi snem.Kumba ngi mut ngi thew ban leh ïa kaba bha, ban roi ka Ri da ba biang ha ka Niam ka Rukom, ka Hok ka Sot, ka Stad ka Nang, ka Spah ka Hajar, ka Nam ka Burom, ka Buit ka Akor. Katta keiñ Kynrad, ïa kane ka jingshad jingkmen jong ngi, kyrkhu hi Maphi, kyrdoh hi Maphi, ba kan bha kan miat, ba kan phuh kan phieng ha u nongshad u nongkmen, ha u nongput u nongtem, u khmih kai u khmih ïaid, shynrang - kynthei ba long u parakur parakha suda baroh. Ai Trai Kynrad ka koit ka nang ryngkat”

(Ynda la dep u sa nguh biang laisien bad ki paidbah ki sa ïa bud lang kumne)

“Kumba la ïabuh, ba la poi ka sngi ka ïa, ban ïa mih, ka shad ka kmen, da ka Suk Mynsiem baroh. Kumba ïa long ba ïa tip i Kur i Kha para khun Khasi Khara. Pyllun na khlieh ha kjat, na Mihngi sha Sepngi, ban ïa bud ïa ka riti. Mynta la ïapoi la ïalang, la ka khreh la ka khrum, baroh la ka riam ka beit shrak.

Para Khun Khasi-Khara, ba dang kheiñi Kur i Kha, katkum la ka Riti, ba ju ïa shongsuk shongsaiñ, ka buit te kawei ka bor te kawei, ban tang sah pyrto la ka Ri.

Katta la ïa ong, mynta ngin ïeng ryngkat kawei, la ka Wait, la u Symphiah ha ka Shad ka Kmen, ha ka Nam ka Burom, ban sah pyrto babha, ha u Briew ha U Blei kum kata pateng la ptaeng”

(Hadien kane, yn saïa kynhoi lang baroh lai sien lai wat)

HOI! HOI! HOI! KIW!, HOI! HOI! HOI! KIW!, HOI! HOI! HOI! KIW!.

Ryngkat bad ka jingkaweh jong ka Lama Seng Khasi, ki hiar sha Lympung.

    Ha ka sngi nohkjat, kata ha ka sngi nyngkong jong ka shad, ynda la poi ha Lympung ha shuwa ban kyntiew ïa ka Lama Seng, U ‘riewtymmen ‘riewsan, ha ryngkat u khaw eh u khaw shan, ka ‘lengspah ‘lenghajar, u klong u skaw bad ka um-ksiar um-rupa, sa shisien pat u ïeng ban ïa pan ïa ka pynsngew ka pynsngap, ka kyrpad ka kyrpon, ka kyrsan ka kyrbah sha u Nongbuh Nongthaw ba kane ka shad ka kmen kan long kaba phuh kaba phieng ha u nongshad nongkmen, u nongput u nongtem, ha u khmih kai u khmih ïaid. U da duwai ruh sha U Blei Trai Kynrad ba Un ai ka khiah krat khiah stang ïa baroh, ka bit ka biang ha ka khih ka kamai, ka khaïi ka pateng, ka thung ka tep, ka stad ka nang bad baroh kiei kiei ba kin long kiba bha kiba miat khnang ban shongsuk shong shngiañ ka Ri bad ka jaidbynriew ban roi ka Hok ha ryngkat ka buit ka akor, ban ïoh ka sngewthuh ka shemphang khnang ban lait na ka dum ka maswa, ka longbieit, ka longraiñ baroh.

    Ka Seng Khasi Kmie ka pynlong ïa ka Shad Suk Mynsiem kaba 106 mynta u snem ha ka 8, 9 bad 10 tarik u Ïaiong. Man la u snem, artaiew-lai taiew shuwa jong kane ka shad ka kmen, kata ha ka sngi Ïewduh jong ka taiew, ju don ka jingpynkiew ïa ka ksing, ka bom, ka tangmuri ha Ïingseng Khasi ha Mawkhar ban pynsawa ïa la ki parakur ki parakha ba ka Shad ka kmen ka la jan bad ba kan don ka jinghikai shad. Ha ka janmiet jong kane ka sngi Ïewduh, ju sdang da ka lehNiam leh rukom ha Ïingseng da ki tymmen ki san jong ka Seng ban pynsngew pynsngap sha U Blei ki Blei bad ba ki jingpynkhreh pynkhrum jong ka shad kin long kiba ïaid beit ïaid ryntih kum ba la thmu. Ki da duwai phirat ruh ha ka syiem jong ki sawpor saw samoi ba kin ai ïa ki sngi shad kiba shai bad kiba syaid. Ha kane ka snem ruh, ïa kane ka kam nguhblei demblei la pyndep da ka kynhun ki Tymmen ki San jong ka Seng Khasi Kmie ha ka jingdon lang jong ki dkhot ka Seng ha ka 21 tarik u Lber, 2017 (Sngi Ïewduh)

    Ka Shad Suk Mynsiem, namarkata, ka dei ka shad Niam kaba baroh u khun khasi khara uba bat uba snoh kyndong ïa la ka Niam ka Rukom u angnud bad ap khmih lynti ïa ka por ba kan wan khnang ba un lah ban mih lympung. Shisien shi snem ha ka por Pyrem, u khun khasi khara u mih lang khrui ban ainguh da ka shad ka kmen ïa la U Blei Trai Kynrad da ka jingïashim bynta ha ka Shad Suk Mynsiem. U da sei ki mardeng markieng, ka ksiar ka rupa, ki snap ki skor, ki khor ki khriam bad ki nara ki muka ban pyni katno U Kynrad Nongthaw U la theh sei ïa ka jingkyrkhu ha u. Namarkata ka daw, ha ngi ki khun Khasi ba bat ïa ka longNiam longrukom, ban ïohsngew ba don ba ong ba ka Shad Suk Mynsiem ka dei tang ka shad rong ka long ka jingpynsting dor ïa kane ka Shad Niam ïa kaba ngin ym lah ban pdiang. Ka long ruh kaba pyndiaw mynsiem bad pynnoh jingsngew ïa ki nongpynkhreh nongpyntaïar ïa kane ka Shad ainguh long-Blei kaba la sdang bad pynbeit thikna da ki longsan ka Seng Khasi naduh mynshuwa, kaba long ka Seng Trai –Ri kaba pynneh pynsah ïa ki riti ki dustur, lada suit da kiwei pat ki jingmut bym shonghok – bym shong tynrai paka nylla. Bynñiaw ruh ban ïohi ba kan don ka jingpyndonkam bakla ïa ki mardeng markieng, ki snap ki skor ha kiwei pat ki bynta ki bym ïadei bad ka shad ka kmen tynrai.

I Babu Spiton Kharakor ha ka dkhot kaba nyngkong ha ka Jingrwai Seng Khasi kaba. 74 kaba I la ai kyrteng “ Shad Suk Mynsiem ka Niam ba pura” I kynthoh kumne:

“Ko Khun Khasi to ïai im sngi nyngkong,
Shad Suk Mynsiem kaba dei la ka jong;
Long ka bynta jong ka Niam ka rukom,
Ïaroh u briew, kyrkhu U Blei na jrong”.

    Shuh shuh I Rangbah Belbin Kyndïah ha ka jingkren Seminar halor ka phang – “Ka Pyrkhat Niam ha ka shad ka kmen u Khasi” ba la pynlong da ka Seng Khasi Mawlai ha u 2007, I la thoh kumne, “ …. ha u Khasi, ka Niam bad ka shad ka kmen ka ïaid ryngkat ryngkat. Weng noh ïa ka Niam na ka shad ka kmen, ka shad ka kmen kam don jingmut shuh, ka long noh tang ka shad kai shad thamula”. Ha katei ka juh ka Seminar kaba la pynlong ha u snem 2007, I Kong Sweetymon Rynjah pat I thoh kumne, ha kaba ïadei bad ka bynta jong ka Niam ha ka Shad Suk Mynsiem, “Katba na la ka Niam pohïing pohsem jong ki longïing longsem ba bat la ka tynrai ki don la ki jingduwai kyrpang hala ki longïing longsem bad jingpynsleh umphniang ïa ki nongshad ba la pynkhreh shuwa ban hiar shad sha lympung ban ïoh ka koit ka khiah, ka roi ka spah, ka longhok ka longsian, ka sngewthuh ka shemphang, ka jingstad ka jingnang ban ïoh ka bor mynsiem, ka buit ka bor, ka buit ka akor, ban roi ha ka jingtip briew ban san ha ka tip Blei, kumta ka Shad Suk Mynsiem ka don ïa ka jingpyrkhat Niam kaba la ka jong kaba pynïasoh pynïadei beit sha la U Blei Nongbuh Nongthaw, Uba marwei”.

    Kawei pat kaba ka Shad Suk Mynsiem ka phalang lyngba ki nongshad shynrang-kynthei ka long ka jingri bad jingsyndongka jong ki ïa la ka burom ka akor kaba la pynlong bad pynlahïakine ki ‘khun ngeit hukum’ ban mih lympung. Ha kine ki sngi bad ki por kiba mynta kiba ka imlang sahlang jong ka jaidbynriew ka sakhi ïa ka jinghiar dor jong ka buit ka akor, ka jingïuhroit ïa ka hok longbriew manbriew bad ka jingthombor ïa ki rit ki ria, ki kynthei ki khynnah,to ngin ïa pusonïakaei kaba ka Shad Suk Mynsiem ka don ban syngkhong na ka bynta ka buromjong ka Ri, ban roi ka tip briew bad ban san ka tip Blei khnang ba baroh kiei kiei kiba bha kin ïai neh tyrsem.

Ha shuwa ban pynkut noh, to ngin ïapuson ruh ïa ka jingkynud jingrwai jong I kong Nelcyda Shabong (Bam kwai ha dwar U Blei) ha ka Jingrwai Seng Khasi kaba I la ai kyrteng “Shad Suk Mynsiem” kaba long kumne:

“Lada Shad Suk Mynsiem kam don shuh ha ngi,
Ha khmat ka pyrthei da ei pat ngin pyn-i,
Hangno shuh ka Niam, dustur bad riti,
Ba dei nongkynti tynrai khun khasi
Bthah ka SC ïa ki 11 ki Chief Justice jong ki HC ban thung hi ïa ki Public Prosecutors
Kynthup lang ïa ka High Court jong ka Meghalaya
9 April, 2017
Shillong, Iaiong 8: Ka ïing bishar ba hakhlieh duh jongka ri ka Supreme Court ka la bthah ne hukum ïa ki 11 ngut ki Chief Justice jong ki ïing bishar High Court ba kin thung hi ïa ki Public Prosecutor (PP) bad pynkylla ïa ki Special Court kum ki Exclusive Court kat kum ka POCSO Act 2012 khnang ban bishar kloi ïa kino kino ki case shah thombor ki khynnah khyllung. Kane ka hukum ka long halor ka mukotduma ba la ujor da u nongïasaid aiñ u Gaurav Kumar Bansal.

    Ha kane ka hukum ka ïing bishar High Court jongka jylla ruh ka la shah kynthup lang.Nalor ka Meghalaya kiwei pat ki jylla kiba u Bansal u kyntu ïa ka ïing bishar SC ban phah thung ïa ki PP ki long Gujarat, Himachal Pradesh, Punjab, Haryana, Tamil Nadu, Kerala, Maharashtra, Chhattisgarh, Mizoram, Nagaland, bad Union Territory Puducherry bad Andaman and Nicobar Islands.

    Ïa kane ka hukum ka ïing bishar SC ka la pynmih ha ka sngi Thohdieng ha kaba la bthah ïa ki 11 ngut ki Chief Justice jong ki High Court kiba don ha kitei ki jylla ba kin thung hi ma ki ïa ki PP ha ki Special Court kiban bishar ïa ki jingshah thombor bad leh beijot ne lehbor ki khynnah kat kum ka POCSO Act.

    Ka kynhun ki nongbishar kiba la bishar ia kane ka mukotduma ki kynthup ïa u Chief Justice Jagdish Singh Khehar, Justice D.Y Chandrachud bad Justice Sanjay Kishan Paul. Hadien ba la bishar bniah ïa katei ka mukotduma u Bansal ki sa pynmih ïa katei ka hukum.

    Haba wanrah ïa ka mukotduma u Bansal u la pynpaw ba kitei ki jylla ba la kdew haneng kim shym la thung satia ïa ki PP kaba long kat kum ka kyndon aiñ Section 32 jongka POCSO Act. U la ong “Ka jylla Gujarat, Goa, Madhya Pradesh, Maharashtra, West Bengal, Chhattisgarh, Arunachal Pradesh, Manipur, Meghalaya, Mizoram bad ki Union Territory ka Puducherry bad Andaman bad Nicobar Island ki la pynkheiñ ïa ka Section 28 jongka POCSO Act ba ki khlem thung ïa ki Special Court”.

    Ka Section 28 jongka POCSO Act ka kren shai ba ha man la ki district dei ban don beit kawei ka Special Court. Haba kdew sha ka National Commission for Protection of Child Rights, u Bansal u la pynpaw ha khmat ka ïing bishar ba ki don haduh 604 ki Special Court ha ki 675 tylli ki District bad kumba long mynta sa 71 tylli ki District ki bym pat don Special Court.

    U la ong “ Kane ka jingbym don ki Special Court, ka ktah ïa ka jingbishar namar ka la suki noh bad slem ban pynshitom ïa kito kiba donkti”.

    Haba phai sha ka jinglum jingkheiñ ka National Crime Record Bureau u Bansal u la ong ka jingbym don kitei ki Court bad ki PP ka la ktah jur ban pynshitom ïa kiba donkti kat kum ka POCSO Act nalor kata ki case ki la nang lang bad ka jingtohkit ruh ka suki noh.
Kurup ki BSF haduh 92 tylli ki masi na Nongskhen ba thmu khaïii sha Bangla
Kwah ïatreilang ki paid Khappud ban tehlakam
9 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong 08: Ki shipaïi Border Security Force (BSF) ryngkat ka jingïatreilang bad ki Pulit ka Jylla, hynnin ka sngi kila ïoh ban kurup haduh 92 tylli ki masi ba shongdor palat T.15 lak na ka khlaw ba don ha shnong Nongskhen, East Khasi Hills, kiba thmu ban shalan tuh sha Bangladesh.

    Ki shipaïi BSF kila ong ba ka jingkhaïi tuh ïa ki masi ha khappud Indïa-Bangladesh kala nang jur nang jur wat hapdeng ki jingpynpulom jong ki shipaï ïa kiba bun ki jingthmu. Ki ong ba ka jingjur ka jingdawa masi na Bangladesh ka dei ka daw bah ba jur ka jingkhaïi tuh ïa ki masi.

    Namar kane, ki shipaïi BSF kila kyntu ïa ki paidbah ba shongshnong ha khappud ka Ri ba kin aïi ka jingïatreilang bad ki shipai na ka bynta ban tehlakam ïa kane ka kam bymman.

    Ki shipaïi BSF ki ong ba hynnin ka sngi ki nongkhaïi tuh ïa ki masi kila buhrieh ïa ki masi hapoh kawei ka jaka khlaw ba don marjan ka khappud bad kila shu ap tang ïa ka kabu ban ïoh pynjam ïa ki masi sha shilliang pud bala ap lypa da ki nongkhaïi ba na Bangladesh.

    Kat kum ka jingong jong ki, ki BSF tang ha kane ka taiew bala leit noh kala ïoh ban kurup haduh 178 tylli ki masi bad ki mar ki mata ba shongdor palat ïa ka T.41 lak, kiba thmu ban khaïi tuh sha Bangladesh lyngba ki khappud ka Jylla Meghalaya.

    Ïa kine ki mar ba ïoh kurup la aïiti noh sha ki bor ka Custom ba kan pynlong ïa ka jingtohkit bad ban leh ïa kaba donkam.

9 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong, 08: Ki pulit ka East Khasi Hills, Shillong ka la maham bad kyntu jur ïa ki paidbah ba don jaka ba kim dei satïa dalei lei ruh em ban ngop ha kino kino ki briew kiba kam da kaba pynithuh ïalade ba ki dei ki nongtrei ka Mobile Company bad kiba kwah jaka ban pynieng ïa u Mobile Tower.

    U Bah Vivek Syiem, Superintendent of Police,(City), ha u kyrwoh ba la phah mynta ka sngi u la ïathuh ba ki pulit ka nongbah Shillong ki la ïoh ujor ba ki don katto katne ki briew kiba pyndik ïa ki riewpaidbah lyngba ka mobile phone da kaba kam ïalade ba ki dei ki nongtrei jong ka Reliance Communication ne jong kiwei kiwei pat ki Mobile Company.

    Une u heh pulit u la ïathuh ba kine kiba kam ïalade kum ki nongtrei Mobile Company ki la kam

ruh hadien ba ladep jurip dalade ïa ka jaka pynieng mobile tower ki la ïoh ïa u mobile number ban ïakren bad ki trai jaka bad pyntip ruh ba ka Kompani ka kwah beit ban ïakren markhmat bad ki trai jaka ban pynieng ïa u Mobile Tower hynrei ym bad kiwei pat.

    “Ha kaba nyngkong kin tohkit shwa la u/ka ki don jaka neem ban pynieng ïa u Mobile Tower bad hadien kane kin pan ïa ki dulir khyndew, kin pan ïa ka jaka sah bapura na ka bynta ban pynshisha lyngba u Satellite bad kiwei kiwei ki Dulir kum ka PAN Card bad kiwei kiwei,” ong une u Heh Pulit.

Kine kiba kam ïalade kum ki nongtrei Mobile Company ki pyndonka da ki SIM card na Kolkata.”

    Ki pulit hadien ba la ïoh ïa ka jingujor, ki la pynlong ka jingtohkit bad ka jingthwer mardor ban lap ïa ki runar ba donkti ha kine ki kam runar.

    Kaba thamula ka long ba une u Actor ka Bollywood u dang im bad u dang don hapdeng ka jingsumar hapoh ka Sir HN Reliance Foundation Hospital naduh ka 31 tarik u Lber namar ka jingtyrkhong um ka met (dehydration).

    Kane ka jingpynbna bakla kala wanrah ïa ka kynrum kynram kaba jur bha ha ka Party hynne ka sngi.

    U General Secretary ka BJP Meghalaya Bah David Kharsati ula pynbna ha ka jingïalang da kaba ong “Shuwa ba ngin sdang ïa ka jingïalang jong ngi mynta ka sngi, ngin pynlong ïa ka jingïasngap jar ba arminit kum ka jingburom ïa ka mynsiem bala duh noh jong u Vinod Khanna”.

    Ha kane ka jingïalang la ïadonlang ruh u Vice President ka BJP Sengkmie ba dei khmih ïa ka Jammu & Kashmir bad ka Rajasthan u Avinash Rai Khanna, uba la wan ban don arsngi ha Jylla na ka bynta ban pynkhlaiñ ïa ka BJP shuwa ba kan pynkhreh ïa ka elekshon MLA-2018 ha Jylla.

    U Vinod Khanna u dei u MP ka BJP jong ka 16th Lok Sabha ba mihkhmat napoh ka Gurdaspur Constituency.     Shuwa ïa kane, ka Ri baroh kawei kala khuslai bad phaikhmat bha sha ka jingshitom jong une u Actor hadien ka jingpur ki dur ki dar bala shon ïa une u Actor hapdeng ka jingshitom.

    Nalor kane, ka jingthoh jong u Amitabh Bachchan ha Twitter kala nang aiding ban pur ki khana khlieng tyngab ba u Vinod Khana ula ïap ha kaba ka BJP Meghalaya ruh kala ngop lang ha ki khubor hamsaia.

    Namar kane ka jingpynbna bakla, ka BJP hynne hi ka janmiet kala phah ïa ka kyrwoh ba pynshai halor kane ka jingjia hynrei wat hapdeng kane ka jingpynshai, kane ka Party kala ngat pat sa ha kawei ka jingjah burom kaba khraw lyngba ka jing bakla biang jong ka ba pynpaw ba u Vinod Khanna u dei u MP barim haba u dang dei u MP kat haduh mynta mynne.

    “Namar ka jingshah ïalam bakla ha ki Social Medïa ba u MP barim ka BJP u Vinod Khanna ula khlad, ka BJP Meghalaya ka kwah ban pynshai ba kat kum ki jingtip ba dang shu ïoh, une u MP ula nang ïohbor. Ngi kitbok ïa u ba un ïohnoh kloi ïa ka jingkoit bad ba un nang im slem” ong u Bah Kharsati ha ka kyrwoh.
Kiew ki jingshah leh be-ijot ki kynthei ha u snem 2016 ha Jylla
9 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong, 08: Ki kam runar ruser pyrshah ïa ki kynthei khynnah ha ka Jylla Meghalaya khamtam kiba ïadei bad ki kam shah leh be-ijot ki la nang kiew rasong, watla ki sengbhalang bapher bapher ba peit ïa ka bha ka miat ki kynthei ki la dawa na ka Sorkar MUA-II ba kan pynjari bad wanrah da ka aiñ kaba khlaiñ ka ban pynshyrkhei ïa ki nongleh kam sniew bad nongleh kam bymman.

    Katkum ka jingïohlum jingkheiñ na ka tnat Pulit, ki don haduh arphew lai tylli ki jingjia shah thombor ki kynthei khynnah ha ka Jylla tang nduh 1tarik Kyllalyngkot haduh 23 tarik, Rymphang, 2017.

    Kane ka jinglum jingkheiñ ki pulit, ha u snem 2016 ki jingjia shah leh be-ijot kaba hap hapoh ka kyndon Section 376 IPC ki long kumba 91 tylli ha kaba kynthup ïa kawei ka jingjia sha leh be-ijot ha ki bun ngut kaba la jia ha u Nohprah.

    Ka jingshah leh be-ijot ki khynnah kynthei ha u snem 2016 kaba hap hapoh ka kyndon section 376 IPC ka long baroh 25 tylli bad 112 tylli ki dei ki case ba la rejistar hapoh ka Protection of Children from Sexual Offences Act 2012 (POSCO).

    Ki kam runar ruser pyrshah ïa ki kynthei katkum ka jinglum jingkheiñ ki pulit ha u snem 2016 ha ka Meghalaya ka long hduh 293 tylli, katba ki kam runar pyrshah ïa ki kynthei ka long 218 tylli.

    Ki paidbah ka Jylla mynta ki don hapdeng ka jinglyngkhum jingmut namar ka jingkiew rasong ki kam runar ruser pyrshah ïa ki kynthei bad khynnah ha kylleng ki bynta jong ka jylla Meghalaya.

    U Mawphor haba pyrshang ban twad jimgut na ki riewpaidbah halor kane, uwei na ki rangbah bym kwah pynpaw kyrteng u la ong, “nga sngewjlep shisha tang shu khie naba thiah bad haba pule kotkhubor ngan ïohi ïa ki jingjia sha leh be-ijot. Kane ka pynngiah bha ïa nga bad ka pynbitar ruh ïa kito riewbymman ki bym don shuh ka mynsiem ïatiplem. Namarkata, ngi donkam ba ka sorkar jylla ka dei ban leh eiei ban pynduhjait ïa kine ki jingjia ba pynpohdor ïa ka imlang ka sahlang ha ka Jylla jong ngi.”

    Lah ban kdew mynta u snem 2017, tad haduh 23 tarik, Rymphang, katkum ka jinglum jingkheiñ ki pulit ki don lai tylli ki case ba kynthup ïa ka jingshah leh be-ijot ha ki kynhun runar ha East

Khasi Hills District, hynriew tylli ki jingshah leh be-ijot ha Ri-bhoi, san tylli ki jingjia ha West Khasi Hills, lai ha West Jaiñtia Hills, ar ha East Jaiñtia Hills, san tylli kynthup ïa ka jingjia shah leh beijot ha ka kynhun da ki khynnah ba dang hapoh 18 snem ka rta ha South West Khasi Hills District bad ar tylli ki jingjia ba kynthup ïa ka jingshah leh be-ijot ha ki runar ha North Garo Hills.

    Katkum ka jingïoh jingtip, ki don palat 600 tylli ki case ba dang sah pongding ha ki ingkashari bapher bapher ka Jylla Meghalaya bad ïa ka jingslem ban rai pynrem ïa ki nongkam bymman lehse kan long kawei na ki daw kaba nang pynkharoi shuh shuh ïa ki kam runar pyrshah ïa ki kynthei.

    Dang shen, ha ka 7 tarik u bnai baladep, ïa ka metïap jong kawei ka longkmie narud surok ha Itshyrwat, ha lynti ban leit sha hospital North Eastern Indira Ghandi Regional Institute of Health and Medical Sciences (NEIGRIHMS), Mawdiangdiang.
1.50 lak mang pisa u MLA ïa ka Nongmensong Dorbar Sec. School
9 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong, 08: Ka Nongmensong Dorbar Secondary School ha ka 5 tarik mynta u bnai ka la ïohpdiang ïa ka jingïarap pisa na ka longing longsem jong u Bah AL Hek, MLA ka Pynthorumkhrah Constituency kaba T.30 hajar bad kynthup ïa kawei ka Computer kaba u la ai sngewbha ha ka kyrteng i Meiieid jong u, i Kong Monica Hek.

    Ha kane ka sngi, u Bah Hek ula mang pisa ruh T.1.50 lak ban shna ïa ka kamra ai jinghikai Computer jong kane ka skul.Ïa kane ka skul la seng da ka Dorbar Shnong Nongmensong ha u snem 1998 bad mynta ka la don haduh Class IX bad Class X bad mynta u snem 2017 ka dei ka sien ba nyngkong ba phra ngut ki samla pule kane ka skul kin ap ban ïohkheit ïa u soh na ka eksamin SSLC ba dang shu dep shen.

    La seng ïa kane ka skul halor ka nongrim ban ai ka jingnang jingstad ïa ki khynnah pule ha kane ka thaiñ khlem da shim bai skul bad ïa ka tulop jong ki nonghikai la shim jingkitkhlieh hi da ka Dorbar Shnong. Hynrei ha ki snem kiba ladep ïa ka bynta jong ka Lower Primary bad Upper Primary la pynrung sha ka Sarba Shiksha Abhiyan (SSA).

    Na ka longing longsem jong u Bah AL Hek ki ju noh synniang sha kane ka skul kumba ki ju don ïa ka mynsiem ban noh synniang sha ki skul kiba pynïaid da ki Dorbar Shnong ym tang ha kane ka Constituency hynrei sha kiwei ki bynta kat kaba ki lah ban ïarap shisien shi snem.

    "Na ka liang ka skul ngi ai khublei ïa ka ing ka sem jong u Bah AL Hek kiba don ïa ka mynsiem ban noh jingïarap ïa ka skul ym tang mynta ka sien hynrei na ka por sha ka por bad naduh ba sdang ïa kane ka skul," ong ka Kong S. Kharsahnoh, Headmistress jong kane ka Skul.

    "Ka skul hi baroh kawei ka kitbok kitrwiang ïa u MLA bad ïa ka ing ka sem ba kin don ha met ba koit ba khiah ba kin nang lah ban nang ïaitrei na ka bynta ka miat jong ka imlang sahlang hi baroh kawei," la ong ka Kong Kharsahnoh.

    U Bah AL Hek u la ïathuh, naduh mynshwa hi ka ing ka sem jong u ka ju ïarap ïa ki skul kum shi bynta ban kyntiew ïa ka jingnang jingtip ha ka imlang sahlang khamtam ki skul kiba la seng da ki bor pynïaid shnong namar ma u ruh u pule ha ki skul shnong bad u sngewthuh ïa ka jingeh jong ki nongpynïaid bad nonghikai ruh kumjuh.

    "Man u snem na ka ing ka sem hi baroh kawei ngi ju ïarap lem katba lah ban ïa kyntiew ïa ka jingnang jingstad bad bsut lem ïa ka jingnang jingtip ha ki khynnah kiba wan na ki longing kiba kham duna ha ka ïoh ka kot. Ngi la noh synniang ïa kawei ka Computer, ka pisa bad na ka MLA scheme nga la mang pisa ban shna ïa ka kamra ai jinghikai Computer,” ong u Bah Hek.

    U ong shuh shuh, “ngi la leh ïa kane ka jingnoh synniang ha ka sien ba lai ïa kane ka skul bad nga khmihlynti ba ka skul kan nang kiew shaphrang katba nang mih ki sngi," ong une u MLA ryngkat ka jingkyntu ïa ki khynnah pule ba kin long kiba minot bad ruh ïa ki nonghikai ba kin ïatreilang khnang ban ïoh ïa ka jingjop ha ka jingim.
Sdang ka Shad Suk Mynsiem ba lai sngi ka Seng Khasi
9 April, 2017
Shillong, Ïaiong 8: Ka Shad Suk Mynsiem ka Seng Khasi, Kmie, Mawkhar, Shillong la sdang ïaka mynta ka sngi da ka jingwan ban iuh kjat da kiba bun ki thei sotti bad ki rang samla ba kynthup lang ia ki hep barit.

    Kumba la seng ïaka, ka jingsdang jong kane ka shad ka dei da ka jingtem ïa ka ksing lumpaid ha phyllaw jong ka Ïing Seng ha Mawkhar, hadien kane, la pynbud da ka jingdwai kaba la ai da u Rgh JSR Syiemlieh hadien kane, ki nongshad shynrang ryngkat ki duhalia bad ki paidbah, ki mih na ïing seng ban hiar sha lympung Weiking Jaïaw.

    Haba la poi ha lympung, shwa ban sdang ïa ka shad, ka la don shwa ka nguh ka dem kaba la pyndep ïaka da u Rgh Skor Jala ryngkat ka jingïasynran lang ki dkhot ka Komiti U Tymmen San bad sakhi lang da u President bad Secretary ka Seng Khasi, Kmie u Rgh Bantei S. Rumnong bad u Rgh Arwan S. Tariang ki dkhot jong ka JPK, ki nongïalam ka Seng Kynthei ka Seng Khasi, Kmie, lem bad ki dkhot ki jong ki, ki nongshad kynthei bad shynrang bad ki nongwan synran ïa ki nongshad bad ki paidbah.

Kat kum na ka khan ka shat na u Rgh Skor Jala, ka pynpaw ïa ki dak ki shin ba mynta ka kynti kane ka shad ka kmen kan long kaba bit ba biang ba ïaid beit ïaid ryntih, kaba U BLei Trai Kynrad u Nongbuh Nongthaw u la pdiang hun mynsiem ïa ka jingpynkhreh ïa kane ka shad ainguh aidem kaba juh long haki lai sngi.

     Hadien ba ladep ka nguh ka dem, ka la poi pat ka pali ban kyntiew ïa ka lama jong ka Seng Khasi, ba la kyntiew ïaka da u waheh N.R Shullai, ka Seiñ Raij Shillong, hynrei shwa ka jingkyntiew ïa ka lama, la ioh ïaka jingkren na u President u Rgh B.S Rumnong bad hadien kane la sdang pat ka jingshad.

    Naka bynta ki ar sngi kiban dang wan jong ka shad, ka Cultural Committee ka Seng Khasi Kmie ka kyntu ïa ki para riew seng bad ïa ki paid nongwan khmih shad bad ïa ki nongsynran ïa ki nongshad, ba kin ïa snoh kti lang da kaba bud ryntih ïa ki jingpynbeit ïa kane ka shad kampher lada dei ha kut ne shabar jong ka lympung.

     “Ka Cultural Committee ka kyrpad ïa phi ki para kur ki para kha, ki paid nongwan khmih shad ba sngewbha ban ïa bud ryntih ïa ki jingpynbeit kampher lada dei ha kut ne shabar jong ka lympung shad, khnang ba baroh ngin ïa ioh shisha ïa kata ka kyrkhu ba kyrdoh ba pura na U Blei Trai Kynrad”, pynpaw u Chairman bad Secretary ka Cultural Committee ka Seng Khasi, Kmie, u Rgh B.D Nongrum bad u Rgh Rangpher Rynjah.
